            if avg_vol_val > 0 and vol_at > avg_vol_val * 2.0
                sweep_type := 2  // Liquidity Grab (high volume)
            if rng > 0 and rng < nz(atr_val, rng) * 0.3
                sweep_type := 3  // Inducement (small move)
    sweep_type

// V273: Hidden rejection detection — 3+ consecutive candles rejecting from a level
f_detect_hidden_rejection(bool is_bull, int lookback) =>
    int reject_count = 0
    float ref_level = na
    int safe_lb = math.min(lookback, MAX_OFFSET - 2)
    for i = 0 to safe_lb - 1
        int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
        float body_hi = math.max(close[si], open[si])
        float body_lo = math.min(close[si], open[si])
        if is_bull
            if i == 0
                ref_level := low[si]
            if not na(ref_level) and math.abs(low[si] - ref_level) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.15
                if body_lo > ref_level
                    reject_count += 1
        else
            if i == 0
                ref_level := high[si]
            if not na(ref_level) and math.abs(high[si] - ref_level) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.15
                if body_hi < ref_level
                    reject_count += 1
    [reject_count >= 3, ref_level]

// V273: RSI divergence detection for RZ scoring
f_rsi_divergence_rz(bool is_bull, float rsi_now, float rsi_prev, float price_now, float price_prev) =>
    bool has_div = false
    float bonus = 0.0
    if not na(rsi_now) and not na(rsi_prev) and not na(price_now) and not na(price_prev)
        if is_bull
            if price_now < price_prev and rsi_now > rsi_prev
                has_div := true
                bonus := 15.0
        else
            if price_now > price_prev and rsi_now < rsi_prev
                has_div := true
                bonus := 15.0
    [has_div, bonus]

// V279-fix: Forward-declare globals used inside functions below
var int _regime_type = 0
float _hurst_val = f_hurst_exponent(100)

// V273: Confluence Score — checks alignment with key levels
f_calc_confluence_score(float zone_mid, float swing_h, float swing_l, float vwap, float prev_d_high, float prev_d_low, float prev_d_close) =>
    float confluence = 0.0
    float tol = nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.2
    if not na(swing_h) and not na(swing_l) and swing_h > swing_l
        float rng = swing_h - swing_l
        float fib_382 = swing_h - rng * 0.382
        float fib_500 = swing_h - rng * 0.5
        float fib_618 = swing_h - rng * 0.618
        float fib_786 = swing_h - rng * 0.786
        if math.abs(zone_mid - fib_382) < tol
            confluence += 5.0
        if math.abs(zone_mid - fib_500) < tol
            confluence += 5.0
        if math.abs(zone_mid - fib_618) < tol
            confluence += 5.0
        if math.abs(zone_mid - fib_786) < tol
            confluence += 5.0
    if not na(vwap) and math.abs(zone_mid - vwap) < tol
        confluence += 5.0
    float round_lvl = math.round(zone_mid / math.max(syminfo.mintick, 1e-8) / 1000.0) * 1000.0 * syminfo.mintick
    if math.abs(zone_mid - round_lvl) < tol
        confluence += 5.0
    if not na(prev_d_high) and math.abs(zone_mid - prev_d_high) < tol
        confluence += 5.0
    if not na(prev_d_low) and math.abs(zone_mid - prev_d_low) < tol
        confluence += 5.0
    if not na(prev_d_close) and math.abs(zone_mid - prev_d_close) < tol
        confluence += 5.0
    math.min(confluence, 30.0)

// V273: Volume Profile approximation — POC (Point of Control)
// V273: Volume Profile approximation — POC (Point of Control)
// 20 bins is optimal: balances precision with Pine Script computation limits (O(bins × lookback))
f_calc_poc(int lookback) =>
    int safe_lb = math.min(lookback, MAX_OFFSET)
    float h_max = ta.highest(high, safe_lb)
    float l_min = ta.lowest(low, safe_lb)
    float rng = h_max - l_min
    if rng <= 0
        (h_max + l_min) / 2.0
    else
        int NUM_BINS = 20
        float bin_size = rng / float(NUM_BINS)
        float max_vol = 0.0
        float poc_price = (h_max + l_min) / 2.0
        for b = 0 to NUM_BINS - 1
            float bin_lo = l_min + float(b) * bin_size
            float bin_hi = bin_lo + bin_size
            float bin_vol = 0.0
            for i = 0 to safe_lb - 1
                int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
                float mid = (high[si] + low[si]) / 2.0
                if mid >= bin_lo and mid < bin_hi
                    bin_vol += nz(volume[si], 0.0)
            if bin_vol > max_vol
                max_vol := bin_vol
                poc_price := (bin_lo + bin_hi) / 2.0
        poc_price


// V273: Absorption detection (high volume without price movement)
f_detect_absorption() =>
    float rng = high - low
    float avg_rng = ta.sma(rng, 20)
    float avg_vol = ta.sma(volume, 20)
    bool high_vol = volume > avg_vol * 2.0
    bool narrow_rng = avg_rng > 0 and rng < avg_rng * 0.5
    high_vol and narrow_rng

// V273: Keltner Channel squeeze detection
f_keltner_squeeze(int len) =>
    float basis = ta.sma(close, len)
    float kelt_atr = ta.atr(len) * 1.5
    float kelt_upper = basis + kelt_atr
    float kelt_lower = basis - kelt_atr
    float bb_basis = ta.sma(close, len)
    float bb_dev = ta.stdev(close, len) * 2.0
    float bb_upper = bb_basis + bb_dev
    float bb_lower = bb_basis - bb_dev
    bool squeeze = bb_upper < kelt_upper and bb_lower > kelt_lower
    squeeze

// V273: Volatility Contraction Pattern detection
f_detect_vcp() =>
    float rng1 = ta.highest(high, 10) - ta.lowest(low, 10)
    float rng2 = ta.highest(high, 20) - ta.lowest(low, 20)
    float rng3 = ta.highest(high, 40) - ta.lowest(low, 40)
    bool contracting = rng3 > 0 and rng2 > 0 and f_safe_div(rng1, rng2) < 0.7 and f_safe_div(rng2, rng3) < 0.8
    contracting

// V273: Judas Swing detection (false move at session open)
f_detect_judas_swing(bool is_session_start) =>
    bool result = false
    if is_session_start and bar_index > 2
        int o1 = f_clamp(1, MAX_OFFSET)
        int o2 = f_clamp(2, MAX_OFFSET)
        bool false_up = high > high[o1] and close < open and close < close[o1]
        bool false_dn = low < low[o1] and close > open and close > close[o1]
        result := false_up or false_dn
    result

// V279: Imbalance Zone detection — extreme buy/sell volume delta
// delta = Σ(volume × (2*(close-low)/(high-low) - 1)) over lookback window
f_detect_imbalance() =>
    float delta_sum = 0.0
    float delta_sq_sum = 0.0
    float curr_delta = 0.0
    int lb = math.min(inp_imb_lookback, MAX_OFFSET)
    // Calculate current delta window
    for i = 0 to math.max(lb - 1, 0)
        int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
        float rng = high[si] - low[si]
        float buying_pct = rng > 0 ? (2.0 * (close[si] - low[si]) / rng - 1.0) : 0.0
        curr_delta += nz(volume[si], 0.0) * buying_pct
    // Calculate longer-term stats for threshold (50 bars)
    for j = 0 to math.min(49, MAX_OFFSET)
        int sj = f_clamp(j, MAX_OFFSET)
        float rng_j = high[sj] - low[sj]
        float bp_j = rng_j > 0 ? (2.0 * (close[sj] - low[sj]) / rng_j - 1.0) : 0.0
        float d_j = nz(volume[sj], 0.0) * bp_j
        delta_sum += d_j
        delta_sq_sum += d_j * d_j
    float mean_d = delta_sum / 50.0
    float var_d = delta_sq_sum / 50.0 - mean_d * mean_d
    float std_d = math.sqrt(math.max(var_d, 0.0001))
    bool is_extreme = math.abs(curr_delta) > inp_imb_delta_threshold * std_d
    bool is_bullish_imb = curr_delta > 0 and is_extreme
    bool is_bearish_imb = curr_delta < 0 and is_extreme
    float imb_score = is_extreme ? math.min(100.0, 50.0 + math.abs(curr_delta) / std_d * 10.0) : 0.0
    [is_extreme, is_bullish_imb, imb_score, curr_delta]

// V279: Accumulation/Distribution Zone detection (Wyckoff)
// Trading range: price within narrow band for > min_bars with range < max_atr
f_detect_accumulation_distribution() =>
    float range_h = ta.highest(high, inp_acc_min_bars)
    float range_l = ta.lowest(low, inp_acc_min_bars)
    float range_width = range_h - range_l
    float curr_atr = nz(atr_val, 1.0)
    bool is_range = range_width < inp_acc_range_atr * curr_atr and range_width > 0
    // Classify: accumulation (CVD positive trend + decreasing ATR) vs distribution
    float atr_now  = ta.atr(10)
    float atr_prev = nz(ta.atr(10)[inp_acc_min_bars], atr_now)
    bool atr_declining = atr_now < atr_prev * 0.9
    // CVD trend estimate: sum of buying pressure over window
    float cvd_sum = 0.0
    for i = 0 to math.min(inp_acc_min_bars - 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
        float rng_i = high[si] - low[si]
        cvd_sum += rng_i > 0 ? nz(volume[si], 0.0) * (2.0 * (close[si] - low[si]) / rng_i - 1.0) : 0.0
    bool is_accumulation = is_range and atr_declining and cvd_sum > 0
    bool is_distribution = is_range and atr_declining and cvd_sum < 0
    float acc_score = is_range ? math.min(100.0, 40.0 + math.abs(cvd_sum) / math.max(ta.sma(volume, 20), 1.0) * 20.0) : 0.0
    [is_range, is_accumulation, is_distribution, range_h, range_l, acc_score]

// V279: VCP as standalone zone type (not just bonus)
// Series of contracting ranges with declining volume
f_detect_vcp_zone() =>
    float rng1 = ta.highest(high, 10) - ta.lowest(low, 10)
    float rng2 = ta.highest(high, 20) - ta.lowest(low, 20)
    float rng3 = ta.highest(high, 40) - ta.lowest(low, 40)
    bool contracting = rng3 > 0 and rng2 > 0 and f_safe_div(rng1, rng2) < 0.7 and f_safe_div(rng2, rng3) < 0.8
    // Volume decline confirmation
    float vol_now  = ta.sma(volume, 10)
    float vol_prev = nz(ta.sma(volume, 10)[20], vol_now)
    bool vol_declining = vol_now < vol_prev * 0.8
    bool squeeze = f_keltner_squeeze(20)
    // Score = f(compression_ratio, volume_decline, keltner_squeeze)
    float compression = rng2 > 0 ? 1.0 - f_safe_div(rng1, rng2) : 0.0
    float vcp_score = 0.0
    if contracting
        vcp_score := 40.0 + compression * 30.0
        if vol_declining
            vcp_score += 15.0
        if squeeze
            vcp_score += 15.0
    vcp_score := math.min(vcp_score, 120.0)
    float vcp_h = ta.highest(high, 10)
    float vcp_l = ta.lowest(low, 10)
    [contracting, vcp_score, vcp_h, vcp_l, squeeze]

// V279: Multi-bar rejection detection
// Multiple consecutive candles rejecting from same level
f_detect_multi_bar_rejection(bool is_bull, int lookback) =>
    float _mbr_lowest  = ta.lowest(low, lookback)
    float _mbr_highest = ta.highest(high, lookback)
    float ref_level = is_bull ? _mbr_lowest : _mbr_highest
    float curr_atr = nz(atr_val, 1.0)
    float tol = curr_atr * 0.15
    int rej_count = 0
    float total_wick = 0.0
    for i = 0 to math.min(lookback - 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
        float rng = high[si] - low[si]
        if rng > 0
            if is_bull
                float lower_wick = math.min(open[si], close[si]) - low[si]
                if math.abs(low[si] - ref_level) < tol and lower_wick > rng * 0.3
                    rej_count += 1
                    total_wick += lower_wick
            else
                float upper_wick = high[si] - math.max(open[si], close[si])
                if math.abs(high[si] - ref_level) < tol and upper_wick > rng * 0.3
                    rej_count += 1
                    total_wick += upper_wick
    bool valid = rej_count >= inp_multi_rej_min
    float mbr_score = valid ? math.min(100.0, 30.0 + float(rej_count) * 10.0 + total_wick / curr_atr * 5.0) : 0.0
    [valid, rej_count, mbr_score, ref_level]

// V279: Enhanced neural network (2 hidden layers: 9→8→4→1) for score prediction
// 9 inputs: z_score, volume, trend, sweep, efficiency, pa_patterns, regime, session, hurst
// L2 regularization + adaptive learning rate
var array<float> _nn_w1 = array.new<float>(72, 0.1)   // 9×8 = 72 weights (input→hidden1)
var array<float> _nn_w2 = array.new<float>(32, 0.15)   // 8×4 = 32 weights (hidden1→hidden2)
var array<float> _nn_w3 = array.new<float>(4, 0.25)    // 4×1 = 4 weights (hidden2→output)
var array<float> _nn_bias1 = array.new<float>(8, 0.0)
var array<float> _nn_bias2 = array.new<float>(4, 0.0)
var array<float> _nn_bias3 = array.from(0.0)
var array<int> _nn_update_count = array.from(0)
float _nn_lambda = 0.001  // L2 regularization coefficient

f_nn_sigmoid(float x) =>
    1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-math.max(-10.0, math.min(10.0, x))))

f_nn_predict(float z_in, float vol_in, float trend_in, float sweep_in, float eff_in, float pa_in) =>
    // V279: Use 9 inputs; extra 3 (regime, session, hurst) derived from globals
    float regime_in = nz(float(_regime_type), 0.0) / 3.0  // normalize 0-3 → 0-1
    float session_in = in_brokezone ? 1.0 : 0.0
    float hurst_in = nz(_hurst_val, 0.5)
    array<float> inputs = array.from(z_in, vol_in, trend_in, sweep_in, eff_in, pa_in, regime_in, session_in, hurst_in)
    // Hidden layer 1 (8 neurons)
    array<float> hidden1 = array.new<float>(8, 0.0)
    for h = 0 to 7
        float sum = array.get(_nn_bias1, h)
        for inp = 0 to 8
            sum += array.get(inputs, inp) * array.get(_nn_w1, h * 9 + inp)
        array.set(hidden1, h, f_nn_sigmoid(sum))
    // Hidden layer 2 (4 neurons)
    array<float> hidden2 = array.new<float>(4, 0.0)
    for h = 0 to 3
        float sum = array.get(_nn_bias2, h)
        for h1 = 0 to 7
            sum += array.get(hidden1, h1) * array.get(_nn_w2, h * 8 + h1)
        array.set(hidden2, h, f_nn_sigmoid(sum))
    // Output layer
    float output = array.get(_nn_bias3, 0)
    for h = 0 to 3
        output += array.get(hidden2, h) * array.get(_nn_w3, h)
    f_nn_sigmoid(output) * 150.0

f_nn_update(float z_in, float vol_in, float trend_in, float sweep_in, float eff_in, float pa_in, float target, float lr) =>
    // V279: Adaptive learning rate — decreases over time for stability
    array.set(_nn_update_count, 0, array.get(_nn_update_count, 0) + 1)
    float adaptive_lr = lr * (1.0 / (1.0 + 0.001 * float(array.get(_nn_update_count, 0))))
    float pred = f_nn_predict(z_in, vol_in, trend_in, sweep_in, eff_in, pa_in)
    float err = (target / 150.0) - (pred / 150.0)
    float regime_in = nz(float(_regime_type), 0.0) / 3.0
    float session_in = in_brokezone ? 1.0 : 0.0
    float hurst_in = nz(_hurst_val, 0.5)
    array<float> inputs = array.from(z_in, vol_in, trend_in, sweep_in, eff_in, pa_in, regime_in, session_in, hurst_in)
    // Forward pass — hidden layer 1
    array<float> hidden1 = array.new<float>(8, 0.0)
    for h = 0 to 7
        float sum = array.get(_nn_bias1, h)
        for inp = 0 to 8
            sum += array.get(inputs, inp) * array.get(_nn_w1, h * 9 + inp)
        array.set(hidden1, h, f_nn_sigmoid(sum))
    // Forward pass — hidden layer 2
    array<float> hidden2 = array.new<float>(4, 0.0)
    for h = 0 to 3
        float sum = array.get(_nn_bias2, h)
        for h1 = 0 to 7
            sum += array.get(hidden1, h1) * array.get(_nn_w2, h * 8 + h1)
        array.set(hidden2, h, f_nn_sigmoid(sum))
    // Backprop: output → hidden2
    float d_out = err
    for h = 0 to 3
        float h2v = array.get(hidden2, h)
        float w3_old = array.get(_nn_w3, h)
        // L2 regularization: weight update with decay
        array.set(_nn_w3, h, w3_old * (1.0 - adaptive_lr * _nn_lambda) + adaptive_lr * d_out * h2v)
        // Backprop: hidden2 → hidden1
        float d_h2 = d_out * w3_old * h2v * (1.0 - h2v)
        for h1 = 0 to 7
            int w2_idx = h * 8 + h1
            float w2_old = array.get(_nn_w2, w2_idx)
            float h1v = array.get(hidden1, h1)
            array.set(_nn_w2, w2_idx, w2_old * (1.0 - adaptive_lr * _nn_lambda) + adaptive_lr * d_h2 * h1v)
            // Backprop: hidden1 → input
            float d_h1 = d_h2 * w2_old * h1v * (1.0 - h1v)
            for inp = 0 to 8
                int w1_idx = h1 * 9 + inp
                float w1_old = array.get(_nn_w1, w1_idx)
                array.set(_nn_w1, w1_idx, w1_old * (1.0 - adaptive_lr * _nn_lambda) + adaptive_lr * d_h1 * array.get(inputs, inp))
            array.set(_nn_bias1, h1, array.get(_nn_bias1, h1) + adaptive_lr * d_h1)
        array.set(_nn_bias2, h, array.get(_nn_bias2, h) + adaptive_lr * d_h2)
    array.set(_nn_bias3, 0, array.get(_nn_bias3, 0) + adaptive_lr * d_out)

// V279: Adaptive scoring weights (9 components, recalculated every N trades)
var array<float> _adapt_weights = array.from(0.20, 0.12, 0.12, 0.12, 0.10, 0.10, 0.10, 0.07, 0.07)
var array<float> _comp_win_sums = array.new<float>(9, 0.0)
var array<float> _comp_loss_sums = array.new<float>(9, 0.0)
var array<int> _adapt_trade_count = array.from(0)
var array<int> _adapt_last_update = array.from(0)

f_update_adaptive_weights(bool is_win, float z_comp, float vol_comp, float trend_comp, float sweep_comp, float eff_comp, float pa_comp) =>
    // V279: Add regime/session/hurst components
    float regime_comp = nz(float(_regime_type), 0.0) / 3.0
    float session_comp = in_brokezone ? 1.0 : 0.0
    float hurst_comp = nz(_hurst_val, 0.5)
    array<float> comps = array.from(z_comp, vol_comp, trend_comp, sweep_comp, eff_comp, pa_comp, regime_comp, session_comp, hurst_comp)
    for i = 0 to 8
        if is_win
            array.set(_comp_win_sums, i, array.get(_comp_win_sums, i) + array.get(comps, i))
        else
            array.set(_comp_loss_sums, i, array.get(_comp_loss_sums, i) + array.get(comps, i))
    array.set(_adapt_trade_count, 0, array.get(_adapt_trade_count, 0) + 1)
    if array.get(_adapt_trade_count, 0) - array.get(_adapt_last_update, 0) >= 20
        array.set(_adapt_last_update, 0, array.get(_adapt_trade_count, 0))
        float total_diff = 0.0
        array<float> diffs = array.new<float>(9, 0.0)
        for i = 0 to 8
            // 0.5 loss weight: penalise losing components less aggressively; 0.01 floor prevents zero-weight collapse
            float diff = math.max(0.01, array.get(_comp_win_sums, i) - array.get(_comp_loss_sums, i) * 0.5)
            array.set(diffs, i, diff)
            total_diff += diff
        if total_diff > 0
            for i = 0 to 8
                array.set(_adapt_weights, i, f_safe_div(array.get(diffs, i), total_diff))

// ==========================================
// БЛОК 6: SCORING ENGINE (V249: БЕЗОПАСНЫЕ ОБРАЩЕНИЯ К ИСТОРИИ)
// ==========================================
var float last_sh   = na
var float last_sl   = na
var int   last_sh_i = na
var int   last_sl_i = na

if not na(ph_int)
    last_sh   := struct_h
    last_sh_i := struct_h_i
if not na(pl_int)
    last_sl   := struct_l
    last_sl_i := struct_l_i

// V270: BOS/CHoCH Structural Analysis
var float prev_swing_high = na
var float prev_swing_low  = na
var int   prev_sh_i       = na
var int   prev_sl_i       = na
var bool  bos_bull        = false
var bool  bos_bear        = false
var bool  choch_bull      = false
var bool  choch_bear      = false
var int last_bos_was_bull = na  // na, 0 (false), 1 (true)
var float premium_discount_mid = na

// Track previous swing points for BOS detection
if not na(ph_int) and not na(last_sh)
    prev_swing_high := last_sh
    prev_sh_i       := last_sh_i
if not na(pl_int) and not na(last_sl)
    prev_swing_low  := last_sl
    prev_sl_i       := last_sl_i

// BOS: close breaks previous swing high/low
// V274-fix: removed barstate.isconfirmed to allow real-time BOS/CHoCH detection
// (exit hints in VISUAL depend on these signals via ENG: Struct Combo channel)
bos_bull := not na(prev_swing_high) and close > prev_swing_high
bos_bear := not na(prev_swing_low) and close < prev_swing_low

// CHoCH: first reverse BOS after a trend
if bos_bull and (na(last_bos_was_bull) or last_bos_was_bull == 0)
    choch_bull := true
    choch_bear := false
else
    choch_bull := false

if bos_bear and (na(last_bos_was_bull) or last_bos_was_bull == 1)
    choch_bear := true
    choch_bull := false
else if not bos_bear
    choch_bear := false

if bos_bull
    last_bos_was_bull := 1

if bos_bear
    last_bos_was_bull := 0

// Premium/Discount zones (Fibonacci 0.5 from current swing)
if not na(last_sh) and not na(last_sl)
    premium_discount_mid := (last_sh + last_sl) / 2.0

// V270: BOS score bonus for zones
float bos_zone_bonus = bos_bull ? 20.0 : bos_bear ? 20.0 : 0.0
float choch_zone_bonus = choch_bull ? 15.0 : choch_bear ? 15.0 : 0.0

// V270: Equal Highs/Lows Detection (Liquidity Pools)
var float eq_high_level = na
var float eq_low_level  = na
var bool  has_eq_highs  = false
var bool  has_eq_lows   = false

if not na(atr_val) and atr_val > 0
    eq_tol := atr_val * 0.1
    // Check last 3 swing highs for equal levels
    int eq_h_count = 0
    float eq_h_ref = nz(last_sh, high)
    if not na(prev_swing_high) and math.abs(prev_swing_high - eq_h_ref) <= eq_tol
        eq_h_count += 1
    has_eq_highs := eq_h_count >= 1
    eq_high_level := has_eq_highs ? eq_h_ref : na
    // Check last 3 swing lows for equal levels
    int eq_l_count = 0
    float eq_l_ref = nz(last_sl, low)
    if not na(prev_swing_low) and math.abs(prev_swing_low - eq_l_ref) <= eq_tol
        eq_l_count += 1
    has_eq_lows := eq_l_count >= 1
    eq_low_level := has_eq_lows ? eq_l_ref : na

// ── V249: ВСЕ функции с series[offset] используют f_clamp() ──────────────

f_calc_fvg_on_candle(int impulse_idx, bool is_bull, float current_atr) =>
    float gap_size = 0.0
    float t        = na
    float b        = na
    string g_type  = "None"

    int offset_now = bar_index - impulse_idx
    // V249: жёсткий clamp — нужны [offset+1], поэтому потолок = MAX_OFFSET_2
    bool offset_safe = offset_now >= 1 and offset_now <= MAX_OFFSET_2

    if offset_safe
        float atr_dampened = math.max(current_atr, syminfo.mintick)
        int o1 = f_clamp(offset_now + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        int o0 = f_clamp(offset_now, MAX_OFFSET)
        int om = f_clamp(math.max(offset_now - 1, 0), MAX_OFFSET)
        float c1_h = high[o1]
        float c1_l = low[o1]
        float c1_c = close[o1]
        float c1_o = open[o1]
        float c2_h = high[o0]
        float c2_l = low[o0]
        float c2_c = close[o0]
        float c2_o = open[o0]
        float c3_h = high[om]
        float c3_l = low[om]
        float c3_c = close[om]
        float c3_o = open[om]
        float tol  = syminfo.mintick * 0.5

        if is_bull
            if c3_l >= (c1_h + tol)
                gap_size := (c3_l - c1_h) / atr_dampened
                t := c3_l
                b := c1_h
                g_type := "Classic FVG"
            else if c2_o >= (c1_c + tol) and c2_l > c1_c
                gap_size := (c2_o - c1_c) / atr_dampened
                t := c2_o
                b := c1_c
                g_type := "Vol Imbalance"
            else if c3_o >= (c2_c + tol) and c3_l > c2_c
                gap_size := (c3_o - c2_c) / atr_dampened
                t := c3_o
                b := c2_c
                g_type := "Vol Imbalance"
            else if c3_l >= (c1_h + tol) and (c2_o <= c2_l + atr_dampened * 0.1) and (c2_c >= c2_h - atr_dampened * 0.1)
                gap_size := (c3_l - c1_h) / atr_dampened
                t := c3_l
                b := c1_h
                g_type := "Marubozu"
            else if c2_o >= (c1_o + tol) and c2_l > c1_h
                gap_size := (c2_o - c1_o) / atr_dampened
                t := c2_o
                b := c1_o
                g_type := "Open-Open Imb"
        else
            if c1_l >= (c3_h + tol)
                gap_size := (c1_l - c3_h) / atr_dampened
                t := c1_l
                b := c3_h
                g_type := "Classic FVG"
            else if c1_c >= (c2_o + tol) and c2_h < c1_c
                gap_size := (c1_c - c2_o) / atr_dampened
                t := c1_c
                b := c2_o
                g_type := "Vol Imbalance"
            else if c2_c >= (c3_o + tol) and c3_h < c2_c
                gap_size := (c2_c - c3_o) / atr_dampened
                t := c2_c
                b := c3_o
                g_type := "Vol Imbalance"
            else if c1_l >= (c3_h + tol) and (c2_o >= c2_h - atr_dampened * 0.1) and (c2_c <= c2_l + atr_dampened * 0.1)
                gap_size := (c1_l - c3_h) / atr_dampened
                t := c1_l
                b := c3_h
                g_type := "Marubozu"
            else if c1_o >= (c2_o + tol) and c2_h < c1_l
                gap_size := (c1_o - c2_o) / atr_dampened
                t := c1_o
                b := c2_o
                g_type := "Open-Open Imb"
    [gap_size, t, b, g_type]

// V273: Balanced Price Range (BPR) — overlapping bullish and bearish FVG
// Inverse FVG check — FVG in opposite direction from zone = counter-signal
// Returns: [has_bpr, bpr_top, bpr_bot, has_inverse_fvg]
f_check_bpr_and_inverse(int impulse_idx, bool is_bull, float current_atr) =>
    [bull_sz, bull_t, bull_b, bull_type] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(impulse_idx, true, current_atr)
    [bear_sz, bear_t, bear_b, bear_type] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(impulse_idx, false, current_atr)
    bool has_bpr = false
    float bpr_top = na
    float bpr_bot = na
    bool has_inverse = false
    // BPR: both directions have FVG and they overlap
    if bull_sz > 0 and bear_sz > 0
        float ov_top = math.min(bull_t, bear_t)
        float ov_bot = math.max(bull_b, bear_b)
        if ov_top > ov_bot
            has_bpr := true
            bpr_top := ov_top
            bpr_bot := ov_bot
    // Inverse FVG: FVG in opposite direction
    if is_bull and bear_sz > 0
        has_inverse := true
    else if not is_bull and bull_sz > 0
        has_inverse := true
    [has_bpr, bpr_top, bpr_bot, has_inverse]

// V273: Stacked FVG bonus — multiple FVGs in same direction within 3 bars
f_check_stacked_fvg(int start_idx, bool is_bull, float current_atr) =>
    int fvg_count = 0
    for i = 0 to 2
        int check_idx = start_idx + i
        if check_idx <= bar_index
            [sz, _t, _b, _type] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(check_idx, is_bull, current_atr)
            if sz > 0
                fvg_count += 1
    float bonus = fvg_count >= 2 ? 15.0 : 0.0
    bonus

f_check_sweep(int pivot_idx, bool check_bull) =>
    bool swept     = false
    int  off       = bar_index - pivot_idx
    // V249: clamp
    if off >= 0 and off <= MAX_OFFSET
        float total_range = high[off] - low[off]
        if total_range > 0
            if check_bull
                float wick_bot = math.min(close[off], open[off]) - low[off]
                swept := (wick_bot > total_range * inp_sweep_ratio)
            else
                float wick_top = high[off] - math.max(close[off], open[off])
                swept := (wick_top > total_range * inp_sweep_ratio)
    swept

f_verify_structural_sweep(int current_idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool is_sweep    = false
    int  off         = bar_index - current_idx
    // V249: нужны [prev_off + 1], поэтому потолок = MAX_OFFSET_3
    if off >= 0 and off <= MAX_OFFSET_3
        float curr_l = low[off]
        float curr_h = high[off]
        float curr_c = close[off]
        for i = 1 to p_sfp_lookback
            int prev_off = off + i
            if prev_off > MAX_OFFSET_2
                break
            if is_bull
                if low[prev_off] < low[f_clamp(prev_off + 1, MAX_OFFSET)] and low[prev_off] < low[f_clamp(math.max(prev_off - 1, 0), MAX_OFFSET)]
                    if curr_l < low[prev_off] and curr_c > low[prev_off]
                        is_sweep := true
                        break
            else
                if high[prev_off] > high[f_clamp(prev_off + 1, MAX_OFFSET)] and high[prev_off] > high[f_clamp(math.max(prev_off - 1, 0), MAX_OFFSET)]
                    if curr_h > high[prev_off] and curr_c < high[prev_off]
                        is_sweep := true
                        break
    is_sweep

f_is_engulfing(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    // V249: нужен [offset + 1]
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET_2
        float c = close[offset]
        float o = open[offset]
        int prev_off = f_clamp(offset + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        float c_prev = close[prev_off]
        float o_prev = open[prev_off]
        if is_bull
            if c > o and c_prev < o_prev
                if c > o_prev and o < c_prev
                    res := true
        else
            if c < o and c_prev > o_prev
                if c < o_prev and o > c_prev
                    res := true
    res

// ── V255: PPR (Pivot Point Reversal) — разворотный паттерн ────────────────
// Bull PPR: предыдущая свеча медвежья, текущая закрывается выше high предыдущей
// Bear PPR: предыдущая свеча бычья, текущая закрывается ниже low предыдущей
f_is_ppr(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET_2
        float c = close[offset]
        float o = open[offset]
        float h = high[offset]
        float l = low[offset]
        int prev_off = f_clamp(offset + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        float c_prev = close[prev_off]
        float o_prev = open[prev_off]
        float h_prev = high[prev_off]
        float l_prev = low[prev_off]
        if is_bull
            // Предыдущая свеча медвежья, текущая закрывается выше high предыдущей
            if c_prev < o_prev and c > h_prev
                res := true
        else
            // Предыдущая свеча бычья, текущая закрывается ниже low предыдущей
            if c_prev > o_prev and c < l_prev
                res := true
    res

// ── V255: Doji — нерешительность рынка (тело < 10% диапазона) ─────────────
f_is_doji(int idx) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET
        float c = close[offset]
        float o = open[offset]
        float h = high[offset]
        float l = low[offset]
        float body  = math.abs(c - o)
        float range_ = h - l
        if range_ > 0
            res := body <= range_ * 0.1
    res

// ── V255: Hammer (бычий) / Hanging Man (медвежий) ─────────────────────────
// Hammer: маленькое тело вверху, длинный нижний хвост ≥ 2× тело
// Hanging Man: маленькое тело внизу, длинный верхний хвост ≥ 2× тело
f_is_hammer(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET
        float c = close[offset]
        float o = open[offset]
        float h = high[offset]
        float l = low[offset]
        float body  = math.abs(c - o)
        float upper = h - math.max(c, o)
        float lower = math.min(c, o) - l
        float range_ = h - l
        if range_ > 0 and body > 0
            if is_bull
                // Hammer: длинный нижний хвост, маленький верхний
                res := (lower >= body * 2.0) and (upper <= body * 0.5)
            else
                // Hanging Man: длинный верхний хвост, маленький нижний
                res := (upper >= body * 2.0) and (lower <= body * 0.5)
    res

// V260: Inverted hammer is just hammer with inverted direction
f_is_inverted_hammer(int idx, bool is_bull) => f_is_hammer(idx, not is_bull)

// V260: Morning/Evening Star merged (бычий/медвежий 3-свечной разворот)
f_is_star(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET_3
        float c0 = close[offset]
        float o0 = open[offset]
        int off1 = f_clamp(offset + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        float c1 = close[off1]
        float o1 = open[off1]
        int off2 = f_clamp(offset + 2, MAX_OFFSET)
        float c2 = close[off2]
        float o2 = open[off2]
        float body1 = math.abs(c1 - o1)
        float body2 = math.abs(c2 - o2)
        float range2 = high[off2] - low[off2]
        bool dir2 = is_bull ? (c2 < o2) : (c2 > o2)
        bool dir0 = is_bull ? (c0 > o0) : (c0 < o0)
        if range2 > 0 and body2 > range2 * 0.3 and dir2
            if body1 < body2 * 0.5
                float mid2 = (c2 + o2) / 2.0
                if dir0 and (is_bull ? (c0 > mid2) : (c0 < mid2))
                    res := true
    res
f_is_morning_star(int idx) => f_is_star(idx, true)
f_is_evening_star(int idx) => f_is_star(idx, false)

// ── V258: Харами (Harami) — тело второй свечи внутри первой ──────────────
// Bull Harami: первая красная, вторая зелёная и тело внутри первой
// Bear Harami: первая зелёная, вторая красная и тело внутри первой
f_is_harami(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    bool res    = false
    int  offset = bar_index - idx
    if offset >= 0 and offset <= MAX_OFFSET_2
        float c0 = close[offset]
        float o0 = open[offset]
        int off1 = f_clamp(offset + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        float c1 = close[off1]
        float o1 = open[off1]
        float body0_hi = math.max(c0, o0)
        float body0_lo = math.min(c0, o0)
        float body1_hi = math.max(c1, o1)
        float body1_lo = math.min(c1, o1)
        // Тело текущей свечи полностью внутри тела предыдущей
        if body0_hi < body1_hi and body0_lo > body1_lo
            if is_bull
                // Bull Harami: предыдущая красная, текущая зелёная
                if c1 < o1 and c0 > o0
                    res := true
            else
                // Bear Harami: предыдущая зелёная, текущая красная
                if c1 > o1 and c0 < o0
                    res := true
    res

// V270: Three White Soldiers / Three Black Crows
f_is_three_soldiers(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o1 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o2 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx + 2, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 0 and (bar_index - idx + 2) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        if is_bull
            result := close[o0] > open[o0] and close[o1] > open[o1] and close[o2] > open[o2] and close[o1] > close[o0] and close[o2] > close[o1] and math.abs(close[o0]-open[o0]) > (high[o0]-low[o0])*0.5 and math.abs(close[o1]-open[o1]) > (high[o1]-low[o1])*0.5 and math.abs(close[o2]-open[o2]) > (high[o2]-low[o2])*0.5
        else
            result := close[o0] < open[o0] and close[o1] < open[o1] and close[o2] < open[o2] and close[o1] < close[o0] and close[o2] < close[o1] and math.abs(close[o0]-open[o0]) > (high[o0]-low[o0])*0.5 and math.abs(close[o1]-open[o1]) > (high[o1]-low[o1])*0.5 and math.abs(close[o2]-open[o2]) > (high[o2]-low[o2])*0.5
    result

// V270: Tweezer Top / Tweezer Bottom
f_is_tweezer(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o1 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 0 and (bar_index - idx + 1) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        float tol = (high[o0] - low[o0]) * 0.05
        if is_bull
            result := math.abs(low[o0] - low[o1]) <= math.max(tol, syminfo.mintick * 2) and close[o1] > open[o1]
        else
            result := math.abs(high[o0] - high[o1]) <= math.max(tol, syminfo.mintick * 2) and close[o1] < open[o1]
    result

// V270: Inside Bar detection
f_is_inside_bar(int idx) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o1 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx - 1, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 1 and (bar_index - idx) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        result := high[o0] <= high[o1] and low[o0] >= low[o1]
    result

// V270: Marubozu detection (body > 90% range)
f_is_marubozu(int idx) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 0 and (bar_index - idx) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        float rng = high[o0] - low[o0]
        float body = math.abs(close[o0] - open[o0])
        result := rng > 0 and body >= rng * 0.9
    result

// V273: Outside Bar detection (range engulfs previous bar's range)
f_is_outside_bar(int idx) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o1 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx - 1, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 1 and (bar_index - idx) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        result := high[o0] > high[o1] and low[o0] < low[o1]
    result

// V273: Fakey pattern (false breakout of inside bar = trap)
f_is_fakey(int idx, bool is_bull) =>
    int o0 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o1 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx + 1, MAX_OFFSET)
    int o2 = f_clamp(bar_index - idx + 2, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool safe = (bar_index - idx) >= 0 and (bar_index - idx + 2) <= MAX_OFFSET
    bool result = false
    if safe
        bool bar1_inside = high[o1] <= high[o2] and low[o1] >= low[o2]
        if bar1_inside
            if is_bull
                result := low[o0] < low[o1] and close[o0] > low[o1]
            else
                result := high[o0] > high[o1] and close[o0] < high[o1]
    result

// ── V258: Мульти-паттерн бонус — увеличение Score зоны ────────────────────
// Подсчёт выполненных условий (PPR, Pin-Bar, Engulfing, Doji, Hammer,
// Inverted Hammer, Morning/Evening Star, Harami)
// и применение процентного бонуса к стандартному Score:
//   1 условие  → стандартный Score (без бонуса)
//   2 условия  → +10% Score
//   3 условия  → +30% Score
//   4 условия  → +40% Score
//   5+ условий → +50% Score
f_multi_pattern_bonus(float base_score, int condition_count) =>
    float bonus_pct = condition_count >= 5 ? 0.50 :
         condition_count == 4 ? 0.40 :
         condition_count == 3 ? 0.30 :
         condition_count == 2 ? 0.10 : 0.0
    base_score * bonus_pct

f_calc_efficiency(int idx, int len) =>
    // V253: ta.highest/lowest вместо ручного цикла
    int   win   = math.min(math.max(len, 1), MAX_BUFF)
    float h_max = ta.highest(high, win)
    float l_min = ta.lowest(low, win)
    if len == 0
        0.0
    else
        int safe_idx  = f_clamp(idx, MAX_OFFSET)
        int safe_back = f_clamp(idx + len, MAX_OFFSET)
        float net_change = math.abs(close[safe_idx] - close[safe_back])
        float approx_path = h_max - l_min
        approx_path != 0.0 ? (net_change / approx_path) : 0.0

f_get_sigmoid_score(float val, float min_v, float max_v, float weight) =>
    if na(val)
        0.0
    else
        float mid      = (min_v + max_v) / 2.0
        float k        = f_safe_div(4.0, math.max(max_v - min_v, 0.0001))
        float raw_sig  = 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-k * (val - mid)))
        // Нормализация: sigmoid(min_v) ≈ 0.119, sigmoid(max_v) ≈ 0.881
        // Масштабируем в полный [0, 1] диапазон
        float sig_at_min = 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-k * (min_v - mid)))
        float sig_at_max = 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-k * (max_v - mid)))
        float range_s    = math.max(sig_at_max - sig_at_min, 0.0001)
        float normalized = math.max(0.0, math.min(f_safe_div(raw_sig - sig_at_min, range_s), 1.0))
        weight * normalized

f_get_log_vol_score(float val, float min_v, float max_v, float weight) =>
    float safe_val = na(val) ? min_v : math.max(val, min_v)
    float max_safe = math.max(max_v, min_v + 0.1)
    float log_val  = math.log(1.0 + (safe_val - min_v))
    float log_max  = math.log(1.0 + (max_safe - min_v))
    weight * math.min(f_safe_div(log_val, log_max), 1.0)

// V279: Expanded zone score computation — 9 weighted components
// Adds: Market Regime Alignment, Session Quality, Multi-TF Confluence
// Improves: Graduated trend alignment, continuous sweep scoring
f_compute_zone_score(float z_val, float vol_val, bool is_aligned,
     bool is_struct_sweep, bool is_wick_sweep, float eff_val,
     bool has_break, bool has_engulf, bool has_sweep_vol,
     float cluster_vol_bonus, float dyn_z, float dyn_v) =>
    float score = 0.0
    // 1. Z-Score component [0, w_zscore_norm]
    score += f_get_sigmoid_score(z_val, dyn_z, p_z_max, w_zscore_norm)
    // 2. Volume component [0, w_vol_norm]
    score += f_get_log_vol_score(vol_val, dyn_v, p_vol_max, w_vol_norm)
    // 3. V279: Graduated Trend Alignment [0, w_trend_norm]
    // Full alignment (HTF + ITF) = 1.0, Partial (ITF only) = 0.5, Counter = 0.0
    float trend_score = 0.0
    if is_aligned  // HTF aligned
        trend_score := w_trend_norm  // Full alignment
    else
        // V279: Partial credit when HTF is not aligned but ITF may be
        // Note: ITF alignment not checkable here (not passed as parameter)
        // 50% credit as conservative estimate for non-counter-trend scenarios
        trend_score := w_trend_norm * 0.5
    score += trend_score
    // 4. V279: Continuous Sweep / Liquidity Grab [0, w_sweep_norm]
    // sweep_score = 0.3 + 0.7 × min(1.0, quality) — continuous function
    float sweep_quality = is_struct_sweep ? 1.0 : (is_wick_sweep ? 0.6 : 0.0)
    float s_sw = 0.0
    if sweep_quality > 0
        float cont_sweep = 0.3 + 0.7 * math.min(1.0, sweep_quality)
        // V279: Volume-confirmed sweep gets 1.3× multiplier
        if has_sweep_vol
            cont_sweep := math.min(1.0, cont_sweep * 1.3)
        s_sw := w_sweep_norm * cont_sweep
    score += s_sw
    // 5. Efficiency / FER [0, w_eff_norm]
    score += f_get_sigmoid_score(eff_val, 0.3, 0.9, w_eff_norm)
    // 6. PA Bonus (Break + Engulf + Sweep Vol) [0, w_bonus_norm]
    float s_bonus = 0.0
    if has_break
        s_bonus += w_bonus_norm * 0.4
    if has_engulf
        s_bonus += w_bonus_norm * 0.4
    if has_sweep_vol and is_aligned
        s_bonus += w_bonus_norm * 0.2
    score += s_bonus
    // 7. V279: Market Regime Alignment [0, w_regime_norm]
    // Trending regime + aligned zone = full weight; ranging = 0.5; counter = 0
    float regime_score = 0.0
    if _regime_type == 0  // trending_up
        regime_score := is_aligned ? w_regime_norm : 0.0
    else if _regime_type == 1  // trending_down
        regime_score := is_aligned ? w_regime_norm : 0.0
    else if _regime_type == 2  // ranging
        regime_score := w_regime_norm * 0.5
    else  // volatile
        regime_score := w_regime_norm * 0.3
    score += regime_score
    // 8. V279: Session Quality [0, w_session_norm]
    // London/NY kill zone = full, Asia = 0.5, Quiet = 0.2
    float session_score = 0.0
    if kz_overlap
        session_score := w_session_norm  // London-NY overlap = best
    else if kz_london or kz_ny
        session_score := w_session_norm * 0.8
    else if kz_asia
        session_score := w_session_norm * 0.5
    else
        session_score := w_session_norm * 0.2
    score += session_score
    // 9. V279: Multi-TF Confluence placeholder [0, w_mtf_norm]
    // Uses Hurst exponent as proxy: H > 0.6 = trending on multiple TFs = higher score
    float hurst_proxy = nz(_hurst_val, 0.5)
    float mtf_score = 0.0
    if hurst_proxy > 0.6
        mtf_score := w_mtf_norm * math.min(1.0, (hurst_proxy - 0.5) * 5.0)
    else
        mtf_score := w_mtf_norm * 0.3
    score += mtf_score
    // Cluster volume bonus (capped)
    score += math.min(cluster_vol_bonus, 25.0)
    score

var array<RejectedInfo> rejected_db = array.new<RejectedInfo>()

// V260: Unified pattern counting, naming & scoring
f_count_score_patterns(bool p_ppr, bool p_pin, bool p_engulf, bool p_doji, bool p_hammer, bool p_inv_h, bool p_star, bool p_harami, bool p_rspike, bool is_bull, float base_score) =>
    array<string> _pats = array.new<string>()
    if p_ppr
        array.push(_pats, "PPR")
    if p_pin
        array.push(_pats, "Pin")
    if p_engulf
        array.push(_pats, "Engulf")
    if p_doji
        array.push(_pats, "Doji")
    if p_hammer
        array.push(_pats, is_bull ? "Hammer" : "ShootStar")
    if p_inv_h
        array.push(_pats, is_bull ? "InvHammer" : "HangMan")
    if p_star
        array.push(_pats, is_bull ? "MornStar" : "EveStar")
    if p_harami
        array.push(_pats, "Harami")
    if p_rspike
        array.push(_pats, "Impulse")
    int cnt = array.size(_pats)
    string pat_str = f_ts(cnt) + " pat: " + (cnt > 0 ? array.join(_pats, ",") : "—")
    float adj_score = base_score
    bool impulse_conf = p_pin and p_rspike
    if cnt < p_multi_pattern_min and not impulse_conf
        adj_score := adj_score * MULTI_PATTERN_PENALTY
    if cnt >= 2
        adj_score += f_multi_pattern_bonus(base_score, cnt)
    [cnt, pat_str, adj_score]

f_cluster(int swing_idx, bool is_bull, bool do_calc, int limit_len, float hist_atr, string ext_reason, float dyn_z, float dyn_v, float dyn_fvg) =>
    float  o_t            = na
    float  o_b            = na
    bool   fd             = false
    box    bx             = na
    float  final_score    = 0.0
    string tier_res       = "NORMAL"
    float  sniper_lvl     = na
    float  idm_lvl        = na
    string debug_log      = ""
    string final_fvg_type = "None"
    string patterns_str   = ""
    bool   run_calc       = do_calc

    float _mem_rvol = rvol
    float _mem_z    = z_score
    float _mem_rsi  = rsi_val
    bool  _mem_brk  = in_brokezone
    float _mem_atr = atr_val
    max_bars_back(_mem_rvol, MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_z,    MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_rsi,  MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_brk,  MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_atr, MAX_BUFF)
    
    float diag_z_val = 0.0
    float diag_v_val = 0.0
    bool  diag_align = false
    bool  is_too_old = not na(swing_idx) and (bar_index - swing_idx > p_max_history)

    // V255: вынос ta.highest/ta.lowest из условного блока для серийной согласованности
    int   _eff_win   = math.min(math.max(p_eff_len, 1), MAX_BUFF)
    float _eff_h_max = ta.highest(high, _eff_win)
    float _eff_l_min = ta.lowest(low, _eff_win)

    if run_calc and not is_too_old
        int b_off_guard = bar_index - swing_idx
        // V249: clamp guard
        if b_off_guard >= 0 and b_off_guard <= MAX_OFFSET
            float p_c    = close[b_off_guard]
            float p_o    = open[b_off_guard]
            float p_h_grd = high[b_off_guard]
            float p_l_grd = low[b_off_guard]
            float p_body = math.abs(p_c - p_o)
            float safe_body = p_body == 0 ? syminfo.mintick : p_body
            if is_bull
                float body_bot  = math.min(p_o, p_c)
                float lower_wick = body_bot - p_l_grd
                if lower_wick < (safe_body * inp_wick_rat)
                    run_calc := false
            else
                float body_top  = math.max(p_o, p_c)
                float upper_wick = p_h_grd - body_top
                if upper_wick < (safe_body * inp_wick_rat)
                    run_calc := false
        else
            run_calc := false

    if run_calc and is_too_old
        if debug_mode
            RejectedInfo r = RejectedInfo.new(swing_idx, is_bull, 0.0, "❌ GUARD: Too Old / History Limit", bar_index)
            array.push(rejected_db, r)
            while array.size(rejected_db) > 30
                array.shift(rejected_db)

    else if run_calc and not is_too_old
        array<string> log_arr = na
        if debug_mode
            log_arr := array.new<string>()
            array.push(log_arr, "━━━━━ MATH V249 ━━━━━")

        int b_off        = bar_index - swing_idx
        // V249: Все дальнейшие обращения через clamp
        int TARGET_BARS  = math.max(1, limit_len)
        float cluster_h  = -1.0e9
        float cluster_l  = 1.0e9
        int search_depth = math.max(15, TARGET_BARS * 10)
        // V279: Adaptive tolerance — higher volume widens tolerance for more significant zones
        float vol_ratio_local = nz(rvol, 1.0)
        float adaptive_tol_mult = 1.0 + math.min(vol_ratio_local, 3.0) / 3.0
        float noise_tol  = math.max(syminfo.mintick, hist_atr * p_cluster_tol * adaptive_tol_mult)
        float cluster_vol_bonus = 0.0
        int candles_found = 0
        // V279: Soft cluster — noise counting and volume-weighted boundaries
        int noise_count  = 0
        int correct_count = 0
        float vwap_h_sum = 0.0  // volume-weighted high accumulator
        float vwap_l_sum = 0.0  // volume-weighted low accumulator
        float vwap_vol_sum = 0.0  // total volume for VWAP weighting
        int safe_hist_off = math.min(p_max_history - b_off - 1, bar_index - b_off - 1)
        int max_search    = math.min(search_depth, math.max(0, safe_hist_off))
        // V249: жёсткий потолок
        int hist_ceil     = math.min(p_max_history - 1, MAX_OFFSET)

        for k = 0 to max_search
            if candles_found >= TARGET_BARS
                break
            int idx = b_off + k
            if idx > hist_ceil
                break
            int safe_k = f_clamp(idx, MAX_OFFSET)
            float c = close[safe_k]
            float o = open[safe_k]
            float h = high[safe_k]
            float l = low[safe_k]
            bool is_red   = (c < o)
            bool is_green = (c > o)
            bool is_doji  = (c == o)
            float loc_rvol = not na(_mem_rvol[safe_k]) ? _mem_rvol[safe_k] : 1.0
            float loc_vol  = nz(volume[safe_k], 1.0)

            if is_bull
                if k == 0
                    cluster_h := h
                    cluster_l := l
                    candles_found += 1
                    correct_count += 1
                    cluster_vol_bonus += (loc_rvol > 1.0 ? loc_rvol * 3.0 : 0.0)
                    // V279: Volume-weighted boundaries
                    vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol
                    vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol
                    vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol
                else
                    if is_red or is_doji
                        cluster_h := math.max(cluster_h, h)
                        cluster_l := math.min(cluster_l, l)
                        candles_found += 1
                        correct_count += 1
                        cluster_vol_bonus += (loc_rvol > 1.0 ? loc_rvol * 3.0 : 0.0)
                        vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol
                        vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol
                        vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol
                    else if is_green
                        // V279: Soft cluster — allow noise candles up to inp_noise_tolerance
                        if noise_count >= inp_noise_tolerance
                            if l < (cluster_l - noise_tol)
                                break
                            else
                                // V279: Check dominance ratio before stopping
                                // +1 in denominator accounts for this candle being considered (lookahead)
                                float dominance = candles_found > 0 ? float(correct_count) / float(candles_found + 1) : 0.0
                                if dominance < inp_cluster_dominance
                                    break
                                cluster_h := math.max(cluster_h, h)
                        else
                            noise_count += 1
                            candles_found += 1
                            cluster_h := math.max(cluster_h, h)
                            cluster_l := math.min(cluster_l, l)
                            // V279: Noise candles get reduced volume weight
                            vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol * 0.5
                            vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol * 0.5
                            vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol * 0.5
            else
                if k == 0
                    cluster_h := h
                    cluster_l := l
                    candles_found += 1
                    correct_count += 1
                    cluster_vol_bonus += (loc_rvol > 1.0 ? loc_rvol * 3.0 : 0.0)
                    vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol
                    vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol
                    vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol
                else
                    if is_green or is_doji
                        cluster_h := math.max(cluster_h, h)
                        cluster_l := math.min(cluster_l, l)
                        candles_found += 1
                        correct_count += 1
                        cluster_vol_bonus += (loc_rvol > 1.0 ? loc_rvol * 3.0 : 0.0)
                        vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol
                        vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol
                        vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol
                    else if is_red
                        // V279: Soft cluster — allow noise candles up to inp_noise_tolerance
                        if noise_count >= inp_noise_tolerance
                            if h > (cluster_h + noise_tol)
                                break
                            else
                                // +1 in denominator accounts for this candle being considered (lookahead)
                                float dominance = candles_found > 0 ? float(correct_count) / float(candles_found + 1) : 0.0
                                if dominance < inp_cluster_dominance
                                    break
                                cluster_l := math.min(cluster_l, l)
                        else
                            noise_count += 1
                            candles_found += 1
                            cluster_h := math.max(cluster_h, h)
                            cluster_l := math.min(cluster_l, l)
                            vwap_h_sum += h * loc_vol * 0.5
                            vwap_l_sum += l * loc_vol * 0.5
                            vwap_vol_sum += loc_vol * 0.5

        if candles_found == 0
            int safe_b = f_clamp(b_off, MAX_OFFSET)
            cluster_h := high[safe_b]
            cluster_l := low[safe_b]

        // V279: Volume-weighted boundary refinement
        // When we have enough volume data, shift boundaries toward volume-weighted levels
        if vwap_vol_sum > 0 and candles_found >= 2
            float vw_h = vwap_h_sum / vwap_vol_sum
            float vw_l = vwap_l_sum / vwap_vol_sum
            // Blend 30% VWAP + 70% raw extremes for stability
            cluster_h := cluster_h * 0.7 + vw_h * 0.3
            cluster_l := cluster_l * 0.7 + vw_l * 0.3
            // Safety: ensure h >= l
            if cluster_h < cluster_l
                float _tmp = cluster_h
                cluster_h := cluster_l
                cluster_l := _tmp

        float abs_extreme_h   = cluster_h
        float abs_extreme_l   = cluster_l
        int lookback_limit    = math.min(p_max_history - b_off - 1, bar_index - b_off - 1)
        lookback_limit := math.min(lookback_limit, math.max(30, (is_bull ? p_pivot_left : p_pivot_left_res) * 3))

        for m = 1 to lookback_limit
            int idx_m = b_off + m
            if idx_m > hist_ceil
                break
            int safe_m = f_clamp(idx_m, MAX_OFFSET)
            if not is_bull
                if close[safe_m] < cluster_l - (hist_atr * 0.1)
                    break
                if high[safe_m] > abs_extreme_h
                    abs_extreme_h := high[safe_m]
            else
                if close[safe_m] > cluster_h + (hist_atr * 0.1)
                    break
                if low[safe_m] < abs_extreme_l
                    abs_extreme_l := low[safe_m]

        float c_h = not is_bull ? abs_extreme_h : cluster_h
        float c_l = is_bull ? abs_extreme_l : cluster_l

        idm_lvl := is_bull ? last_sl : last_sh

        int   sn_idx = f_clamp(b_off, MAX_OFFSET)
        float sw_h   = high[sn_idx]
        float sw_l   = low[sn_idx]
        float sw_o   = open[sn_idx]
        float sw_c   = close[sn_idx]

        if is_bull
            float body_bot = math.min(sw_o, sw_c)
            float wick_len = body_bot - sw_l
            if wick_len > (sw_h - sw_l) * sniper_fit
                sniper_lvl := sw_l + (wick_len * sniper_prc)
            else
                sniper_lvl := body_bot
        else
            float body_top = math.max(sw_o, sw_c)
            float wick_len = sw_h - body_top
            if wick_len > (sw_h - sw_l) * sniper_fit
                sniper_lvl := sw_h - (wick_len * sniper_prc)
            else
                sniper_lvl := body_top

        int   best_impulse_idx = na
        int   backup_idx       = na
        bool  has_fvg          = false
        bool  align            = false
        float val_vol          = 1.0
        float z_val            = 0.0
        float found_ft         = na
        float found_fb         = na

        int loop_limit = math.max(0, p_fvg_lookback - 1)
        for i = 0 to loop_limit
            int idx_check  = swing_idx + i
            int off_check  = bar_index - idx_check
            // V249: нужен [off_check + 1] в f_calc_fvg_on_candle
            bool idx_safe  = off_check >= 1 and off_check <= MAX_OFFSET_2
            if not idx_safe
                break
            float current_step_atr = nz(_mem_atr[f_clamp(off_check, MAX_OFFSET)], 1.0)
            int safe_oc = f_clamp(off_check, MAX_OFFSET)
            bool dir_ok = is_bull ? (close[safe_oc] > open[safe_oc]) : (close[safe_oc] < open[safe_oc])
            if dir_ok
                if na(backup_idx)
                    backup_idx := idx_check
                bool z_gate = not na(_mem_z[safe_oc]) and _mem_z[safe_oc] >= dyn_z
                float check_vol = not na(_mem_rvol[safe_oc]) ? _mem_rvol[safe_oc] : 1.0
                bool  v_gate = not use_vol_flt or (check_vol >= math.max(dyn_v, p_fvg_rvol_min))
                if z_gate and v_gate
                    [f_sz_temp, ft, fb, g_type_temp] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(idx_check, is_bull, current_step_atr)
                    bool has_real_fvg = f_sz_temp >= dyn_fvg and f_sz_temp <= p_fvg_max
                    if has_real_fvg
                        best_impulse_idx := idx_check
                        found_ft := ft
                        found_fb := fb
                        final_fvg_type := g_type_temp
                        has_fvg := true
                        break

        if na(best_impulse_idx) and not na(backup_idx)
            best_impulse_idx := backup_idx

        if not has_fvg
            if req_fvg
                run_calc := false
            else if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
                array.push(log_arr, "⚠️ PENALTY: No FVG (-15% to Final Score)")

        int _pre_off_eff = not na(best_impulse_idx) ? (bar_index - best_impulse_idx) : 0
        int _pre_soc_eff = f_clamp(_pre_off_eff, MAX_OFFSET)
        // V255: инлайн вычисление efficiency с предвычисленными _eff_h_max/_eff_l_min
        float _eff_path  = _eff_h_max - _eff_l_min
        float _pre_eff   = (_eff_path != 0.0 and p_eff_len > 0) ? f_safe_div(math.abs(close[_pre_soc_eff] - close[f_clamp(_pre_off_eff + p_eff_len, MAX_OFFSET)]), _eff_path) : 0.0

        if not na(best_impulse_idx) and run_calc
            int off_check = bar_index - best_impulse_idx
            int safe_oc   = f_clamp(off_check, MAX_OFFSET)
            z_val := not na(_mem_z[safe_oc]) ? _mem_z[safe_oc] : 0.0
            val_vol := na(_mem_rvol[safe_oc]) ? 1.0 : _mem_rvol[safe_oc]
            align := is_bull ? global_bull : global_bear

            diag_z_val := z_val
            diag_v_val := val_vol
            diag_align := align

            bool is_wick_sweep   = f_check_sweep(swing_idx, is_bull)
            bool is_struct_sweep = f_verify_structural_sweep(swing_idx, is_bull)
            bool has_sweep_vol   = (is_struct_sweep or is_wick_sweep) and val_vol > p_mom_rvol

            // V269: Use extracted f_compute_zone_score() for 6 weighted components
            final_score += f_compute_zone_score(z_val, val_vol, align,
                 is_struct_sweep, is_wick_sweep, _pre_eff,
                 _mem_brk[safe_oc], f_is_engulfing(best_impulse_idx, is_bull), has_sweep_vol,
                 cluster_vol_bonus > 0 ? cluster_vol_bonus : 0.0, dyn_z, dyn_v)

            float rsi_at_zone = na(_mem_rsi[safe_oc]) ? 50.0 : _mem_rsi[safe_oc]
            if use_rsi
                if is_bull  and rsi_at_zone < inp_rsi_os
                    final_score += 10.0
                if not is_bull and rsi_at_zone > inp_rsi_ob
                    final_score += 10.0
            // V273: BPR, Inverse FVG, Stacked FVG bonuses
            float _bpr_atr = nz(_mem_atr[safe_oc], 1.0)
            [_has_bpr, _bpr_t, _bpr_b, _has_inv_fvg] = f_check_bpr_and_inverse(best_impulse_idx, is_bull, _bpr_atr)
            if _has_bpr
                final_score += 10.0  // BPR: balanced zone confirmation
                if not na(_bpr_t) and not na(_bpr_b)
                    final_fvg_type := "BPR"
            if _has_inv_fvg
                final_score := final_score * 0.90  // Inverse FVG penalty (counter-signal)
            float _stacked_bonus = f_check_stacked_fvg(best_impulse_idx, is_bull, _bpr_atr)
            if _stacked_bonus > 0
                final_score += _stacked_bonus
            // V254: Мульти-пин-бар бонус для OB (Support/Resistance)
            // Сканируем свечи на пивоте и считаем пин-бары — больше пин-баров = надёжнее зона
            int ob_pin_count = 0
            int ob_pin_scan  = math.min(inp_pinbar_lookback, MAX_OFFSET - safe_oc)
            for pki = 0 to math.max(ob_pin_scan - 1, 0)
                int pks = f_clamp(safe_oc + pki, MAX_OFFSET)
                float pkr = high[pks] - low[pks]
                float pkb = math.abs(close[pks] - open[pks])
                if pkr > 0 and pkb > 0
                    if is_bull
                        float pkl = math.min(close[pks], open[pks]) - low[pks]
                        if pkl > pkb * inp_pin_ratio
                            ob_pin_count += 1
                    else
                        float pku = high[pks] - math.max(close[pks], open[pks])
                        if pku > pkb * inp_pin_ratio
                            ob_pin_count += 1
            if ob_pin_count >= 1
                float pin_bonus = math.min(20.0, float(ob_pin_count) * 5.0 + 3.0)
                if ob_pin_count < inp_min_pinbars
                    pin_bonus := pin_bonus * 0.6
                final_score += pin_bonus

            // V254: Обратный всплеск бонус для OB (Support/Resistance)
            // Ищем импульсную свечу в обратном направлении после пивота
            bool ob_rspike = false
            int ob_rspike_scan = math.min(inp_rspike_lookfwd, safe_oc)
            for rsi_k = 1 to math.max(ob_rspike_scan, 1)
                int rsk = f_clamp(safe_oc - rsi_k, MAX_OFFSET)
                if rsk >= 0
                    float orkv = nz(_mem_rvol[rsk], 1.0)
                    float orkb = math.abs(close[rsk] - open[rsk])
                    float orkr = high[rsk] - low[rsk]
                    bool orkd = is_bull ? (close[rsk] > open[rsk]) : (close[rsk] < open[rsk])
                    if orkd and orkr > 0 and (orkb >= orkr * 0.5) and (orkv >= inp_rspike_rvol)
                        ob_rspike := true
                        break
            if ob_rspike
                final_score += 12.0
            if not has_fvg
                final_score := final_score * 0.85
            // V259: Мульти-паттерн бонус для OB — подсчёт условий и бонус к Score
            // Паттерны проверяются на свече пивота (swing_idx) и соседних (±1),
            // т.к. разворотные паттерны формируются у пивота, а не на импульсной свече.
            // Условия: PPR, Pin-Bar, Engulfing, Doji, Hammer, Inverted Hammer, Morning/Evening Star, Harami, Impulse
            // V259: Индексы свечи пивота и соседей для сканирования паттернов
            int _sw0    = swing_idx
            int _sw_prv = swing_idx > 0 ? (swing_idx - 1) : swing_idx
            int _sw_nxt = (swing_idx + 1 <= bar_index) ? (swing_idx + 1) : swing_idx
            bool ob_has_ppr      = f_is_ppr(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_ppr(_sw_prv, is_bull) or f_is_ppr(_sw_nxt, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_pinbar   = ob_pin_count >= 1
            bool ob_has_engulf   = f_is_engulfing(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_engulfing(_sw_prv, is_bull) or f_is_engulfing(_sw_nxt, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_doji     = f_is_doji(_sw0) or f_is_doji(_sw_prv) or f_is_doji(_sw_nxt)
            bool ob_has_hammer   = f_is_hammer(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_hammer(_sw_prv, is_bull) or f_is_hammer(_sw_nxt, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_inv_hammer = f_is_inverted_hammer(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_inverted_hammer(_sw_prv, is_bull) or f_is_inverted_hammer(_sw_nxt, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_star     = is_bull ? (f_is_morning_star(_sw0) or f_is_morning_star(_sw_prv) or f_is_morning_star(_sw_nxt)) : (f_is_evening_star(_sw0) or f_is_evening_star(_sw_prv) or f_is_evening_star(_sw_nxt))
            bool ob_has_harami   = f_is_harami(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_harami(_sw_prv, is_bull) or f_is_harami(_sw_nxt, is_bull)
            // V260: Unified pattern counting, naming & scoring via helper
            [ob_cond_count, _tmp_patterns_str, _tmp_final_score] = f_count_score_patterns(ob_has_ppr, ob_has_pinbar, ob_has_engulf, ob_has_doji, ob_has_hammer, ob_has_inv_hammer, ob_has_star, ob_has_harami, ob_rspike, is_bull, final_score)
            patterns_str := _tmp_patterns_str
            final_score := _tmp_final_score
            // V270: Additional pattern bonuses
            bool ob_has_soldiers = f_is_three_soldiers(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_three_soldiers(_sw_prv, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_tweezer = f_is_tweezer(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_tweezer(_sw_prv, is_bull)
            bool ob_has_inside = f_is_inside_bar(_sw0) or f_is_inside_bar(_sw_prv)
            bool ob_has_marubozu = f_is_marubozu(_sw0) or f_is_marubozu(_sw_prv)
            if ob_has_soldiers
                final_score += 10.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",3WS"
            if ob_has_tweezer
                final_score += 8.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",Twzr"
            if ob_has_inside
                final_score += 5.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",IB"
            if ob_has_marubozu
                final_score += 12.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",Maru"
            // V273: Outside Bar and Fakey pattern bonuses
            bool ob_has_outside = f_is_outside_bar(_sw0) or f_is_outside_bar(_sw_prv)
            bool ob_has_fakey = f_is_fakey(_sw0, is_bull) or f_is_fakey(_sw_prv, is_bull)
            if ob_has_outside
                final_score += 8.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",OutBar"
            if ob_has_fakey
                final_score += 10.0
                patterns_str := patterns_str + ",Fakey"
            final_score := math.min(final_score, 150.0)
            if ob_cond_count < p_multi_pattern_min and not (ob_has_pinbar and ob_rspike)
                if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
                    array.push(log_arr, "⚠️ LOW PATTERNS: " + f_ts(ob_cond_count) + "/" + f_ts(p_multi_pattern_min))
            // V254: Гарантия что score не превышает потолок 150 после всех бонусов
            final_score := math.min(final_score, 150.0)
            float current_step_atr = nz(_mem_atr[safe_oc], 1.0)
            [f_sz, ft, fb, tmp_type] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(best_impulse_idx, is_bull, current_step_atr)

            if use_score and final_score < p_min_score
                if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
                    array.push(log_arr, "❌ REJECTED: Score " + str.tostring(final_score, "#.0"))
                fd := false
            else
                if final_score >= 100
                    tier_res := "BEST"
                else if final_score >= 80
                    tier_res := "STRONG"
                else if final_score >= 40
                    tier_res := "NORMAL"
                else
                    tier_res := "PIVOT"

                float zone_h      = math.abs(c_h - c_l)
                float atr_now     = hist_atr
                bool zone_size_ok = (atr_now > 0) ? (zone_h >= atr_now * 0.1 and zone_h <= atr_now * 8.0) : true

                if not zone_size_ok
                    fd := false
                    if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
                        array.push(log_arr, "❌ ATR SIZE: " + str.tostring(f_safe_div(zone_h, atr_now), "#.1") + " ATR")
                else
                    if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
                        string type_str = has_fvg ? " [" + final_fvg_type + "]" : ""
                        array.push(log_arr, "✅ ACCEPTED: " + tier_res + " (" + str.tostring(final_score, "#.0") + ")" + type_str)
                    fd  := true
                    o_t := c_h
                    o_b := c_l

                    int  draw_start      = best_impulse_idx + 1
                    // V250: не рисуем отдельный FVG box если FVG целиком внутри OB зоны
                    bool fvg_inside_ob   = not na(found_ft) and not na(found_fb) and
                                           found_ft <= math.max(c_h, c_l) + syminfo.mintick and
                                           found_fb >= math.min(c_h, c_l) - syminfo.mintick
                    bool should_draw_box = show_fvg and has_fvg and not fvg_inside_ob
                    if should_draw_box
                        if not na(found_ft) and not na(found_fb)
                            bx := box.new(draw_start, found_ft, bar_index + 5, found_fb,
                                 border_color=na,
                                 bgcolor=f_fvg_color(final_score, is_bull),
                                 xloc=xloc.bar_index)
                    else
                        bx := na

        if debug_mode and array.size(log_arr) > 0
            string joined = array.join(log_arr, "\n")
            debug_log := str.length(joined) > MAX_STR_LEN ? str.substring(joined, 0, MAX_STR_LEN - TRUNCATE_SUFFIX_LEN) + TRUNCATE_SUFFIX : joined

        if not fd and debug_mode
            array<string> err_log = array.new<string>()
            if not has_fvg and req_fvg
                err_log.push("❌ СТРОГИЙ SMC: Нет FVG на 1-" + f_ts(p_fvg_lookback) + " свече.")
            else if na(best_impulse_idx)
                err_log.push("❌ ИМПУЛЬС: Валидная инициализирующая свеча не найдена.")
            else
                if use_score and final_score < p_min_score
                    float deficit = p_min_score - final_score
                    err_log.push("📉 SCORE: " + str.tostring(final_score, "#.0") + " (Не хватает: " + str.tostring(deficit, "#.0") + ")")
                int off_err = bar_index - best_impulse_idx
                int safe_err = f_clamp(off_err, MAX_OFFSET)
                float atr_err_step = nz(_mem_atr[safe_err], 1.0)
                [f_sz_err, ft_err, fb_err, err_type] = f_calc_fvg_on_candle(best_impulse_idx, is_bull, atr_err_step)
                float real_fvg = na(f_sz_err) ? 0.0 : f_sz_err
                if real_fvg < dyn_fvg
                    err_log.push("📏 GAP: " + str.tostring(real_fvg, "#.######") + " ATR < Мин. " + str.tostring(dyn_fvg, "#.######") + " ATR")
                if diag_z_val < dyn_z
                    err_log.push("📉 Z-SCORE: " + str.tostring(diag_z_val, "#.######") + "σ")
                if use_trend and not diag_align
                    err_log.push("⚖️ СТРУКТУРА: Вектор контр-тренда.")
                if use_vol_flt and diag_v_val < dyn_v
                    err_log.push("🔇 ОБЪЕМ: RVOL " + str.tostring(diag_v_val, "#.######") + " (Нужно: " + str.tostring(dyn_v, "#.######") + ")")
            if array.size(err_log) == 0
                if ext_reason != ""
                    err_log.push("🛡️ ОРКЕСТРАТОР: " + ext_reason)
                else if not run_calc
                    err_log.push("❌ GUARD: Длина хвоста (< " + f_ts(inp_wick_rat*100) + "%)")
                else
                    err_log.push("❌ АНОМАЛИЯ: Математический отказ фильтра.")
            string reasons = array.join(err_log, "\n")
            RejectedInfo r = RejectedInfo.new(swing_idx, is_bull, final_score, reasons, bar_index)
            array.push(rejected_db, r)
            while array.size(rejected_db) > 30
                array.shift(rejected_db)

    [o_t, o_b, fd, bx, final_score, tier_res, sniper_lvl, idm_lvl, debug_log, final_fvg_type, patterns_str]

// ==========================================
// БЛОК 7: ZONE MANAGER (V249: безопасный + визуализация)
// ==========================================
f_delete_zone_graphics(Zone z) =>
    box.delete(z.gfx)
    if not na(z.sn_lbl)
        label.delete(z.sn_lbl)
    if not na(z.debug_lbl)
        label.delete(z.debug_lbl)
    if not na(z.fvg_gfx)
        box.delete(z.fvg_gfx)
    while array.size(z.grid_lines) > 0
        line.delete(array.pop(z.grid_lines))
        label.delete(array.pop(z.grid_labels))
    while array.size(z.fvg_lines) > 0
        line.delete(array.pop(z.fvg_lines))
        label.delete(array.pop(z.fvg_labels))
    // V249: удаляем визуальные эффекты
    f_delete_zone_visuals(z)

f_remove_old_rejected() =>
    if debug_mode and array.size(rejected_db) > 0
        for i = array.size(rejected_db) - 1 to 0
            RejectedInfo r = array.get(rejected_db, i)
            if (bar_index - r.origin_idx > p_max_history)
                array.remove(rejected_db, i)

f_calc_zone_validity(Zone z) =>
    float dist = na(z.bot) or na(z.top) or na(close) ? na :
                 z.is_bull ? f_safe_div(z.bot - close, atr_val) : f_safe_div(close - z.top, atr_val)
    float inv_limit = z.is_bull ? p_inv_dist : p_inv_dist_res
    bool far   = not na(dist) and (dist > inv_limit)
    [dist, far]

f_update_sfp(Zone z) =>
    bool is_sfp_update   = false
    float potential_sniper = na
    bool sfp_bull = z.is_bull and (low < z.bot) and (close >= z.bot)
    bool sfp_bear = not z.is_bull and (high > z.top) and (close <= z.top)

    if sfp_bull or sfp_bear
        float new_price = sfp_bull ? low : high
        bool is_deeper  = (z.sniper_stage != 2) or (sfp_bull ? new_price < z.sniper_price : new_price > z.sniper_price)
        if is_deeper
            potential_sniper := new_price
            is_sfp_update    := true
            // V270: SFP + FVG combo doubles bonus
            float sfp_bonus = 20.0
            if not na(z.fvg_gfx)
                sfp_bonus := 40.0  // doubled when FVG present
            z.score          := math.min(z.score + sfp_bonus, 150.0)
            z.chop_count     := 0
            z.tier := f_tier(z.score)

    if is_sfp_update and not na(potential_sniper)
        z.sniper_price := potential_sniper
        z.sniper_stage := 2
        if not na(z.sn_lbl)
            label.set_xy(z.sn_lbl, bar_index + 5, potential_sniper)
            label.set_text(z.sn_lbl, "🎯 SFP (Boosted) " + f_mt(potential_sniper))
            label.set_color(z.sn_lbl, color.new(color.fuchsia, 0))
            label.set_textcolor(z.sn_lbl, color.white)
        else if show_sniper
            z.sn_lbl := label.new(bar_index + 5, potential_sniper,
                 text="🎯 SFP (Boosted) " + f_mt(potential_sniper),
                 color=color.new(color.fuchsia, 0), textcolor=color.white,
                 style=label.style_label_left, size=size.small)
    false

f_process_critical_changes(Zone z, bool is_closed, float prev_low, float prev_high) =>
    bool real_breakout   = false
    bool deep_wick_broke = false

    if is_closed
        bool is_broken_now  = z.is_bull ? (close < z.bot) : (close > z.top)
        bool reverse_break  = z.is_bull ? (close > z.top) : (close < z.bot)
        bool stitched       = (open > z.top and close < z.bot) or (open < z.bot and close > z.top)
        bool recovered      = z.is_bull  ? (z.pending_break and close >= z.bot and close <= z.top) :
                                           (z.pending_break and close <= z.top and close >= z.bot)

        if recovered and not stitched
            z.pending_break := false
            z.chop_count    := 0
            z.score         := math.min(z.score + 8.0, 150.0)  // Recovery: +8 (слабее чем SFP)
            z.tier := f_tier(z.score)
            float trap_price = z.is_bull ? prev_low : prev_high
            z.sniper_price   := trap_price
            if not na(z.sn_lbl)
                label.set_text(z.sn_lbl, "🪤 TRAP RECOVERY " + f_mt(trap_price))
                label.set_color(z.sn_lbl, color.fuchsia)

        else if stitched
            float body        = math.abs(close - open)
            float rng         = high - low
            bool is_full_body = (rng > 0) and (body > rng * p_mom_ratio)
            bool is_momentum  = is_full_body and (z_score > p_z_min) and (rvol > p_mom_rvol)
            if is_momentum
                if z.pending_break
                    real_breakout := true
                else
                    z.pending_break := true
            else
                z.chop_count += 1

        else if is_broken_now
            if z.pending_break
                real_breakout := true
            else
                z.pending_break := true

        else if reverse_break
            if z.pending_break
                z.chop_count   += 1
                z.pending_break := false

        else
            bool closed_inside = (close <= z.top and close >= z.bot)
            if closed_inside
                z.chop_count += 1

        float squeeze_tol = atr_val * p_squeeze_tol
        if z.is_bull
            if low < (z.bot - squeeze_tol) and close < z.bot
                deep_wick_broke := true
        else
            if high > (z.top + squeeze_tol) and close > z.top
                deep_wick_broke := true

    [real_breakout, deep_wick_broke]

f_handle_zone_removal(Zone z, bool is_closed, bool far, bool deep_wick_broke, bool real_breakout, int i, bool strong_break, float bb_rspike_bonus) =>
    bool is_choppy = z.chop_count >= chopcount_int
    if z.z_type == "BB"
        is_choppy := false
    bool is_expired  = use_zone_age_fade and ((bar_index - z.created_at) > zone_max_age) and z.z_type != "BB"
    bool broke_cond  = (not z.active) or far or deep_wick_broke or is_choppy or real_breakout or is_expired
    if z.pending_break and not real_breakout and not deep_wick_broke and z.active
        broke_cond := false
    bool zone_removed = false

    // V256: BB conversion on single bar close beyond zone (support broken down / resistance broken up)
    bool close_beyond = false
    if is_closed
        if z.is_bull and close < z.bot
            close_beyond := true
        else if not z.is_bull and close > z.top
            close_beyond := true
    bool _trigger_cond = is_closed and close_beyond and use_bb and (z.z_type == "OB" or z.z_type == "BB")
    z.trigger_bb(strong_break, z_score, _trigger_cond, bb_rspike_bonus)
    bool _was_converted = _trigger_cond and z.z_type == "BB" and z.active
    if _was_converted
        z.chop_count    := 0
        z.pending_break := false

    if broke_cond and is_closed
        if not _was_converted
            string order_id = (z.is_bull ? "L_" : "S_") + f_ts(z.origin_idx)
