            // indicator mode: strategy.cancel removed (no order management)
            f_delete_zone_graphics(z)
            array.remove(zone_db, i)
            zone_removed := true
    else
        z.update()

    if z.pending_break and not na(z.sn_lbl)
        label.set_text(z.sn_lbl, "⚠️ Pending Break...")
    zone_removed

f_garbage_collection(array<Zone> to_keep) =>
    if array.size(zone_db) > 0
        for i = array.size(zone_db) - 1 to 0
            Zone z = array.get(zone_db, i)
            bool keep_active = z.active and array.indexof(to_keep, z) != -1
            if not keep_active
                f_delete_zone_graphics(z)
                array.remove(zone_db, i)

f_merge_nested_zones() =>
    int sz = array.size(zone_db)
    if sz > 1
        for i = sz - 1 to 1
            Zone z1 = array.get(zone_db, i)
            if not z1.active or z1.mitigated
                continue
            for j = i - 1 to 0
                Zone z2 = array.get(zone_db, j)
                if not z2.active or z2.mitigated
                    continue
                bool same_dir  = z1.is_bull == z2.is_bull
                bool bb_compat = z1.z_type == "BB" and z2.z_type == "BB"
                bool ob_compat = z1.z_type == "OB" and z2.z_type == "OB"
                bool rz_compat = z1.z_type == "RZ" and z2.z_type == "RZ"
                bool ob_rz_absorb = (z1.z_type == "OB" and z2.z_type == "RZ") or (z1.z_type == "RZ" and z2.z_type == "OB")
                // V279: New zone types can merge with similar types
                bool imb_compat = z1.z_type == "IMB" and z2.z_type == "IMB"
                bool mbr_compat = z1.z_type == "MBR" and z2.z_type == "MBR"
                bool can_merge = same_dir and (bb_compat or ob_compat or rz_compat or ob_rz_absorb or imb_compat or mbr_compat)
                if can_merge
                    bool z2_inside_z1 = z2.top <= z1.top and z2.bot >= z1.bot
                    bool z1_inside_z2 = z1.top <= z2.top and z1.bot >= z2.bot
                    // V250: также объединяем зоны с перекрытием более 70%
                    float ov_h = math.min(z1.top, z2.top)
                    float ov_l = math.max(z1.bot, z2.bot)
                    float ov_sz  = ov_h > ov_l ? ov_h - ov_l : 0.0
                    float min_sz = math.min(z1.top - z1.bot, z2.top - z2.bot)
                    bool high_overlap = min_sz > 0 and (ov_sz / min_sz >= 0.7)
                    bool is_contained = z2_inside_z1 or z1_inside_z2 or high_overlap
                    if is_contained
                        Zone outer_z = z1_inside_z2 ? z2 : z1
                        Zone inner_z = z1_inside_z2 ? z1 : z2
                        Zone master  = outer_z
                        Zone slave   = inner_z

                        float conf_mult  = master.z_type == "BB" ? 0.35 : (ob_rz_absorb ? 0.15 : (slave.z_type == "RZ" ? 0.30 : 0.25))
                        float conf_bonus = slave.score * conf_mult
                        master.score := math.min(master.score + conf_bonus, 150.0)
                        master.absorbed_count := master.absorbed_count + 1
                        master.tier := f_tier(master.score)

                        if master.z_type == "BB"
                            master.sniper_price := (master.top + master.bot) / 2.0

                        string absorb_tag = master.z_type == "BB" ? "🛡️ BB-ABSORBED: " : slave.z_type  == "RZ" ? "🎯 RZ-ABSORBED: " : "🔗 OB-ABSORBED: "
                        master.debug_log := f_safe_append(master.debug_log, "\n" + absorb_tag + "Zone #" + f_ts(slave.origin_idx) + " (+" + str.tostring(conf_bonus, "#.1") + " Score)" + " [now " + str.tostring(master.score, "#.0") + "]")

                        slave.active    := false
                        slave.mitigated := true
                        f_delete_zone_graphics(slave)
                        master.update()

                        if slave.origin_idx == z1.origin_idx
                            break

// ── V250: Разрешение конфликтов между зонами ──────────────────────────────
f_resolve_zone_conflicts() =>
    int sz = array.size(zone_db)
    if sz > 1
        for i = sz - 1 to 0
            Zone zi = array.get(zone_db, i)
            if not zi.active or zi.mitigated
                continue
            for j = i - 1 to 0
                Zone zj = array.get(zone_db, j)
                if not zj.active or zj.mitigated
                    continue
                float ov_h = math.min(zi.top, zj.top)
                float ov_l = math.max(zi.bot, zj.bot)
                if ov_h <= ov_l
                    continue
                // BB vs OB противоположного направления: BB имеет приоритет, OB удаляется
                bool opposite_dir = zi.is_bull != zj.is_bull
                bool bb_ob_conflict = opposite_dir and
                                      ((zi.z_type == "BB" and zj.z_type == "OB") or
                                       (zj.z_type == "BB" and zi.z_type == "OB"))
                if bb_ob_conflict
                    Zone ob_z  = zi.z_type == "OB" ? zi : zj
                    ob_z.active    := false
                    ob_z.mitigated := true
                    f_delete_zone_graphics(ob_z)
                    continue
                // FVG+OB того же направления: добавить 30% score FVG зоны к OB зоне
                bool same_dir = zi.is_bull == zj.is_bull
                if same_dir and zi.z_type == "OB" and zj.z_type == "OB"
                    bool zi_has_fvg = zi.fvg_type != "None" and zi.fvg_type != ""
                    bool zj_has_fvg = zj.fvg_type != "None" and zj.fvg_type != ""
                    if zi_has_fvg and not zj_has_fvg
                        zj.score := math.min(zj.score + zi.score * 0.3, 150.0)
                        zj.tier := f_tier(zj.score)
                    else if zj_has_fvg and not zi_has_fvg
                        zi.score := math.min(zi.score + zj.score * 0.3, 150.0)
                        zi.tier := f_tier(zi.score)
        // Очищаем неактивные зоны после разрешения конфликтов
        for i = array.size(zone_db) - 1 to 0
            Zone z = array.get(zone_db, i)
            if not z.active and z.mitigated
                array.remove(zone_db, i)

// V278: Pre-GC zone counts — computed before garbage collection for accurate dashboard display
// Wrapped in single-element arrays to allow modification inside f_limit_visible_zones() (Pine v6 rule)
var array<int> _pre_gc_cnt_sup = array.from(0)
var array<int> _pre_gc_cnt_res = array.from(0)
var array<int> _pre_gc_cnt_bb  = array.from(0)
var array<int> _pre_gc_cnt_rz  = array.from(0)

f_limit_visible_zones() =>
    if array.size(zone_db) > 0
        array<Zone> candidates = array.new<Zone>()
        for z in zone_db
            if z.active
                array.push(candidates, z)

        // V278: Count ALL active zones by type BEFORE garbage collection
        array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_sup, 0, 0)
        array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_res, 0, 0)
        array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_bb,  0, 0)
        array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_rz,  0, 0)
        for z in candidates
            if z.z_type == "BB"
                array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_bb,  0, array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_bb,  0) + 1)
            else if z.z_type == "RZ"
                array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_rz,  0, array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_rz,  0) + 1)
            else if z.is_bull
                array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_sup, 0, array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_sup, 0) + 1)
            else
                array.set(_pre_gc_cnt_res, 0, array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_res, 0) + 1)

        if array.size(candidates) > 0
            float[] scores  = array.new_float()
            for z in candidates
                array.push(scores, z.score)
            int[] sorted_indices = array.sort_indices(scores, order.descending)
            array<Zone> to_keep  = array.new<Zone>()

            // V278: Dynamic SAFE_MAX — accounts for actual drawing element usage per zone
            // TradingView hard limits: max_boxes_count=500, max_lines_count=500, max_labels_count=500
            // Each zone uses: 1 box (body) + optional FVG box + grid lines/labels + visual effects
            int _reserved   = 10  // Reserve slots for Previous Day (PD) band lines/boxes (3 lines + 2 boxes) + misc
            int _avail      = 500 - _reserved
            int _boxes_pz   = show_fvg ? 2 : 1
            int _lines_pz   = (use_fib_grid ? 8 : 0) + (use_glow_best ? 2 : 0) + (use_health_bar ? 1 : 0) + (use_fvg_connector ? 1 : 0) + 1  // V282: +1 for side_stripe (V281)
            int _labels_pz  = (use_fib_grid ? 7 : 0) + (show_sniper ? 1 : 0) + (use_bb_arrow ? 1 : 0)
            int _lim_box    = _boxes_pz  > 0 ? math.floor(_avail / _boxes_pz)  : _avail
            int _lim_line   = _lines_pz  > 0 ? math.floor(_avail / _lines_pz)  : _avail
            int _lim_label  = _labels_pz > 0 ? math.floor(_avail / _labels_pz) : _avail
            int SAFE_MAX    = math.max(math.min(_lim_box, _lim_line, _lim_label), 3)  // min 3: ensures at least 1 bull + 1 bear + 1 BB zone
            int final_limit = math.min(max_visible_zones, SAFE_MAX)

            if final_limit == 1
                Zone best_bull = na
                Zone best_bear = na
                Zone best_bb   = na
                float max_bull_score = -1.0
                float max_bear_score = -1.0
                float max_bb_score   = -1.0
                for idx = 0 to array.size(sorted_indices) - 1
                    int k = array.get(sorted_indices, idx)
                    Zone z = array.get(candidates, k)
                    if z.z_type == "BB" and max_bb_score == -1.0
                        best_bb := z
                        max_bb_score := z.score
                    else if z.is_bull and max_bull_score == -1.0
                        best_bull := z
                        max_bull_score := z.score
                    else if not z.is_bull and max_bear_score == -1.0
                        best_bear := z
                        max_bear_score := z.score
                if not na(best_bull)
                    array.push(to_keep, best_bull)
                if not na(best_bear)
                    array.push(to_keep, best_bear)
                if not na(best_bb)
                    array.push(to_keep, best_bb)
            else
                int lim = math.min(final_limit, array.size(candidates))
                for idx = 0 to lim - 1
                    int best_idx = array.get(sorted_indices, idx)
                    array.push(to_keep, array.get(candidates, best_idx))

            f_garbage_collection(to_keep)

// V260: RZ debug log string helper to reduce token count
f_rz_log(bool bull, float wr, float rv, int pc, bool rsp, int cond, float sc) =>
    (bull ? "RZ Bull" : "RZ Bear") + " | Wick:" + str.tostring(wr,"#.2") + "ATR | RVOL:" + str.tostring(rv,"#.2") + " | PinBars:" + f_ts(pc) + " | RSpike:" + (rsp ? "✓" : "✗") + " | Patterns:" + f_ts(cond) + " | Score:" + str.tostring(sc,"#.0")

// V260: RZ pin bar count helper — scans lookback candles and counts pin bars
f_rz_pin_scan(int rz_safe, bool is_bull) =>
    int count = 0
    int scan = math.min(inp_pinbar_lookback, MAX_OFFSET - rz_safe)
    for pi = 0 to math.max(scan - 1, 0)
        int ps = f_clamp(rz_safe + pi, MAX_OFFSET)
        float pcr = high[ps] - low[ps]
        float pbd = math.abs(close[ps] - open[ps])
        if pcr > 0 and pbd > 0
            float pw = is_bull ? (math.min(close[ps], open[ps]) - low[ps]) : (high[ps] - math.max(close[ps], open[ps]))
            if pw > pbd * inp_pin_ratio
                count += 1
    count

// V260: RZ reverse spike detection helper
f_rz_rspike_scan(int rz_safe, bool is_bull, float mem_rvol) =>
    bool found = false
    int scan = math.min(inp_rspike_lookfwd, rz_safe)
    for ri = 1 to math.max(scan, 1)
        int rs = f_clamp(rz_safe - ri, MAX_OFFSET)
        if rs >= 0
            float rrv = nz(mem_rvol[rs], 1.0)
            float rbd = math.abs(close[rs] - open[rs])
            float rrng = high[rs] - low[rs]
            bool rdir = is_bull ? (close[rs] > open[rs]) : (close[rs] < open[rs])
            if rdir and rrng > 0 and (rbd >= rrng * 0.5) and (rrv >= inp_rspike_rvol)
                found := true
                break
    found

// ── Вспомогательная функция создания новой Zone (V249: единая точка создания) ──
f_make_zone(int origin, float t, float b, bool bull, string ztype, float sc, string tier, float idm, float sniper, box main_bx, box fvg_bx, string fvg_tp, string dlog, string pat_info) =>
    label l_sn = na
    if show_sniper and not na(sniper)
        l_sn := label.new(bar_index + 5, sniper, text="🎯 " + f_mt(sniper),
             color=C_BLACK100, textcolor=color.new(color.white, 0),
             style=label.style_label_left, size=size.small)
    Zone n = Zone.new(
        gfx=main_bx, fvg_gfx=fvg_bx, grid_lines=array.new<line>(), grid_labels=array.new<label>(),
        fvg_lines=array.new<line>(), fvg_labels=array.new<label>(),
        top=t, bot=b, is_bull=bull, z_type=ztype, active=true,
        created_at=bar_index, origin_idx=origin, mitigated=false,
        score=sc, tier=tier, idm_lvl=idm, idm_swept=(ztype == "RZ"),
        sniper_price=sniper, sn_lbl=l_sn, debug_lbl=na, sniper_stage=0,
        chop_count=0, pending_break=false, debug_log=dlog, debug_shown=false,
        fvg_type=fvg_tp, fvg_break_count=0, fvg_was_penetrated=false, absorbed_count=0, bb_break_count=0,
        patterns_info=pat_info,
        glow_line_top=na, glow_line_bot=na, health_line=na,
        bb_arrow_lbl=na, fvg_connector=na, rz_zigzag_lines=array.new<line>(),
        refined_top=na, refined_bot=na, is_propulsion=false, is_mitigation=false,
        mb_stage=0, bb_age_bars=0.0, bb_cascade_count=0, fvg_fill_pct=0.0,
        fvg_ce_level=na, kill_zone_bonus=0.0, confluence_bonus=0.0, decay_factor=1.0,
        regime_at_creation=0, inst_footprint=0.0,
        initial_score=sc, retest_count=0,
        side_stripe=na)
    n

f_create_new_zones() =>
    // V250: локальные series-ссылки с max_bars_back для безопасного доступа к истории
    float _mem_atr  = atr_val
    float _mem_rvol = rvol
    float _mem_rsi  = rsi_val
    var float _sf_mu   = na
    var float _sf_sig  = na
    var float _sf_eta  = na
    var float _sf_prob = 0.0
    var int   _sf_n    = 0
    // V273-fix: guard against duplicate zone creation on same pivot bar
    var int _last_created_bull_idx = -1
    var int _last_created_bear_idx = -1
    max_bars_back(_mem_atr,  MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_rvol, MAX_BUFF)
    max_bars_back(_mem_rsi,  MAX_BUFF)
    // V273-fix: pre-compute ta-dependent functions outside conditionals for per-bar consistency
    bool _pre_absorption = f_detect_absorption()
    bool _pre_squeeze    = f_keltner_squeeze(20)
    // V273-fix: pre-compute f_rz_rspike_scan outside conditionals for per-bar consistency
    int _pre_rz_off_b  = not na(last_sl_i) ? (bar_index - last_sl_i) : 0
    int _pre_rz_safe_b = f_clamp(_pre_rz_off_b, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool _pre_rspike_b = f_rz_rspike_scan(_pre_rz_safe_b, true, _mem_rvol)
    int _pre_rz_off_s  = not na(last_sh_i) ? (bar_index - last_sh_i) : 0
    int _pre_rz_safe_s = f_clamp(_pre_rz_off_s, MAX_OFFSET)
    bool _pre_rspike_s = f_rz_rspike_scan(_pre_rz_safe_s, false, _mem_rvol)
    // V279-fix: pre-compute ta-dependent zone detectors outside conditionals for per-bar consistency
    [_pre_acc_range, _pre_is_acc, _pre_is_dist, _pre_acc_h, _pre_acc_l, _pre_acc_score] = f_detect_accumulation_distribution()
    [_pre_vcp_valid, _pre_vcp_score, _pre_vcp_h, _pre_vcp_l, _pre_vcp_squeeze] = f_detect_vcp_zone()
    [_pre_mbr_b_valid, _pre_mbr_b_count, _pre_mbr_b_score, _pre_mbr_b_level] = f_detect_multi_bar_rejection(true, 8)
    [_pre_mbr_s_valid, _pre_mbr_s_count, _pre_mbr_s_score, _pre_mbr_s_level] = f_detect_multi_bar_rejection(false, 8)
    
    bool allow        = (not use_adx or not global_flat)
    bool confirmed_bar = barstate.isconfirmed
    float discount = 0.0
    if _sf_n >= stoch_min_val and _sf_prob > 80.0
        discount := math.min(0.25, (_sf_prob - 80.0) / 20.0 * 0.25)

    float dyn_z_min   = p_z_min * (1.0 - discount)
    float dyn_vol_min = p_vol_min * (1.0 - discount)
    float tick_fvg_limit = f_safe_div(syminfo.mintick * 0.5, math.max(atr_val, syminfo.mintick))
    float smart_fvg_base = math.min(p_fvg_min, tick_fvg_limit)
    float dyn_fvg_min    = smart_fvg_base * (1.0 - discount)
    // V273: Volatility-adjusted FVG threshold — increase minimum on high volatility
    // 1.5× threshold: vol_ratio_c > 1.5 means ATR is 50%+ above slow ATR (elevated regime)
    // 1.3× multiplier: raises FVG minimum by 30% to filter noise in volatile conditions
    if nz(vol_ratio_c, 1.0) > 1.5
        dyn_fvg_min := dyn_fvg_min * 1.3

    bool active_bull_fvg_lock = false
    bool active_bear_fvg_lock = false
    if req_fvg_seq and confirmed_bar
        if array.size(zone_db) > 0
            for z in zone_db
                if z.active and not na(z.fvg_gfx)
                    float f_top = box.get_top(z.fvg_gfx)
                    float f_bot = box.get_bottom(z.fvg_gfx)
                    if z.is_bull  and last_sl <= f_top and last_sl >= f_bot
                        active_bull_fvg_lock := true
                    if not z.is_bull and last_sh <= f_top and last_sh >= f_bot
                        active_bear_fvg_lock := true

    // ── Bull (Support) ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    bool hist_ok_b = not na(last_sl_i) and (bar_index - last_sl_i < p_max_history)
    int  safe_sl_i = nz(last_sl_i)
    PivotMetrics pm_b = f_analyze_pivot_quality(safe_sl_i, true, p_pivot_left, p_pivot_right, hist_ok_b and confirmed_bar)
    bool smart_ok_b   = na(pm_b) or pm_b.is_valid

    string fail_b = ""
    if confirmed_bar and in_window
        if not allow
            fail_b += "[ADX Flat] "
        else if not hist_ok_b
            fail_b += "[Лимит Истории] "
        else if not smart_ok_b and not na(pm_b)
            fail_b += "[Pivot Qual: " + str.tostring(pm_b.strength, "#.1") + " < " + f_ts(min_piv_qual) + "] "
        else if active_bull_fvg_lock
            fail_b += "[Pivot Inside Unfilled FVG] "

    bool  do_b = confirmed_bar and in_window and allow and hist_ok_b and smart_ok_b and not active_bull_fvg_lock
    int   offset_b = not na(last_sl_i) ? (bar_index - last_sl_i) : 0
    // V249: clamp
    int safe_off_b = f_clamp(offset_b, MAX_OFFSET)
    float atr_at_creation_b = (safe_off_b > 0 and safe_off_b <= MAX_OFFSET) ? nz(_mem_atr[safe_off_b], atr_val) : atr_val

    [t_b, b_b, f_b, bx_b, s_b, tier_b, sn_b, idm_b, log_b, fvg_type_b, pat_b] = f_cluster(last_sl_i, true, do_b, p_ob_len, atr_at_creation_b, fail_b, dyn_z_min, dyn_vol_min, dyn_fvg_min)

    // V250: бонус от соседних пивотов → поддержка усиливается кластером лоу
    float nb_bonus_b = 0.0
    if f_b and not na(pm_b) and pm_b.neighbor_count >= 1
        nb_bonus_b := math.min(25.0, pm_b.neighbor_strength * 10.0)
        s_b := math.min(s_b + nb_bonus_b, 150.0)
        if s_b >= 80
            tier_b := f_tier(s_b)

    if f_b
        bool dup = false
        // V273-fix: fast guard against same-bar duplicate creation
        if not na(last_sl_i) and last_sl_i == _last_created_bull_idx
            dup := true
        if not dup and array.size(zone_db) > 0
            for z in zone_db
                if z.origin_idx == last_sl_i
                    dup := true
        if not dup
            string full_log = log_b
            if not na(pm_b) and use_smart_piv
                full_log := f_safe_append(full_log, "\n" + pm_b.debug_info)
            if (bar_index - last_sl_i) < math.min(p_max_history, MAX_BUFF)
                box bx_new = box.new(last_sl_i, t_b, bar_index + 5, b_b,
                     border_color=f_zone_bd(c_sup_base),
                     bgcolor=f_zone_bg(c_sup_base, f_score_to_transp(s_b)),
                     xloc=xloc.bar_index)
                Zone n = f_make_zone(last_sl_i, t_b, b_b, true, "OB", s_b, tier_b, idm_b, sn_b, bx_new, bx_b, fvg_type_b, full_log, pat_b)
                // V270: Kill Zone timing bonus
                bool active_session = kz_london or kz_ny or kz_overlap
                if active_session
                    n.kill_zone_bonus := 10.0
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 10.0, 150.0)
                else if kz_asia
                    n.kill_zone_bonus := -5.0
                    n.score := math.max(10.0, n.score - 5.0)
                n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: BOS/CHoCH bonus
                if (n.is_bull and bos_bull) or (not n.is_bull and bos_bear)
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + bos_zone_bonus, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                if (n.is_bull and choch_bull) or (not n.is_bull and choch_bear)
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + choch_zone_bonus, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Institutional footprint check
                float inst_vol = nz(rvol, 1.0)
                float inst_body_ratio = atr_val > 0 ? f_safe_div(math.abs(close - open), high - low) : 0.0
                if inst_vol > 2.0 and inst_body_ratio > 0.7
                    n.inst_footprint := 15.0
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 15.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Propulsion Block: OB + FVG on same candle
                if fvg_type_b != "None" and fvg_type_b != ""
                    n.is_propulsion := true
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 20.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Confluence Score (Fibonacci/VWAP/round/prev day levels)
                float zone_mid_b = (t_b + b_b) / 2.0
                float conf_score_b = f_calc_confluence_score(zone_mid_b, last_sh, last_sl, vwap_val, prev_day_high, prev_day_low, prev_day_close)
                if conf_score_b > 0
                    n.confluence_bonus := conf_score_b
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + conf_score_b, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Absorption bonus (institutional absorption near zone)
                if _pre_absorption
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 10.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Keltner squeeze bonus (momentum building)
                if _pre_squeeze
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 8.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Regime at creation
                n.regime_at_creation := _regime_type
                array.push(zone_db, n)
                _last_created_bull_idx := last_sl_i
                int last_orig_b = array.get(global_origin_state, 0)
                if not na(last_orig_b)
                    int delta = last_sl_i - last_orig_b
                    if delta > 0 and delta < p_max_history
                        array.push(zone_deltas, delta)
                        if array.size(zone_deltas) > 50
                            array.shift(zone_deltas)
                        // V269: Record RVOL at zone creation for bivariate model
                        array.push(zone_vol_deltas, nz(rvol, 1.0))
                        if array.size(zone_vol_deltas) > 50
                            array.shift(zone_vol_deltas)
                array.set(global_origin_state, 0, last_sl_i)

    // ── Bear (Resistance) ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    bool hist_ok_s = not na(last_sh_i) and (bar_index - last_sh_i < p_max_history)
    int  safe_sh_i = nz(last_sh_i)
    PivotMetrics pm_s = f_analyze_pivot_quality(safe_sh_i, false, p_pivot_left_res, p_pivot_right_res, hist_ok_s and confirmed_bar)
    bool smart_ok_s   = na(pm_s) or pm_s.is_valid

    string fail_s = ""
    if confirmed_bar and in_window
        if not allow
            fail_s += "[ADX Flat] "
        else if not hist_ok_s
            fail_s += "[Лимит Истории] "
        else if not smart_ok_s and not na(pm_s)
            fail_s += "[Pivot Qual: " + str.tostring(pm_s.strength, "#.1") + " < " + f_ts(min_piv_qual) + "] "
        else if active_bear_fvg_lock
            fail_s += "[Pivot Inside Unfilled FVG] "

    bool  do_s = confirmed_bar and in_window and allow and hist_ok_s and smart_ok_s and not active_bear_fvg_lock
    int   offset_s = not na(last_sh_i) ? (bar_index - last_sh_i) : 0
    // V250: clamp (аналогично bull-стороне)
    int   safe_off_s = f_clamp(offset_s, MAX_OFFSET)
    float atr_at_creation_s = (safe_off_s > 0 and safe_off_s <= MAX_OFFSET) ? nz(_mem_atr[safe_off_s], atr_val) : atr_val

    [t_s, b_s, f_s, bx_s, s_s, tier_s, sn_s, idm_s, log_s, fvg_type_s, pat_s] = f_cluster(last_sh_i, false, do_s, p_ob_len_res, atr_at_creation_s, fail_s, dyn_z_min, dyn_vol_min, dyn_fvg_min)

    // V250: бонус от соседних пивотов → сопротивление усиливается кластером хаёв
    float nb_bonus_s = 0.0
    if f_s and not na(pm_s) and pm_s.neighbor_count >= 1
        nb_bonus_s := math.min(25.0, pm_s.neighbor_strength * 10.0)
        s_s := math.min(s_s + nb_bonus_s, 150.0)
        if s_s >= 80
            tier_s := f_tier(s_s)

    if f_s
        bool dup = false
        // V273-fix: fast guard against same-bar duplicate creation
        if not na(last_sh_i) and last_sh_i == _last_created_bear_idx
            dup := true
        if not dup and array.size(zone_db) > 0
            for z in zone_db
                if z.origin_idx == last_sh_i
                    dup := true
        if not dup
            string full_log = log_s
            if not na(pm_s) and use_smart_piv
                full_log := f_safe_append(full_log, "\n" + pm_s.debug_info)
            if (bar_index - last_sh_i) < math.min(p_max_history, MAX_BUFF)
                box bx_new = box.new(last_sh_i, t_s, bar_index + 5, b_s,
                     border_color=f_zone_bd(c_res_base),
                     bgcolor=f_zone_bg(c_res_base, f_score_to_transp(s_s)),
                     xloc=xloc.bar_index)
                Zone n = f_make_zone(last_sh_i, t_s, b_s, false, "OB", s_s, tier_s, idm_s, sn_s, bx_new, bx_s, fvg_type_s, full_log, pat_s)
                // V270: Kill Zone timing bonus
                bool active_session_s = kz_london or kz_ny or kz_overlap
                if active_session_s
                    n.kill_zone_bonus := 10.0
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 10.0, 150.0)
                else if kz_asia
                    n.kill_zone_bonus := -5.0
                    n.score := math.max(10.0, n.score - 5.0)
                n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: BOS/CHoCH bonus
                if (n.is_bull and bos_bull) or (not n.is_bull and bos_bear)
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + bos_zone_bonus, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                if (n.is_bull and choch_bull) or (not n.is_bull and choch_bear)
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + choch_zone_bonus, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Institutional footprint check
                float inst_vol_s = nz(rvol, 1.0)
                float inst_body_ratio_s = atr_val > 0 ? f_safe_div(math.abs(close - open), high - low) : 0.0
                if inst_vol_s > 2.0 and inst_body_ratio_s > 0.7
                    n.inst_footprint := 15.0
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 15.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Propulsion Block: OB + FVG on same candle
                if fvg_type_s != "None" and fvg_type_s != ""
                    n.is_propulsion := true
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 20.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Confluence Score (Fibonacci/VWAP/round/prev day levels)
                float zone_mid_s = (t_s + b_s) / 2.0
                float conf_score_s = f_calc_confluence_score(zone_mid_s, last_sh, last_sl, vwap_val, prev_day_high, prev_day_low, prev_day_close)
                if conf_score_s > 0
                    n.confluence_bonus := conf_score_s
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + conf_score_s, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Absorption bonus (institutional absorption near zone)
                if _pre_absorption
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 10.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V273: Keltner squeeze bonus (momentum building)
                if _pre_squeeze
                    n.score := math.min(n.score + 8.0, 150.0)
                    n.tier := f_tier(n.score)
                // V270: Regime at creation
                n.regime_at_creation := _regime_type
                array.push(zone_db, n)
                _last_created_bear_idx := last_sh_i
                int last_orig_s = array.get(global_origin_state, 0)
                if not na(last_orig_s)
                    int delta = last_sh_i - last_orig_s
                    if delta > 0 and delta < p_max_history
                        array.push(zone_deltas, delta)
                        if array.size(zone_deltas) > 50
                            array.shift(zone_deltas)
                        // V269: Record RVOL at zone creation for bivariate model
                        array.push(zone_vol_deltas, nz(rvol, 1.0))
                        if array.size(zone_vol_deltas) > 50
                            array.shift(zone_vol_deltas)
                array.set(global_origin_state, 0, last_sh_i)

    // ── Создание Rejection Zones (RZ) ────────────────────────────────────
    // RZ Bull: сильный нижний хвост на пивотном лоу → зона = [wick_low, body_low]
    // RZ Bear: сильный верхний хвост на пивотном хае → зона = [body_high, wick_high]
    // RZ НЕ является Order Block — это чисто wick-rejection зона.
    if use_rz
        // ── Bull RZ (от пивота лоу) ──────────────────────────────────────
        bool rz_hist_b = not na(last_sl_i) and (bar_index - last_sl_i < p_max_history)
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and rz_hist_b
            int rz_off_b = bar_index - last_sl_i
            // V250: clamp для безопасного доступа к истории
            int rz_safe_b = f_clamp(rz_off_b, MAX_OFFSET)
            bool rz_off_safe = rz_off_b >= 0 and rz_off_b <= math.min(p_max_history - 2, MAX_OFFSET)
            if rz_off_safe
                float rz_o     = open[rz_safe_b]
                float rz_c     = close[rz_safe_b]
                float rz_l     = low[rz_safe_b]
                float body_bot = math.min(rz_o, rz_c)
                float wick_len = body_bot - rz_l
                float body_len = math.abs(rz_c - rz_o)
                float safe_body = math.max(body_len, syminfo.mintick)
                // Условие: значительный нижний хвост (inp_rz_wick_mult × тело)
                // И хвост > 0.3 × ATR
                float rz_atr = nz(_mem_atr[rz_safe_b], atr_val)
                bool rz_wick_ok = (wick_len >= safe_body * inp_rz_wick_mult) and (wick_len >= rz_atr * 0.3)
                bool rz_dup    = false
                if array.size(zone_db) > 0
                    for z in zone_db
                        if z.z_type == "RZ" and z.is_bull and z.origin_idx == last_sl_i
                            rz_dup := true
                if rz_wick_ok and not rz_dup
                    // Score RZ Bull = wick_ratio × RSI bonus × vol bonus
                    float rz_wick_ratio = wick_len / rz_atr
                    float rz_score = math.min(80.0, rz_wick_ratio * 20.0)
                    float rz_rvol = nz(_mem_rvol[rz_safe_b], 1.0)
                    if rz_rvol > p_mom_rvol
                        rz_score += math.min(20.0, (rz_rvol - 1.0) * 10.0)
                    float rz_rsi = nz(_mem_rsi[rz_safe_b], 50.0)
                    if rz_rsi < inp_rsi_os
                        rz_score += 15.0
                    // V250: бонус от соседних пивотов для RZ Bull
                    if not na(pm_b) and pm_b.neighbor_count >= 1
                        rz_score += math.min(15.0, pm_b.neighbor_strength * 7.0)
                    int rz_pin_count_b = f_rz_pin_scan(rz_safe_b, true)
                    if rz_pin_count_b >= inp_min_pinbars
                        rz_score += math.min(15.0, float(rz_pin_count_b) * 5.0)
                    bool rz_rspike_b = _pre_rspike_b
                    if rz_rspike_b
                        rz_score += 10.0
                    // V260: Unified pattern counting, naming & scoring via helper
                    [rz_b_cond, rz_b_pat_str, _tmp_rz_score] = f_count_score_patterns(f_is_ppr(last_sl_i, true), rz_pin_count_b >= 1, f_is_engulfing(last_sl_i, true), f_is_doji(last_sl_i), f_is_hammer(last_sl_i, true), f_is_inverted_hammer(last_sl_i, true), f_is_morning_star(last_sl_i), f_is_harami(last_sl_i, true), rz_rspike_b, true, rz_score)
                    rz_score := _tmp_rz_score
                    // V270: Adaptive RZ threshold — longer wick = lower threshold
                    float rz_adapt_thresh = float(p_min_score) * (0.4 + 0.2 * f_safe_div(rz_wick_ratio, 1.0))
                    // V279: Sigmoid wick ratio scoring (replaces quadratic)
                    // Smooth saturation at ~30 for wick_ratio > 3, hard cap 35
                    float wick_sig_bonus = 30.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-3.0 * (rz_wick_ratio - 2.0)))
                    rz_score += math.min(35.0, wick_sig_bonus)
                    // V273: RSI divergence bonus for RZ Bull
                    float _rz_rsi_prev_b = nz(_mem_rsi[f_clamp(rz_safe_b + 5, MAX_OFFSET)], 50.0)
                    float _rz_price_prev_b = nz(low[f_clamp(rz_safe_b + 5, MAX_OFFSET)], low)
                    [_rz_div_b, _rz_div_bonus_b] = f_rsi_divergence_rz(true, rz_rsi, _rz_rsi_prev_b, rz_l, _rz_price_prev_b)
                    if _rz_div_b
                        rz_score += _rz_div_bonus_b
                    // V273: Hidden rejection bonus for RZ Bull
                    [_hr_found_b, _hr_level_b] = f_detect_hidden_rejection(true, 8)
                    if _hr_found_b and not na(_hr_level_b) and math.abs(_hr_level_b - rz_l) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.2
                        rz_score += 12.0
                    rz_score := math.min(rz_score, 150.0)
                    if use_score and rz_score < rz_adapt_thresh
                        rz_score := -1.0  // marker to skip
                    if rz_score >= 0.0
                        float rz_top = body_bot
                        float rz_bot = rz_l
                        if (rz_top - rz_bot) >= syminfo.mintick * 2 and (bar_index - last_sl_i) < math.min(p_max_history, MAX_BUFF)
                            string rz_tier = f_tier(rz_score)
                            box bx_rz = box.new(last_sl_i, rz_top, bar_index + 5, rz_bot,
                                 border_color = color.new(c_rz_bull, 0),
                                 bgcolor      = f_zone_bg(c_rz_bull, f_score_to_transp(rz_score)),
                                 border_style = line.style_dotted,
                                 xloc         = xloc.bar_index)
                            Zone rz_n = f_make_zone(last_sl_i, rz_top, rz_bot, true, "RZ", rz_score, rz_tier, na, (rz_top + rz_bot) / 2.0, bx_rz, na, "None", f_rz_log(true, rz_wick_ratio, rz_rvol, rz_pin_count_b, rz_rspike_b, rz_b_cond, rz_score), rz_b_pat_str)
                            array.push(zone_db, rz_n)

        // ── Bear RZ (от пивота хай) ──────────────────────────────────────
        bool rz_hist_s = not na(last_sh_i) and (bar_index - last_sh_i < p_max_history)
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and rz_hist_s
            int rz_off_s = bar_index - last_sh_i
            // V250: clamp для безопасного доступа к истории
            int rz_safe_s = f_clamp(rz_off_s, MAX_OFFSET)
            bool rz_off_safe_s = rz_off_s >= 0 and rz_off_s <= math.min(p_max_history - 2, MAX_OFFSET)
            if rz_off_safe_s
                float rz_o_s   = open[rz_safe_s]
                float rz_c_s   = close[rz_safe_s]
                float rz_h_s   = high[rz_safe_s]
                float body_top_s = math.max(rz_o_s, rz_c_s)
                float wick_len_s = rz_h_s - body_top_s
                float body_len_s = math.abs(rz_c_s - rz_o_s)
                float safe_body_s = math.max(body_len_s, syminfo.mintick)
                float rz_atr_s = nz(_mem_atr[rz_safe_s], atr_val)
                bool rz_wick_ok_s = (wick_len_s >= safe_body_s * inp_rz_wick_mult) and (wick_len_s >= rz_atr_s * 0.3)
                bool rz_dup_s   = false
                if array.size(zone_db) > 0
                    for z in zone_db
                        if z.z_type == "RZ" and not z.is_bull and z.origin_idx == last_sh_i
                            rz_dup_s := true
                if rz_wick_ok_s and not rz_dup_s
                    float rz_wick_ratio_s = wick_len_s / rz_atr_s
                    float rz_score_s = math.min(80.0, rz_wick_ratio_s * 20.0)
                    float rz_rvol_s = nz(_mem_rvol[rz_safe_s], 1.0)
                    if rz_rvol_s > p_mom_rvol
                        rz_score_s += math.min(20.0, (rz_rvol_s - 1.0) * 10.0)
                    float rz_rsi_s = nz(_mem_rsi[rz_safe_s], 50.0)
                    if rz_rsi_s > inp_rsi_ob
                        rz_score_s += 15.0
                    // V250: бонус от соседних пивотов для RZ Bear
                    if not na(pm_s) and pm_s.neighbor_count >= 1
                        rz_score_s += math.min(15.0, pm_s.neighbor_strength * 7.0)
                    int rz_pin_count_s = f_rz_pin_scan(rz_safe_s, false)
                    if rz_pin_count_s >= inp_min_pinbars
                        rz_score_s += math.min(15.0, float(rz_pin_count_s) * 5.0)
                    bool rz_rspike_s = _pre_rspike_s
                    if rz_rspike_s
                        rz_score_s += 10.0
                    // V260: Unified pattern counting, naming & scoring via helper
                    [rz_s_cond, rz_s_pat_str, _tmp_rz_score_s] = f_count_score_patterns(f_is_ppr(last_sh_i, false), rz_pin_count_s >= 1, f_is_engulfing(last_sh_i, false), f_is_doji(last_sh_i), f_is_hammer(last_sh_i, false), f_is_inverted_hammer(last_sh_i, false), f_is_evening_star(last_sh_i), f_is_harami(last_sh_i, false), rz_rspike_s, false, rz_score_s)
                    rz_score_s := _tmp_rz_score_s
                    // V270: Adaptive RZ threshold — longer wick = lower threshold
                    float rz_adapt_thresh_s = float(p_min_score) * (0.4 + 0.2 * f_safe_div(rz_wick_ratio_s, 1.0))
                    // V279: Sigmoid wick ratio scoring (replaces quadratic)
                    float wick_sig_bonus_s = 30.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-3.0 * (rz_wick_ratio_s - 2.0)))
                    rz_score_s += math.min(35.0, wick_sig_bonus_s)
                    // V273: RSI divergence bonus for RZ Bear
                    float _rz_rsi_prev_s = nz(_mem_rsi[f_clamp(rz_safe_s + 5, MAX_OFFSET)], 50.0)
                    float _rz_price_prev_s = nz(high[f_clamp(rz_safe_s + 5, MAX_OFFSET)], high)
                    [_rz_div_s, _rz_div_bonus_s] = f_rsi_divergence_rz(false, rz_rsi_s, _rz_rsi_prev_s, rz_h_s, _rz_price_prev_s)
                    if _rz_div_s
                        rz_score_s += _rz_div_bonus_s
                    // V273: Hidden rejection bonus for RZ Bear
                    [_hr_found_s, _hr_level_s] = f_detect_hidden_rejection(false, 8)
                    if _hr_found_s and not na(_hr_level_s) and math.abs(_hr_level_s - rz_h_s) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.2
                        rz_score_s += 12.0
                    rz_score_s := math.min(rz_score_s, 150.0)
                    if use_score and rz_score_s < rz_adapt_thresh_s
                        rz_score_s := -1.0  // marker to skip
                    if rz_score_s >= 0.0
                        float rz_top_s = rz_h_s
                        float rz_bot_s = body_top_s
                        if (rz_top_s - rz_bot_s) >= syminfo.mintick * 2 and (bar_index - last_sh_i) < math.min(p_max_history, MAX_BUFF)
                            string rz_tier_s = f_tier(rz_score_s)
                            box bx_rz_s = box.new(last_sh_i, rz_top_s, bar_index + 5, rz_bot_s,
                                 border_color = color.new(c_rz_bear, 0),
                                 bgcolor      = f_zone_bg(c_rz_bear, f_score_to_transp(rz_score_s)),
                                 border_style = line.style_dotted,
                                 xloc         = xloc.bar_index)
                            Zone rz_s = f_make_zone(last_sh_i, rz_top_s, rz_bot_s, false, "RZ", rz_score_s, rz_tier_s, na, (rz_top_s + rz_bot_s) / 2.0, bx_rz_s, na, "None", f_rz_log(false, rz_wick_ratio_s, rz_rvol_s, rz_pin_count_s, rz_rspike_s, rz_s_cond, rz_score_s), rz_s_pat_str)
                            array.push(zone_db, rz_s)

        // ── V279: Imbalance Zones ─────────────────────────────────────────
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and use_imb_zones
            [_imb_valid, _imb_bull, _imb_score, _imb_delta] = f_detect_imbalance()
            if _imb_valid and _imb_score >= float(p_min_score) * 0.6
                // Check for duplicates within last 10 bars
                bool imb_dup = false
                for z in zone_db
                    if z.z_type == "IMB" and z.active and (bar_index - z.created_at) < 10
                        imb_dup := true
                if not imb_dup
                    float imb_h = high
                    float imb_l = low
                    string imb_tier = f_tier(_imb_score)
                    color imb_col = c_imb_base
                    box bx_imb = box.new(bar_index, imb_h, bar_index + 5, imb_l,
                         border_color = color.new(imb_col, 0),
                         bgcolor = f_zone_bg(imb_col, f_score_to_transp(_imb_score)),
                         border_style = line.style_dashed,
                         xloc = xloc.bar_index)
                    Zone imb_z = f_make_zone(bar_index, imb_h, imb_l, _imb_bull, "IMB", _imb_score, imb_tier, na, (imb_h + imb_l) / 2.0, bx_imb, na, "None", "IMB Delta=" + str.tostring(_imb_delta, "#.0"), "")
                    array.push(zone_db, imb_z)

        // ── V279: Accumulation/Distribution Zones ─────────────────────────
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and use_acc_zones
            if _pre_acc_range and _pre_acc_score >= float(p_min_score) * 0.5
                bool acc_dup = false
                for z in zone_db
                    if (z.z_type == "ACC" or z.z_type == "DST") and z.active and (bar_index - z.created_at) < inp_acc_min_bars
                        acc_dup := true
                if not acc_dup
                    string acc_type = _pre_is_acc ? "ACC" : "DST"
                    string acc_tier = f_tier(_pre_acc_score)
                    color acc_col = c_acc_base
                    box bx_acc = box.new(bar_index - inp_acc_min_bars, _pre_acc_h, bar_index + 5, _pre_acc_l,
                         border_color = color.new(acc_col, 0),
                         bgcolor = f_zone_bg(acc_col, f_score_to_transp(_pre_acc_score)),
                         border_style = line.style_dotted,
                         xloc = xloc.bar_index)
                    Zone acc_z = f_make_zone(bar_index, _pre_acc_h, _pre_acc_l, _pre_is_acc, acc_type, _pre_acc_score, acc_tier, na, (_pre_acc_h + _pre_acc_l) / 2.0, bx_acc, na, "None", acc_type + " Score=" + str.tostring(_pre_acc_score, "#.0"), "Wyckoff")
                    array.push(zone_db, acc_z)

        // ── V279: VCP Zones ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and use_vcp_zones
            if _pre_vcp_valid and _pre_vcp_score >= float(p_min_score) * 0.5
                bool vcp_dup = false
                for z in zone_db
                    if z.z_type == "VCP" and z.active and (bar_index - z.created_at) < 10
                        vcp_dup := true
                if not vcp_dup
                    string vcp_tier = f_tier(_pre_vcp_score)
                    string vcp_info = _pre_vcp_squeeze ? "Sqz+VCP" : "VCP"
                    box bx_vcp = box.new(bar_index - 10, _pre_vcp_h, bar_index + 5, _pre_vcp_l,
                         border_color = color.new(c_vcp_base, 0),
                         bgcolor = f_zone_bg(c_vcp_base, f_score_to_transp(_pre_vcp_score)),
                         border_style = line.style_dashed,
                         xloc = xloc.bar_index)
                    Zone vcp_z = f_make_zone(bar_index, _pre_vcp_h, _pre_vcp_l, true, "VCP", _pre_vcp_score, vcp_tier, na, (_pre_vcp_h + _pre_vcp_l) / 2.0, bx_vcp, na, "None", vcp_info + " Score=" + str.tostring(_pre_vcp_score, "#.0"), vcp_info)
                    array.push(zone_db, vcp_z)

        // ── V279: Multi-Bar Rejection (enhanced RZ) ──────────────────────
        if confirmed_bar and in_window and use_multi_rej
            // Bull multi-bar rejection
            if _pre_mbr_b_valid and _pre_mbr_b_score >= float(p_min_score) * 0.6
                bool mbr_b_dup = false
                for z in zone_db
                    if z.z_type == "MBR" and z.is_bull and z.active and math.abs(z.bot - _pre_mbr_b_level) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.3
                        mbr_b_dup := true
                if not mbr_b_dup
                    float mbr_b_top = close
                    float mbr_b_bot = _pre_mbr_b_level
                    string mbr_b_tier = f_tier(_pre_mbr_b_score)
                    box bx_mbr_b = box.new(bar_index - 8, mbr_b_top, bar_index + 5, mbr_b_bot,
                         border_color = color.new(c_rz_bull, 30),
                         bgcolor = f_zone_bg(c_rz_bull, f_score_to_transp(_pre_mbr_b_score)),
                         border_style = line.style_dotted,
                         xloc = xloc.bar_index)
                    Zone mbr_b = f_make_zone(bar_index, mbr_b_top, mbr_b_bot, true, "MBR", _pre_mbr_b_score, mbr_b_tier, na, (mbr_b_top + mbr_b_bot) / 2.0, bx_mbr_b, na, "None", "MBR×" + str.tostring(_pre_mbr_b_count), "MultiRej")
                    array.push(zone_db, mbr_b)
            // Bear multi-bar rejection
            if _pre_mbr_s_valid and _pre_mbr_s_score >= float(p_min_score) * 0.6
                bool mbr_s_dup = false
                for z in zone_db
                    if z.z_type == "MBR" and not z.is_bull and z.active and math.abs(z.top - _pre_mbr_s_level) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.3
                        mbr_s_dup := true
                if not mbr_s_dup
                    float mbr_s_top = _pre_mbr_s_level
                    float mbr_s_bot = close
                    string mbr_s_tier = f_tier(_pre_mbr_s_score)
                    box bx_mbr_s = box.new(bar_index - 8, mbr_s_top, bar_index + 5, mbr_s_bot,
                         border_color = color.new(c_rz_bear, 30),
                         bgcolor = f_zone_bg(c_rz_bear, f_score_to_transp(_pre_mbr_s_score)),
                         border_style = line.style_dotted,
                         xloc = xloc.bar_index)
                    Zone mbr_s = f_make_zone(bar_index, mbr_s_top, mbr_s_bot, false, "MBR", _pre_mbr_s_score, mbr_s_tier, na, (mbr_s_top + mbr_s_bot) / 2.0, bx_mbr_s, na, "None", "MBR×" + str.tostring(_pre_mbr_s_count), "MultiRej")
                    array.push(zone_db, mbr_s)

f_mng() =>
    bool is_closed = barstate.isconfirmed
    bool  g_strong_break = true
    float g_prev_low   = nz(low[1])
    float g_prev_high  = nz(high[1])

    if is_closed
        f_remove_old_rejected()

    // V258: pre-compute bb_rspike_bonus unconditionally for series consistency
    // (extracted from trigger_bb to avoid calling f_handle_zone_removal in conditional scope)
    float _bb_rspike_bull = 0.0
    float _bb_rspike_bear = 0.0
    for bbi = 0 to math.min(inp_rspike_lookfwd - 1, MAX_OFFSET)
        int bbs = f_clamp(bbi, MAX_OFFSET)
        float bbrv = nz(rvol[bbs], 1.0)
        float bbrng = high[bbs] - low[bbs]
        float bbbd = math.abs(close[bbs] - open[bbs])
        if bbrng > 0 and (bbbd >= bbrng * 0.5) and (bbrv >= inp_rspike_rvol)
            if _bb_rspike_bull == 0.0 and close[bbs] < open[bbs]
                _bb_rspike_bull := 10.0
            if _bb_rspike_bear == 0.0 and close[bbs] > open[bbs]
                _bb_rspike_bear := 10.0
        if _bb_rspike_bull != 0.0 and _bb_rspike_bear != 0.0
            break

    int _zdb_sz = array.size(zone_db)  // V270: cached size
    if _zdb_sz > 0
        for i = _zdb_sz - 1 to 0
            Zone z = array.get(zone_db, i)
            bool far = false
            bool deep_wick_broke = false
            bool real_breakout = false
            if is_closed
                [dist, _far] = f_calc_zone_validity(z)
                far := _far
                f_update_sfp(z)
                // V270: BB age decay — reduce score by 20% after 100 bars untouched
                if z.z_type == "BB" and (bar_index - z.created_at) > 100 and not z.mitigated
                    z.bb_age_bars := float(bar_index - z.created_at)
                    float age_penalty = math.min(0.2, f_safe_div(z.bb_age_bars - 100.0, 500.0))
                    z.score := math.max(10.0, z.score * (1.0 - age_penalty))
                    z.tier := f_tier(z.score)
                // V270: Mitigation Block — BB retested and held
                if z.z_type == "BB" and z.mb_stage == 0
                    bool bb_retest = z.is_bull ? (low <= z.top and close >= z.bot) : (high >= z.bot and close <= z.top)
                    if bb_retest
                        z.mb_stage := 1  // Retested
                        z.is_mitigation := true
                        z.score := math.min(z.score + 20.0, 150.0)
                        z.tier := f_tier(z.score)
                // V279: Adaptive exponential score decay
                // High-quality zones (initial_score > 100) decay slower
                // Decay rate: 0.001 × (150 / max(initial_score, 50))
                // Minimum floor at 0.05 to prevent full score elimination
                float age_bars = float(bar_index - z.created_at)
                float adaptive_decay_rate = 0.001 * f_safe_div(150.0, math.max(nz(z.initial_score, 50.0), 50.0))
                z.decay_factor := math.max(0.05, math.exp(-adaptive_decay_rate * age_bars))
                // V279: Retest-based age refresh — retested zones stay "fresher"
                // If price touches zone but doesn't break it → retest → reduce effective age
                if z.z_type != "BB"
                    bool zone_touched = z.is_bull ? (low <= z.top and close >= z.bot) : (high >= z.bot and close <= z.top)
                    bool zone_broken  = z.is_bull ? (close < z.bot) : (close > z.top)
                    if zone_touched and not zone_broken and barstate.isconfirmed
                        z.retest_count := nz(z.retest_count, 0) + 1
                        // Reset 30% of age on each retest (diminishing returns)
                        float age_reset_factor = math.max(0.5, 1.0 - 0.3 * math.min(z.retest_count, 3))
                        // V279: Move created_at forward to reduce effective age
                        int new_created_at = int(bar_index - age_bars * age_reset_factor)
                        if new_created_at > z.created_at
                            z.created_at := new_created_at
                // V270: FVG fill tracking
                if not na(z.fvg_gfx) and z.active
                    float fvg_top = box.get_top(z.fvg_gfx)
                    float fvg_bot = box.get_bottom(z.fvg_gfx)
                    float fvg_size = fvg_top - fvg_bot
                    if fvg_size > 0
                        float fill_amt = 0.0
                        if z.is_bull
                            fill_amt := math.max(0, fvg_top - math.max(low, fvg_bot))
                        else
                            fill_amt := math.max(0, math.min(high, fvg_top) - fvg_bot)
                        z.fvg_fill_pct := math.min(1.0, f_safe_div(fill_amt, fvg_size))
                        // V279: Nonlinear quadratic FVG fill penalty
                        // Quadratic growth: 0 at 50% → 25 at 100% fill
                        // More gradual penalty for partially filled FVGs, aggressive for near-complete fills
                        if z.fvg_fill_pct > 0.5
                            float fill_excess = z.fvg_fill_pct - 0.5
                            float penalty = 25.0 * math.pow(fill_excess, 2) / 0.25
                            z.score := math.max(10.0, z.score - penalty)
                        z.tier := f_tier(z.score)
                        // Consequent Encroachment level
                        z.fvg_ce_level := (fvg_top + fvg_bot) / 2.0
                [_real_breakout, _deep_wick_broke] = f_process_critical_changes(z, is_closed, g_prev_low, g_prev_high)
                real_breakout := _real_breakout
                deep_wick_broke := _deep_wick_broke
            else
                if z.active
                    box.set_right(z.gfx, bar_index + 5)
                    if not na(z.fvg_gfx)
                        box.set_right(z.fvg_gfx, bar_index + 3)
                    if not na(z.sn_lbl)
                        label.set_x(z.sn_lbl, bar_index + 5)
            bool was_removed = f_handle_zone_removal(z, is_closed, far, deep_wick_broke, real_breakout, i, g_strong_break, z.is_bull ? _bb_rspike_bull : _bb_rspike_bear)

    if is_closed
        f_merge_nested_zones()
        // V273: RZ Clustering — merge nearby RZ into Strong Rejection Area
        int _rz_sz = array.size(zone_db)
        if _rz_sz > 1
            for i = _rz_sz - 1 to 1
                Zone rz1 = array.get(zone_db, i)
                if not rz1.active or rz1.z_type != "RZ"
                    continue
                for j = i - 1 to 0
                    Zone rz2 = array.get(zone_db, j)
                    if not rz2.active or rz2.z_type != "RZ" or rz1.is_bull != rz2.is_bull
                        continue
                    float rz_dist = math.abs((rz1.top + rz1.bot) / 2.0 - (rz2.top + rz2.bot) / 2.0)
                    if rz_dist < nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.5
                        Zone rz_master = rz1.score >= rz2.score ? rz1 : rz2
                        Zone rz_slave = rz1.score >= rz2.score ? rz2 : rz1
                        rz_master.top := math.max(rz1.top, rz2.top)
                        rz_master.bot := math.min(rz1.bot, rz2.bot)
                        rz_master.score := math.min(rz_master.score + 15.0, 150.0)
                        rz_master.tier := f_tier(rz_master.score)
                        rz_master.absorbed_count += 1
                        rz_slave.active := false
                        rz_slave.mitigated := true
                        f_delete_zone_graphics(rz_slave)
                        box.set_top(rz_master.gfx, rz_master.top)
                        box.set_bottom(rz_master.gfx, rz_master.bot)
                        break
        f_limit_visible_zones()

// V253: stochastic forecast кэш — один вызов на бар
var float _sf_mu   = na
var float _sf_sig  = na
var float _sf_eta  = na
var float _sf_prob = 0.0
var int   _sf_n    = 0
if barstate.isconfirmed
    [_m, _s, _e, _p, _nn] = f_get_stochastic_forecast()
    _sf_mu   := _m
    _sf_sig  := _s
    _sf_eta  := _e
    _sf_prob := _p
    _sf_n    := _nn

// V270: Regime detection (must be computed BEFORE f_mng → f_create_new_zones)
float _trend_angle_pre = ta.sma(close, 10) - ta.sma(close, 50)
float _atr_pct_pre = atr_val > 0 ? f_safe_div(atr_val, close) * 100.0 : 0.0
_regime_type := f_detect_regime(_atr_pct_pre, _trend_angle_pre, nz(vol_ratio_c, 1.0))

f_mng()
f_create_new_zones()
if barstate.isconfirmed
    f_resolve_zone_conflicts()

// ==========================================
// БЛОК 8: EXECUTION & DYNAMIC RISK + DASHBOARD
// ==========================================
bool trigger_buy  = false
bool trigger_sell = false

// V275: Simulated position tracking for indicator mode
var bool  sim_in_position  = false
var int   sim_direction    = 0      // 1 = LONG, -1 = SHORT
var float sim_entry_price  = na
var float sim_sl_price     = na
var float sim_tp1_price    = na
var float sim_tp2_price    = na
var int   sim_entry_bar    = na
var int   sim_trades       = 0
var int   sim_wins         = 0
var float sim_gross_profit = 0.0
var float sim_gross_loss   = 0.0
var float sim_equity       = SIM_INITIAL_CAPITAL

// V275: Export variables for current trade (reset each bar)
float exp_entry_price = sim_in_position ? sim_entry_price : na
float exp_sl_price    = sim_in_position ? sim_sl_price    : na
float exp_tp1_price   = sim_in_position ? sim_tp1_price   : na
float exp_tp2_price   = sim_in_position ? sim_tp2_price   : na
float exp_sim_dir     = sim_in_position ? float(sim_direction) : 0.0

float d_mu   = _sf_mu
float d_sig  = _sf_sig
float d_eta  = _sf_eta
float d_prob = _sf_prob
int   d_n    = _sf_n
float d_discount = 0.0
if d_n >= stoch_min_val and d_prob > 80.0
    d_discount := math.min(0.25, f_safe_div(d_prob - 80.0, 20.0) * 0.25)

// ── V254: Подсчёт пин-баров в окне lookback рядом с зоной ────────────────
// Сканирует последние `lookback` свечей и считает количество пин-баров
// в направлении `is_bull`. Для подтверждения зоны требуется ≥ inp_min_pinbars.
// Математика: Pin-bar = свеча где хвост > body × inp_pin_ratio и противоположный хвост < body.
f_count_pinbars(bool is_bull, int lookback) =>
    int count = 0
    int safe_lb = math.min(lookback, MAX_OFFSET)
    for i = 0 to safe_lb - 1
        int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
        float cr = high[si] - low[si]
        float bd = math.abs(close[si] - open[si])
        float uw = high[si] - math.max(close[si], open[si])
        float lw = math.min(close[si], open[si]) - low[si]
        // V254: Гарантия что тело > 0 (исключаем doji, у которых bd=0)
        if cr > 0 and bd > 0
            if is_bull
                if (lw > bd * inp_pin_ratio) and (uw < bd)
                    count += 1
            else
                if (uw > bd * inp_pin_ratio) and (lw < bd)
                    count += 1
    count

// ── V254: Обнаружение аномального обратного всплеска ──────────────────────
// После формирования пин-баров у зоны ожидаем аномальный ценовой/объёмный
// всплеск В ОБРАТНУЮ СТОРОНУ (т.е. движение ОТ зоны) на следующих барах.
// Это подтверждает реактивность зоны: цена не только остановилась, но и
// агрессивно оттолкнулась. Проверяем: RVOL > порог AND направление свечи.
// Возвращает true если хотя бы одна свеча в окне поиска показала всплеск.
f_reverse_spike(bool is_bull, int lookfwd) =>
    bool found = false
    if not use_reverse_spike
        found := true  // отключено — пропускаем фильтр
    else
        int safe_lf = math.min(lookfwd, MAX_OFFSET)
        for i = 0 to safe_lf - 1
            int si = f_clamp(i, MAX_OFFSET)
            float rv = nz(rvol[si], 1.0)
            float bd = math.abs(close[si] - open[si])
            float rng = high[si] - low[si]
            // Обратный всплеск: для bull-зоны — мощная зелёная свеча (закрытие > открытие)
            //                    для bear-зоны — мощная красная свеча (закрытие < открытие)
            bool dir_ok = is_bull ? (close[si] > open[si]) : (close[si] < open[si])
            // Импульсная свеча: тело ≥ 50% диапазона + аномальный объём
            bool is_impulse = (rng > 0) and (bd >= rng * 0.5) and (rv >= inp_rspike_rvol)
            if dir_ok and is_impulse
                found := true
                break
    found
// ── ИСПРАВЛЕНИЕ: f_qty учитывает syminfo.pointvalue для фьючерсов ─────────
f_qty(float dist) =>
    float min_guard = math.max(syminfo.mintick * 10, atr_val * 0.1)
    float safe_dist = math.max(dist, min_guard)
    // safe_pv = pointvalue для фьючерсов, 1.0 для spot/stock
    float dollar_risk = SIM_INITIAL_CAPITAL * (p_risk / 100.0)
    f_safe_div(dollar_risk, safe_dist * safe_pv)

float auto_pad_mult = 1.0
if rvol > p_mom_rvol
    auto_pad_mult := 1.5
else if htf_adx < 20
    auto_pad_mult := 0.8
// Дополнительный ATR padding для волатильных активов
auto_pad_mult := auto_pad_mult * asset_atr_mult

float stoch_sl_boost = 1.0 + (d_discount * 2.0)
float final_pad_mult = auto_pad_mult * stoch_sl_boost

f_check_clearance(bool is_long_entry, float entry_price, float risk_distance) =>
    bool is_clear = true
    if array.size(zone_db) > 0
        for i = 0 to array.size(zone_db) - 1
            Zone z = array.get(zone_db, i)
            if z.active and z.is_bull != is_long_entry
                float dist_to_wall = na
                if is_long_entry
                    if z.bot > entry_price
                        dist_to_wall := z.bot - entry_price
                else
                    if z.top < entry_price
                        dist_to_wall := entry_price - z.top
                if not na(dist_to_wall) and dist_to_wall < (risk_distance * inp_rr_clear)
                    is_clear := false
                    break
    is_clear

bool is_actionable_bar = entry_mode == "Touch (Limit)" ? true : barstate.isconfirmed

// V255: безусловный вызов f_reverse_spike для серийной согласованности
bool _pre_spike_bull = f_reverse_spike(true, inp_rspike_lookfwd)
bool _pre_spike_bear = f_reverse_spike(false, inp_rspike_lookfwd)

// V275: Simulated position management — exit logic
// Check SL/TP/BOS exits BEFORE entry scan so same-bar re-entry is possible
bool sim_exit_this_bar = false
if sim_in_position
    bool _sim_long  = sim_direction == 1
    bool _sim_short = sim_direction == -1
    float _sim_pnl  = na
    bool _hit_sl  = false
    bool _hit_tp1 = false
    bool _hit_tp2 = false
    bool _hit_bos = false
    // SL check
    if _sim_long  and not na(sim_sl_price) and low <= sim_sl_price
        _hit_sl := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_sl_price - sim_entry_price
    if _sim_short and not na(sim_sl_price) and high >= sim_sl_price
        _hit_sl := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_entry_price - sim_sl_price
    // TP2 check (full exit)
    if not _hit_sl and _sim_long  and not na(sim_tp2_price) and high >= sim_tp2_price
        _hit_tp2 := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_tp2_price - sim_entry_price
    if not _hit_sl and _sim_short and not na(sim_tp2_price) and low <= sim_tp2_price
        _hit_tp2 := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_entry_price - sim_tp2_price
    // TP1 check (partial — for tracking, close fully for simplicity)
    if not _hit_sl and not _hit_tp2 and _sim_long  and not na(sim_tp1_price) and high >= sim_tp1_price
        _hit_tp1 := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_tp1_price - sim_entry_price
    if not _hit_sl and not _hit_tp2 and _sim_short and not na(sim_tp1_price) and low <= sim_tp1_price
        _hit_tp1 := true
        _sim_pnl := sim_entry_price - sim_tp1_price
    // BOS exit (structure break against position)
    if not _hit_sl and not _hit_tp1 and not _hit_tp2
        if _sim_long  and bos_bear
            _hit_bos := true
            _sim_pnl := close - sim_entry_price
        if _sim_short and bos_bull
            _hit_bos := true
            _sim_pnl := sim_entry_price - close
    // Process exit
    if _hit_sl or _hit_tp1 or _hit_tp2 or _hit_bos
        sim_exit_this_bar := true
        sim_trades += 1
        if not na(_sim_pnl) and _sim_pnl > 0
            sim_wins += 1
            sim_gross_profit += _sim_pnl
        else if not na(_sim_pnl) and _sim_pnl < 0
            sim_gross_loss += math.abs(_sim_pnl)
        sim_equity := SIM_INITIAL_CAPITAL + sim_gross_profit - sim_gross_loss
        sim_in_position  := false
        sim_direction    := 0
        sim_entry_price  := na
        sim_sl_price     := na
        sim_tp1_price    := na
        sim_tp2_price    := na
        sim_entry_bar    := na
        // Update export vars after exit (needed immediately: plot() reads these same bar)
        exp_entry_price  := na
        exp_sl_price     := na
        exp_tp1_price    := na
        exp_tp2_price    := na
        exp_sim_dir      := 0.0

if array.size(zone_db) > 0 and is_actionable_bar
    for i = 0 to array.size(zone_db) - 1
        Zone z = array.get(zone_db, i)
        bool is_cooled_down = (bar_index - z.created_at) >= chopcount_int

        if z.active and not z.mitigated and is_cooled_down
            bool _is_bb_rz = z.z_type == "BB" or z.z_type == "RZ"
            bool _zb = z.is_bull
            bool tr_ok  = _zb ? (not use_trend or global_bull) : (not use_trend or global_bear)
            bool pd_ok  = true
            if use_pd
                pd_ok := z.z_type == "BB" ? true : (_zb ? close < pd_mid : close > pd_mid)
            bool rsi_ok = use_rsi ? (_zb ? (rsi_val < inp_rsi_ob) : (rsi_val > inp_rsi_os)) : true
            bool idm_ok = true
            if use_idm
                // BB и RZ не требуют IDM (у RZ idm_swept=true по умолчанию)
                idm_ok := _is_bb_rz ? true : z.idm_swept

            bool itf_ok    = not use_itf_align or (_zb ? itf_bull : itf_bear)
            bool vwap_ok   = _is_bb_rz ? true : (_zb ? vwap_bull_ok : vwap_bear_ok)
            bool major_ok  = not use_major_bos or (_zb == major_bull_trend) or _is_bb_rz

            bool mss_ok = true
            if use_mss_confirm
                bool in_zone = close >= z.bot and close <= z.top
                if _zb
                    mss_ok := in_zone and (high > high[1]) and (close > open)
                else
                    mss_ok := in_zone and (low < low[1]) and (close < open)

            // V275: Trend-aware confluence — counter-trend entries need +1 extra factor
            bool _trend_supports_entry = _zb ? (itf_bull or global_bull) : (itf_bear or global_bear)
            int _trend_penalty  = _trend_supports_entry ? 0 : 1
            int confluence_count = (tr_ok ? 1 : 0) + (itf_ok ? 1 : 0) + (vwap_ok ? 1 : 0) +
                                   (rsi_ok ? 1 : 0) + (idm_ok ? 1 : 0) + (major_ok ? 1 : 0)
            bool conf_ok = confluence_count >= (min_confluence + _trend_penalty)

            string order_id    = (_zb ? "L_" : "S_") + f_ts(z.origin_idx)
            bool is_sfp_event  = false
            if use_sfp
                if _zb
                    if low < z.bot and close >= z.bot
                        is_sfp_event := true
                else
                    if high > z.top and close <= z.top
                        is_sfp_event := true

            // V277: Block entry if already in simulated position OR just exited this bar
            // Prevents exit→re-enter cycle within same bar that causes rapid label spam
            bool already_in_trade = sim_in_position or sim_exit_this_bar

            bool is_bb_creation_bar = (z.z_type == "BB" and z.created_at == bar_index)

            // V250: блокируем сигнал если req_fvg_seq включён и FVG зоны ещё не заполнены
            bool fvg_seq_ok = true
            if req_fvg_seq and not na(z.fvg_gfx)
                fvg_seq_ok := false

            if (tr_ok and pd_ok and rsi_ok and idm_ok and itf_ok and conf_ok and mss_ok and fvg_seq_ok) and not is_bb_creation_bar and not already_in_trade
                float en_calc = na 
                float sl_calc = na
                float z_edge  = _zb ? z.top : z.bot
                en_calc := na(z.sniper_price) ? z_edge : z.sniper_price

                if is_sfp_event
                    en_calc := close
                else if entry_mode == "Candle Close" or entry_mode == "ChoCh (Confirm)"
                    en_calc := close

                sl_calc := _zb ?
                     (z.bot - atr_val * sl_pad * final_pad_mult) :
                     (z.top + atr_val * sl_pad * final_pad_mult)

                float risk_dist    = math.abs(en_calc - sl_calc)
                bool path_is_clear = f_check_clearance(_zb, en_calc, risk_dist)

                if path_is_clear
                    float en_price = en_calc
                    if not is_sfp_event and entry_mode == "Touch (Limit)" and in_window and use_fib_entry and na(z.sniper_price)
                        float z_height     = math.abs(z.top - z.bot)
                        float entry_offset = z_height * p_fib_entry
                        float limit_front  = (atr_val * 0.2) * (d_discount * 4.0)
                        en_price := _zb ? (z.top - entry_offset + limit_front) : (z.bot + entry_offset - limit_front)

                    float sl_price = sl_calc
                    float dist     = math.abs(en_price - sl_price)
                    float qty      = f_qty(dist)

                    float tp1 = na 
                    float tp2 = na
                    float _d = _zb ? 1.0 : -1.0
                    if target_mode == "Fibonacci Extensions"
                        tp1 := en_price + _d * dist * fib_tp1
                        tp2 := en_price + _d * dist * fib_tp2
                    else
                        tp1 := en_price + _d * dist * part_ratio
                        tp2 := en_price + _d * dist * inp_tp_ratio

                    float t_points = use_trail ? (dist * tr_act / syminfo.mintick) : na
                    float t_offset = use_trail ? (dist * tr_off / syminfo.mintick) : na

                    bool do_trade = false 
                    string entry_comment = ""
					// V255: используем предвычисленные значения f_reverse_spike
					bool _pre_spike = _zb ? _pre_spike_bull : _pre_spike_bear
                    if is_sfp_event
                        do_trade := true 
                        entry_comment := "🔥 SFP Sweep"
                    else if entry_mode == "Touch (Limit)" and in_window
                        bool can_enter = true
                        if use_pin
                            bool touched = _zb ? (low <= z.top) : (high >= z.bot)
                            // V254: Требуем ≥ inp_min_pinbars пин-баров в окне lookback
                            int pin_count = f_count_pinbars(_zb, inp_pinbar_lookback)
                            bool multi_pin_ok = pin_count >= inp_min_pinbars
                            // V254: Проверяем аномальный обратный всплеск
                            bool spike_ok = _pre_spike
                            // V259: Альтернатива: 1+ пин-бар + импульс = подтверждённый вход
                            // Импульс (reverse spike) — основное подтверждение зоны
                            bool pattern_ok = multi_pin_ok or (pin_count >= 1 and spike_ok)
                            if not touched or not pattern_ok
                                can_enter := false
                        if can_enter
                            do_trade := true 
                            entry_comment := use_pin ? "Smart Limit" : "Limit Touch"
                    else if entry_mode == "Candle Close"
                        bool touched = _zb ? (low <= z.top) : (high >= z.bot)
                        if touched
                            bool valid_close = _zb ? (close >= z.bot) : (close <= z.top)
                            if valid_close and use_pin
                                // V254: Требуем ≥ inp_min_pinbars пин-баров + обратный всплеск
                                int pin_count_cc = f_count_pinbars(_zb, inp_pinbar_lookback)
                                bool multi_pin_ok_cc = pin_count_cc >= inp_min_pinbars
                                bool spike_ok_cc = _pre_spike
                                // V259: Альтернатива: 1+ пин-бар + импульс = подтверждённый вход
                                bool pattern_ok_cc = multi_pin_ok_cc or (pin_count_cc >= 1 and spike_ok_cc)
                                if not pattern_ok_cc
                                    valid_close := false
                            if valid_close
                                do_trade := true 
                                entry_comment := "Candle Close"
                    else if entry_mode == "ChoCh (Confirm)"
                        bool touched_now  = _zb ? (low <= z.top) : (high >= z.bot)
                        bool touched_prev = _zb ? (low[1] <= z.top) : (high[1] >= z.bot)
                        if touched_now or touched_prev
                            bool choch_signal = false
                            if _zb
                                // V251: CHoCH = пробой предыдущего свинг-хай (struct_h), а не просто high[1]
                                if not na(struct_h) and close > struct_h and close > open
                                    choch_signal := true
                            else
                                // V251: CHoCH = пробой предыдущего свинг-лоу (struct_l), а не просто low[1]
                                if not na(struct_l) and close < struct_l and close < open
                                    choch_signal := true
                            if choch_signal
                                do_trade := true 
                                entry_comment := "⚡ ChoCh Confirm"

                    if do_trade
                        // V275: Minimum R:R filter — block entries with poor risk:reward
                        float _actual_rr = dist > 0 ? math.abs(tp1 - en_price) / dist : 0.0
                        if _actual_rr < inp_min_rr
                            do_trade := false

                    if do_trade
                        string fvg_out   = (z.fvg_type != "None" and z.fvg_type != "") ? z.fvg_type : "No Gap"
                        string _tk_tf    = '","ticker":"' + syminfo.ticker + '","tf":"' + timeframe.period + '"}'
                        string msg_entry = '{"action":"' + (_zb ? "BUY" : "SELL") +
                             '","ticker":"' + syminfo.ticker + '","tf":"' + timeframe.period +
                             '","entry":' + f_mt(en_price) +
                             ',"sl":' + f_mt(sl_price) +
                             ',"tp1":' + f_mt(tp1) +
                             ',"tp2":' + f_mt(tp2) +
                             ',"tier":"' + z.tier + '","score":' + str.tostring(z.score, "#.1") +
                             ',"fvg":"' + fvg_out + '","trigger":"' + entry_comment +
                             '","prob":' + str.tostring(d_prob, "#.1") +
                             ',"asset":"' + asset_label + '"}'
                        string msg_exit1 = '{"action":"EXIT_TP1' + _tk_tf
                        string msg_exit2 = '{"action":"EXIT_TP2' + _tk_tf
                        string comm_suf  = " (Lvl " + f_ts(z.sniper_stage) + ")"
                        string idm_suf   = use_idm ? " +IDM" : ""

                        string _entry_comm = entry_comment + comm_suf + idm_suf
                        float  _entry_lim  = entry_mode=="Touch (Limit)" and not is_sfp_event ? en_price : na
                        // V275: Simulated position tracking (replaces strategy.entry/exit)

                        if entry_mode != "Touch (Limit)" or is_sfp_event
                            if _zb  
                                trigger_buy  := true
                            else          
                                trigger_sell := true
                        else
                            if _zb  and low  <= en_price 
                                trigger_buy  := true
                            if not _zb and high >= en_price 
                                trigger_sell := true

                        // V275: Update simulated position state on entry
                        if (trigger_buy or trigger_sell) and not sim_in_position
                            sim_in_position := true
                            sim_direction   := _zb ? 1 : -1
                            sim_entry_price := en_price
                            sim_sl_price    := sl_price
                            sim_tp1_price   := tp1
                            sim_tp2_price   := tp2
                            sim_entry_bar   := bar_index
                            // Update export vars
                            exp_entry_price := en_price
                            exp_sl_price    := sl_price
                            exp_tp1_price   := tp1
                            exp_tp2_price   := tp2
                            exp_sim_dir     := _zb ? 1.0 : -1.0

// ── Breakeven manager ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// V255: безусловный вызов ta.highest/ta.lowest для серийной согласованности
float _be_high_pre = ta.highest(high, 2)
float _be_low_pre  = ta.lowest(low, 2)

// indicator mode: breakeven manager disabled (no open trades to manage)

// V280: LONG/SHORT signal labels moved to VISUAL (hint system handles entry labels)

float dist_to_bull = na
float dist_to_bear = na
if not na(pd_high) 
    dist_to_bull := (pd_high - close) / syminfo.mintick
if not na(pd_low)  
    dist_to_bear := (close - pd_low)  / syminfo.mintick

// ── VWAP plot перемещён после ENG: export channels (см. конец блока 9) ──

// ==========================================
// БЛОК 9: ENGINE EXPORTS (для Visual-индикатора)
// ==========================================
// V278: Use pre-GC zone counts + count newly created zones after GC for accuracy
// _pre_gc_cnt_* captures zones before garbage collection (inside f_limit_visible_zones)
// zone_db here has post-GC surviving zones + new zones added by f_create_new_zones()
// We take max() to cover both: zones deleted by GC and zones added since GC ran
int _post_cnt_sup = 0
int _post_cnt_res = 0
int _post_cnt_bb  = 0
int _post_cnt_rz  = 0
for z in zone_db
    if z.active
        if z.z_type == "BB"
            _post_cnt_bb += 1
        else if z.z_type == "RZ"
            _post_cnt_rz += 1
        else if z.is_bull
            _post_cnt_sup += 1
        else
            _post_cnt_res += 1
int cnt_sup = math.max(array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_sup, 0), _post_cnt_sup)
int cnt_res = math.max(array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_res, 0), _post_cnt_res)
int cnt_bb  = math.max(array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_bb,  0),  _post_cnt_bb)
int cnt_rz  = math.max(array.get(_pre_gc_cnt_rz,  0),  _post_cnt_rz)

var float max_eq = SIM_INITIAL_CAPITAL
max_eq := math.max(max_eq, sim_equity)
float dd_pct = max_eq > 0 ? f_safe_div(max_eq - sim_equity, max_eq) * 100 : 0

// V269: Risk Management Metrics ──────────────────────────────────────────
int  RM_MAX_RETURNS       = 100  // Rolling window for trade returns (balance recency vs. sample size)
int  RM_MIN_FOR_RISK      = 5    // Min trades for Sharpe/Sortino (statistical significance)
int  RM_MIN_FOR_MC        = 10   // Min trades for Monte Carlo bootstrap resampling
int  RM_MC_MAX_STEPS      = 50   // Max path length per MC sim (perf vs. accuracy trade-off)
// V275: Use simulated trade data instead of hardcoded zeros
int _rm_trades = sim_trades
int _rm_wins   = sim_wins
