int _rm_losses = _rm_trades - _rm_wins
float _rm_wr   = _rm_trades > 0 ? f_safe_div(float(_rm_wins), float(_rm_trades)) : 0.0
float _rm_avg_win  = _rm_wins > 0 ? f_safe_div(sim_gross_profit, float(_rm_wins)) : 0.0
float _rm_avg_loss = _rm_losses > 0 ? f_safe_div(sim_gross_loss, float(_rm_losses)) : 0.0
float _kelly_f = _rm_avg_win > 0 ? f_safe_div(_rm_wr * _rm_avg_win - (1.0 - _rm_wr) * _rm_avg_loss, _rm_avg_win) : 0.0
_kelly_f := math.max(0.0, math.min(_kelly_f, 1.0))

// Sharpe Ratio (annualized, assuming 252 trading days)
// Uses per-trade returns approximation
var array<float> _trade_returns = array.new<float>()
if _rm_trades > 0 and _rm_trades != nz(_rm_trades[1], 0)
    // V275: Use simulated trade P&L
    float last_pnl = sim_exit_this_bar ? (sim_gross_profit - nz(sim_gross_profit[1], 0.0)) - (sim_gross_loss - nz(sim_gross_loss[1], 0.0)) : 0.0
    float last_eq  = math.max(sim_equity, 1.0)
    float ret = f_safe_div(last_pnl, last_eq)
    array.push(_trade_returns, ret)
    if array.size(_trade_returns) > RM_MAX_RETURNS
        array.shift(_trade_returns)

float _sharpe  = 0.0
float _sortino = 0.0
int _ret_n = array.size(_trade_returns)
if _ret_n >= RM_MIN_FOR_RISK
    float _ret_sum = 0.0
    for _ri = 0 to _ret_n - 1
        _ret_sum += array.get(_trade_returns, _ri)
    float _ret_mean = f_safe_div(_ret_sum, float(_ret_n))
    float _ret_sq_sum = 0.0
    float _ret_down_sq = 0.0
    for _ri = 0 to _ret_n - 1
        float _r = array.get(_trade_returns, _ri)
        _ret_sq_sum += math.pow(_r - _ret_mean, 2)
        if _r < 0
            _ret_down_sq += math.pow(_r, 2)
    float _ret_std = math.sqrt(f_safe_div(_ret_sq_sum, float(math.max(_ret_n - 1, 1))))
    float _down_std = math.sqrt(f_safe_div(_ret_down_sq, float(math.max(_ret_n - 1, 1))))
    _sharpe  := f_safe_div(_ret_mean, _ret_std) * math.sqrt(252.0)
    _sortino := f_safe_div(_ret_mean, _down_std) * math.sqrt(252.0)

// V270: Monte Carlo Simulation (500 iterations, block bootstrap)
// Uses deterministic index shuffling (no RNG in Pine) for reproducible results
float _mc_dd95 = 0.0
if _ret_n >= RM_MIN_FOR_MC
    var array<float> _mc_dds = array.new<float>()
    array.clear(_mc_dds)
    for _sim = 0 to 499
        float _mc_eq = 1.0
        float _mc_peak = 1.0
        float _mc_max_dd = 0.0
        int _block_size = 3 + (_sim % 3)  // V270: Block bootstrap (blocks of 3-5)
        for _step = 0 to math.min(_ret_n - 1, RM_MC_MAX_STEPS - 1)
            // V270: Block bootstrap with deterministic index for autocorrelation
            int _block_start = (_sim * 7 + (_step / _block_size) * 13) % _ret_n
            int _pick = (_block_start + (_step % _block_size)) % _ret_n
            float _r = array.get(_trade_returns, _pick)
            _mc_eq := _mc_eq * (1.0 + _r)
            _mc_peak := math.max(_mc_peak, _mc_eq)
            float _dd = f_safe_div(_mc_peak - _mc_eq, _mc_peak)
            _mc_max_dd := math.max(_mc_max_dd, _dd)
        array.push(_mc_dds, _mc_max_dd)
    // Sort and take 95th percentile
    array.sort(_mc_dds)
    int _p95_idx = math.min(474, array.size(_mc_dds) - 1)  // 95th pctile of 500 (0-indexed: 474)
    _mc_dd95 := array.get(_mc_dds, _p95_idx) * 100.0

// V270: CVD tracking
float _cvd_delta_val = f_cvd_delta()
cvd_cumulative += _cvd_delta_val
// V270: CVD divergence detection
var float cvd_prev_low   = 0.0
var float cvd_prev_high  = 0.0
var float price_prev_low  = na
var float price_prev_high = na
bool cvd_bull_div = false
bool cvd_bear_div = false
if not na(pl_int)
    if not na(price_prev_low) and low < price_prev_low and cvd_cumulative > cvd_prev_low
        cvd_bull_div := true  // Price lower low, CVD higher low = bullish divergence
    cvd_prev_low  := cvd_cumulative
    price_prev_low := low
if not na(ph_int)
    if not na(price_prev_high) and high > price_prev_high and cvd_cumulative < cvd_prev_high
        cvd_bear_div := true  // Price higher high, CVD lower high = bearish divergence
    cvd_prev_high  := cvd_cumulative
    price_prev_high := high
float cvd_div_signal = cvd_bull_div ? 1.0 : cvd_bear_div ? -1.0 : 0.0

// V270: Hurst Exponent computation
_hurst_val := f_hurst_exponent(100)

// V270: VSA signal
int _vsa_signal = f_vsa_signal()

// V273: Volume Profile POC computation
float _poc_price = f_calc_poc(100)

// V273: VCP and Keltner squeeze detection
bool _is_vcp = f_detect_vcp()
bool _is_squeeze = f_keltner_squeeze(20)

// V273: Absorption detection
bool _is_absorption = f_detect_absorption()

// V273: Neural network and adaptive weights update on new trade
// sweep/eff/pa use 0.5 (neutral) as these per-trade aggregate values aren't stored at exit time;
// z_score and rvol are normalized to [0,1]; trend is binary (1.0 = bull, 0.0 = bear)
if _rm_trades > 0 and _rm_trades != nz(_rm_trades[1], 0)
    bool _is_win_trade = false  // indicator mode: no real trades
    f_update_adaptive_weights(_is_win_trade, nz(z_score, 0.0), nz(rvol, 1.0), global_bull ? 1.0 : 0.0, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5)
    // lr=0.01: small learning rate prevents overreaction to single trades
    f_nn_update(nz(z_score, 0.0) / 5.0, math.min(nz(rvol, 1.0), 5.0) / 5.0, global_bull ? 1.0 : 0.0, 0.5, 0.5, 0.5, _is_win_trade ? 100.0 : 30.0, 0.01)

// V273: POC bonus for active zones near POC
if not na(_poc_price) and array.size(zone_db) > 0
    float _poc_tol = nz(atr_val, 1.0) * 0.3
    for z in zone_db
        if z.active
            float _zmid = (z.top + z.bot) / 2.0
            if math.abs(_zmid - _poc_price) < _poc_tol
                z.score := math.min(z.score + 15.0, 150.0)
                z.tier := f_tier(z.score)

// V270: Top zone tracking for VISUAL export
float _top1_zone_price = na
float _top1_zone_score = 0.0
float _top1_zone_dist  = na
if array.size(zone_db) > 0
    float _best_score = -1.0
    for z in zone_db
        if z.active and z.score > _best_score
            _best_score := z.score
            _top1_zone_score := z.score
            _top1_zone_price := (z.top + z.bot) / 2.0
            _top1_zone_dist := z.is_bull ? f_safe_div(close - z.top, atr_val) : f_safe_div(z.bot - close, atr_val)

// V282: Nearest zone boundary export for VISUAL rendering
// Exports top/bottom of the 2 nearest support zones and 2 nearest resistance zones.
// Includes ALL active zone types (OB, IMB, VCP, ACC, DST, MBR) — not just OB.
// BB zones are excluded (they have their own Breaker Block visual style).
// "Nearest" = smallest absolute distance from close to zone midpoint.
float _exp_sup1_top = 0.0
float _exp_sup1_bot = 0.0
float _exp_sup2_top = 0.0
float _exp_sup2_bot = 0.0
float _exp_res1_top = 0.0
float _exp_res1_bot = 0.0
float _exp_res2_top = 0.0
float _exp_res2_bot = 0.0
if array.size(zone_db) > 0
    float _NO_ZONE_DIST = 1e18  // sentinel value: no zone found
    float _best_sup1_dist = _NO_ZONE_DIST
    float _best_sup2_dist = _NO_ZONE_DIST
    float _best_res1_dist = _NO_ZONE_DIST
    float _best_res2_dist = _NO_ZONE_DIST
    for z in zone_db
        if not z.active
            continue
        // Skip BB zones (Breaker Blocks have their own visual style)
        if z.z_type == "BB"
            continue
        float _zmid = (z.top + z.bot) / 2.0
        float _zdist = math.abs(close - _zmid)
        if z.is_bull  // Support zone
            if _zdist < _best_sup1_dist
                _best_sup2_dist := _best_sup1_dist
                _exp_sup2_top   := _exp_sup1_top
                _exp_sup2_bot   := _exp_sup1_bot
                _best_sup1_dist := _zdist
                _exp_sup1_top   := z.top
                _exp_sup1_bot   := z.bot
            else if _zdist < _best_sup2_dist
                _best_sup2_dist := _zdist
                _exp_sup2_top   := z.top
                _exp_sup2_bot   := z.bot
        else  // Resistance zone
            if _zdist < _best_res1_dist
                _best_res2_dist := _best_res1_dist
                _exp_res2_top   := _exp_res1_top
                _exp_res2_bot   := _exp_res1_bot
                _best_res1_dist := _zdist
                _exp_res1_top   := z.top
                _exp_res1_bot   := z.bot
            else if _zdist < _best_res2_dist
                _best_res2_dist := _zdist
                _exp_res2_top   := z.top
                _exp_res2_bot   := z.bot

// Equity curve for VISUAL plot
float _equity_curve = sim_equity  // V275: use simulated equity

// V280: Invariant check label moved to VISUAL

// Кодирование направлений тренда как float:  1=bull, -1=bear, 0=flat
float _eng_htf  = global_bull ? 1 : global_bear ? -1 : 0
float _eng_itf  = itf_bull    ? 1 : itf_bear    ? -1 : 0
float _eng_bos  = major_bull_trend ? 1 : 0

// ── Plot-каналы для Visual-индикатора (input.source) ──────────────────────

plot(284.0,                              "ENG: Version",      color=color.new(#000000, 100))

// ── V279: Alert System ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Alerts for zone creation, entry signals, and new zone types

// Entry signal alerts
alertcondition(trigger_buy, title="🟢 LONG Signal", message="LONG signal triggered on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")
alertcondition(trigger_sell, title="🔴 SHORT Signal", message="SHORT signal triggered on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")
alertcondition(trigger_buy or trigger_sell, title="⚡ Any Trade Signal", message="Trade signal on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")

// High-quality zone alerts (score >= 100)
bool _alert_best_zone = false
if barstate.isconfirmed and array.size(zone_db) > 0
    for z in zone_db
        if z.active and z.score >= 100 and (bar_index - z.created_at) == 0
            _alert_best_zone := true
alertcondition(_alert_best_zone, title="⭐ BEST Zone Created", message="High-quality zone (Score≥100) created on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")

// New zone type alerts
bool _alert_imb_zone = false
bool _alert_vcp_zone = false
bool _alert_acc_zone = false
bool _alert_mbr_zone = false
if barstate.isconfirmed and array.size(zone_db) > 0
    for z in zone_db
        if z.active and (bar_index - z.created_at) == 0
            if z.z_type == "IMB"
                _alert_imb_zone := true
            if z.z_type == "VCP"
                _alert_vcp_zone := true
            if z.z_type == "ACC" or z.z_type == "DST"
                _alert_acc_zone := true
            if z.z_type == "MBR"
                _alert_mbr_zone := true
alertcondition(_alert_imb_zone, title="⚡ Imbalance Zone", message="Imbalance zone detected on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")
alertcondition(_alert_vcp_zone, title="🔻 VCP Zone", message="VCP compression zone on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")
alertcondition(_alert_acc_zone, title="📊 Accumulation/Distribution", message="Wyckoff A/D zone on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")
alertcondition(_alert_mbr_zone, title="🔀 Multi-Bar Rejection", message="Multi-bar rejection on {{ticker}} {{interval}}")

// V284: Все визуализации (дашборд, подсказки, сессии, PD, зоны, equity curve)

// ── Хелперы визуализации ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
f_hint_tier(float score) =>
    score >= 100 ? "BEST" : score >= 80 ? "STRONG" : score >= 40 ? "NORMAL" : "PIVOT"

// ── Derived display variables (direct from ENGINE — no input.source needed) ──
bool  v_global_bull  = global_bull
bool  v_global_bear  = global_bear
bool  v_itf_bull     = itf_bull
bool  v_itf_bear     = itf_bear
bool  v_major_bull   = major_bull_trend
float v_vwap_val     = vwap_val
float v_z_score      = nz(z_score, 0.0)
float v_rvol         = nz(rvol, 0.0)
float v_dist_bull    = nz(dist_to_bull, 0.0)
float v_dist_bear    = nz(dist_to_bear, 0.0)
float v_d_prob       = nz(d_prob, 0.0)
int   v_d_n          = nz(d_n, 0)
float v_d_discount   = nz(d_discount, 0.0)
int   v_total_tr     = _rm_trades
int   v_wins         = _rm_wins
float v_gross_profit = sim_gross_profit
float v_gross_loss   = sim_gross_loss
float v_equity       = sim_equity
float v_dd_pct       = dd_pct
int   v_cnt_sup      = cnt_sup
int   v_cnt_res      = cnt_res
int   v_cnt_bb       = cnt_bb
int   v_cnt_rz       = cnt_rz
float v_safe_pv      = safe_pv
float v_vol_ratio    = vol_ratio_c
float v_htf_vol      = htf_vol_ctx_c
float v_max_hist     = float(p_max_history)
float v_fvg_min      = p_fvg_min
float v_fvg_max      = p_fvg_max
float v_min_confl    = float(min_confluence)
float v_z_min        = p_z_min
float v_z_max        = p_z_max
float v_vol_max      = p_vol_max
float v_stoch_mu     = nz(d_mu, 0.0)
float v_stoch_sigma  = nz(d_sig, 0.0)
float v_stoch_eta    = nz(d_eta, 0.0)
float v_kelly_f      = nz(_kelly_f, 0.0)
float v_sharpe       = nz(_sharpe, 0.0)
float v_sortino      = nz(_sortino, 0.0)
float v_mc_dd95      = nz(_mc_dd95, 0.0)
float v_equity_curve = nz(_equity_curve, SIM_INITIAL_CAPITAL)
float v_top1_price   = _top1_zone_price
float v_top1_score   = nz(_top1_zone_score, 0.0)
float v_top1_dist    = _top1_zone_dist
float v_regime       = float(_regime_type)
float v_hurst        = nz(_hurst_val, 0.5)
float v_cvd_div      = nz(cvd_div_signal, 0.0)
float v_poc_price    = _poc_price
float v_bos_signal   = bos_bull ? 1.0 : bos_bear ? -1.0 : 0.0
float v_choch_signal = choch_bull ? 1.0 : choch_bear ? -1.0 : 0.0
float v_vcp          = _is_vcp ? 1.0 : 0.0
float v_squeeze      = _is_squeeze ? 1.0 : 0.0
float v_absorption   = _is_absorption ? 1.0 : 0.0
float v_sim_entry    = nz(exp_entry_price, 0.0)
float v_sim_sl       = nz(exp_sl_price, 0.0)
float v_sim_tp1      = nz(exp_tp1_price, 0.0)
float v_sim_tp2      = nz(exp_tp2_price, 0.0)
float v_sim_dir      = nz(exp_sim_dir, 0.0)
bool  v_sim_in_long  = v_sim_dir > 0.5
bool  v_sim_in_short = v_sim_dir < -0.5
bool  v_sim_in_trade = v_sim_in_long or v_sim_in_short
float v_sup1_top     = _exp_sup1_top
float v_sup1_bot     = _exp_sup1_bot
float v_sup2_top     = _exp_sup2_top
float v_sup2_bot     = _exp_sup2_bot
float v_res1_top     = _exp_res1_top
float v_res1_bot     = _exp_res1_bot
float v_res2_top     = _exp_res2_top
float v_res2_bot     = _exp_res2_bot

// Derived values
float v_win_rate = v_total_tr > 0 ? f_safe_div(v_wins * 100.0, v_total_tr) : 0.0
float v_pf       = v_gross_loss != 0 ? f_safe_div(v_gross_profit, math.max(math.abs(v_gross_loss), 0.001)) : na

// Auto-tuner display values (direct from ENGINE)
float v_piv_l_sup    = float(p_pivot_left)
float v_piv_r_sup    = float(p_pivot_right)
float v_piv_l_res    = float(p_pivot_left_res)
float v_piv_r_res    = float(p_pivot_right_res)
float v_ob_len_sup   = float(p_ob_len)
float v_ob_len_res   = float(p_ob_len_res)
float v_cluster_tol  = nz(atr_val, 1.0) * inp_cluster_tol
float v_inv_dist_sup = inp_inv_dist * nz(atr_val, 1.0)
float v_inv_dist_res = inp_inv_dist_r * nz(atr_val, 1.0)

// Определение типа актива
string v_asset_label = "UNKNOWN"
if str.contains(syminfo.type, "crypto")
    v_asset_label := "CRYPTO"
else if str.contains(syminfo.type, "futures") or str.contains(syminfo.type, "fund")
    v_asset_label := "FUTURES"
else if str.contains(syminfo.type, "forex")
    v_asset_label := "FOREX"
else if str.contains(syminfo.type, "stock")
    v_asset_label := "STOCK"
else if str.contains(syminfo.type, "index")
    v_asset_label := "INDEX"

// Определение сессии
f_vis_in_session(string sess_spec) =>
    string tz = sess_timezone == "" ? syminfo.timezone : sess_timezone
    not na(time(timeframe.period, sess_spec, tz))
bool _kz_asia    = f_vis_in_session(sess_asia_t)
bool _kz_london  = f_vis_in_session(sess_lond_t)
bool _kz_ny      = f_vis_in_session(sess_ny_t)
bool _kz_overlap = f_vis_in_session(sess_ovrl_t)
string _temp_s   = (_kz_asia ? "Asia " : "") + (_kz_london ? "London " : "") + (_kz_ny ? "NY " : "") + (_kz_overlap ? "Overlap" : "")
string v_session  = _temp_s == "" ? "Quiet" : str.trim(_temp_s)

// ── ТОРГОВЫЕ ПОДСКАЗКИ — ЛОГИКА (Entry/Exit State Machine) ───────────────
var int   hint_state       = 0
var float hint_entry_price = na
var float hint_sl_price    = na
var float hint_tp1_price   = na
var float hint_tp2_price   = na
var int   hint_entry_bar   = na

// Проверки зон
bool _hint_has_zone        = not na(v_top1_price) and v_top1_score >= hint_min_score
bool _hint_zone_near       = _hint_has_zone and not na(v_top1_dist) and v_top1_dist >= -0.5 and v_top1_dist <= hint_zone_dist
bool _hint_zone_is_support = _hint_has_zone and v_top1_price < close
bool _hint_zone_is_resist  = _hint_has_zone and v_top1_price > close

// Sync with sim state — detect entry/exit transitions
bool _eng_entered_long  = v_sim_in_long  and (hint_state != 1)
bool _eng_entered_short = v_sim_in_short and (hint_state != -1)
bool _eng_exited_long   = hint_state == 1  and not v_sim_in_long
bool _eng_exited_short  = hint_state == -1 and not v_sim_in_short

// Conditions: sim state + zone proximity
bool _entry_long_ok  = _eng_entered_long  and v_sim_entry > 0 and _hint_zone_near
bool _entry_short_ok = _eng_entered_short and v_sim_entry > 0 and _hint_zone_near
bool _exit_long_ok   = _eng_exited_long
bool _exit_short_ok  = _eng_exited_short

// Fallback zone-based hints (when sim not active)
if not v_sim_in_trade and hint_state == 0
    bool _hint_vwap_ok = not na(v_vwap_val)
    _entry_long_ok  := _hint_zone_near and _hint_zone_is_support and
         (v_global_bull or v_itf_bull) and _hint_vwap_ok and close >= v_vwap_val and v_regime != 3.0
    _entry_short_ok := _hint_zone_near and _hint_zone_is_resist and
         (v_global_bear or v_itf_bear) and _hint_vwap_ok and close <= v_vwap_val and v_regime != 3.0
if not v_sim_in_trade and hint_state != 0
    _exit_long_ok   := hint_state == 1 and (v_bos_signal < -0.5 or v_choch_signal < -0.5 or (v_global_bear and v_itf_bear) or v_regime == 3.0 or (_hint_zone_near and _hint_zone_is_resist))
    _exit_short_ok  := hint_state == -1 and (v_bos_signal > 0.5 or v_choch_signal > 0.5 or (v_global_bull and v_itf_bull) or v_regime == 3.0 or (_hint_zone_near and _hint_zone_is_support))

float _hint_saved_entry = hint_entry_price

bool hint_entry_long  = false
bool hint_entry_short = false
bool hint_exit_long   = false
bool hint_exit_short  = false

if barstate.isconfirmed
    if _entry_long_ok
        hint_entry_long  := true
        hint_state       := 1
        hint_entry_price := v_sim_entry > 0 ? v_sim_entry : close
        hint_sl_price    := v_sim_sl  > 0 ? v_sim_sl  : na
        hint_tp1_price   := v_sim_tp1 > 0 ? v_sim_tp1 : na
        hint_tp2_price   := v_sim_tp2 > 0 ? v_sim_tp2 : na
        hint_entry_bar   := bar_index
    else if _entry_short_ok
        hint_entry_short := true
        hint_state       := -1
        hint_entry_price := v_sim_entry > 0 ? v_sim_entry : close
        hint_sl_price    := v_sim_sl  > 0 ? v_sim_sl  : na
        hint_tp1_price   := v_sim_tp1 > 0 ? v_sim_tp1 : na
        hint_tp2_price   := v_sim_tp2 > 0 ? v_sim_tp2 : na
        hint_entry_bar   := bar_index
    else if _exit_long_ok
        hint_exit_long   := true
        hint_state       := 0
        hint_entry_price := na
        hint_sl_price    := na
        hint_tp1_price   := na
        hint_tp2_price   := na
        hint_entry_bar   := na
    else if _exit_short_ok
        hint_exit_short  := true
        hint_state       := 0
        hint_entry_price := na
        hint_sl_price    := na
        hint_tp1_price   := na
        hint_tp2_price   := na
        hint_entry_bar   := na

// ── DASHBOARD ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var table dash = table.new(position.top_right, 2, 48, bgcolor=color.new(color.black, 40), border_width=1)

f_dr(int row, string lbl, string value, color lc, color vc, string sz) =>
    table.cell(dash, 0, row, lbl, text_color=lc, text_size=sz)
    table.cell(dash, 1, row, value, text_color=vc, text_size=sz)

f_fmt_dist(float dist, color break_col) =>
    string txt = "N/A"
    color  col = color.gray
    if not na(dist)
        if dist <= 0
            txt := "⚡ BREAK!"
            col := break_col
        else
            txt := str.tostring(dist,"#") + " tks"
            col := color.white
    [txt, col]

if barstate.islast and show_dash
    string t_sz  = dash_size == "Tiny" ? size.tiny : (dash_size == "Small" ? size.small : size.normal)
    string h_txt = dash_collapse ? "TFA V1.0 (MINI)" : "Trading Fluppy ENGINE 🟢 (Integrated V284)"

    table.cell(dash, 0, 0, h_txt, text_color=color.white, bgcolor=color.new(color.teal, 55), text_size=t_sz)
    table.cell(dash, 1, 0, dash_collapse ? "➕" : "➖", text_color=color.white, bgcolor=color.new(color.purple, 55), text_size=t_sz)

    if not dash_collapse
        string trend_txt  = v_global_bull ? "BULLISH 🟢" : v_global_bear ? "BEARISH 🔴" : "FLAT ⚪"
        string itf_txt    = v_itf_bull ? "🟢 ITF Bull" : v_itf_bear ? "🔴 ITF Bear" : "⚪ ITF Flat"
        string vwap_txt   = close > v_vwap_val ? "Above 🟢" : "Below 🔴"
        string major_txt  = v_major_bull ? "BULL META 🟢" : "BEAR META 🔴"

        f_dr(1,  "Asset Type", v_asset_label + (v_safe_pv != 1.0 ? " PV=" + str.tostring(v_safe_pv,"#.##") : ""), color.gray, color.yellow, t_sz)
        f_dr(2,  "HTF Trend", trend_txt, color.gray, v_global_bull ? color.lime : color.red, t_sz)
        f_dr(3,  "ITF Trend", itf_txt, color.gray, v_itf_bull ? color.lime : color.orange, t_sz)
        f_dr(4,  "Major BOS", major_txt, color.gray, v_major_bull ? color.lime : color.red, t_sz)
        f_dr(5,  "VWAP", vwap_txt, color.gray, close > v_vwap_val ? color.lime : color.orange, t_sz)
        f_dr(6,  "Z-Score", str.tostring(v_z_score,"#.##") + " σ", color.gray, v_z_score > v_z_max ? #FFD700 : (v_z_score > v_z_min ? color.lime : color.white), t_sz)
        f_dr(7,  "RVOL", str.tostring(v_rvol,"#.##") + "×", color.gray, v_rvol > v_vol_max ? #FFD700 : (v_rvol > 1.0 ? color.lime : color.red), t_sz)
        f_dr(8,  "Hist Depth", str.tostring(v_max_hist, "#") + " (" + hist_mode + ")", color.gray, color.white, t_sz)

        string _zones_txt = "Sup:" + str.tostring(v_cnt_sup, "#") + " Res:" + str.tostring(v_cnt_res, "#") + " BB:" + str.tostring(v_cnt_bb, "#") + " RZ:" + str.tostring(v_cnt_rz, "#")
        f_dr(9,  "Active Zones", _zones_txt, color.gray, color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(10, "Total Trades", str.tostring(v_total_tr, "#"), color.gray, color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(11, "Win Rate", str.tostring(v_win_rate,"#.#") + "%", color.gray, v_win_rate > 50 ? color.lime : color.orange, t_sz)
        f_dr(12, "Profit Factor", na(v_pf) ? "N/A" : str.tostring(v_pf,"#.##"), color.gray, (not na(v_pf) and v_pf > 1.5) ? color.lime : color.white, t_sz)

        f_dr(13, "Cur DD", str.tostring(v_dd_pct,"#.#") + "%", color.white, v_dd_pct > 10 ? color.orange : color.lime, t_sz)
        f_dr(14, "Equity", str.tostring(v_equity, format.mintick), color.gray, color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(15, "Active Session", v_session, color.gray, color.white, t_sz)

        [txt_bull_dist, col_bull_dist] = f_fmt_dist(v_dist_bull, color.lime)
        f_dr(16, "To Bull Break", txt_bull_dist, color.gray, col_bull_dist, t_sz)

        [txt_bear_dist, col_bear_dist] = f_fmt_dist(v_dist_bear, color.red)
        f_dr(17, "To Bear Break", txt_bear_dist, color.gray, col_bear_dist, t_sz)

        string ui_prob = v_d_n >= stoch_min_val ? str.tostring(v_d_prob,"#.#") + "%" : "Wait (" + str.tostring(v_d_n, "#") + "/" + str.tostring(stoch_min_val, "#") + ")"
        string ui_disc = v_d_discount > 0 ? " (-" + str.tostring(v_d_discount*100,"#") + "%)" : ""
        color col_prob = v_d_prob >= 90.0 ? color.fuchsia : (v_d_prob > 60.0 ? color.orange : color.lime)
        f_dr(18, "Min Confluence", str.tostring(v_min_confl, "#") + " factors" + (use_mss_confirm ? " +MSS" : ""), color.aqua, color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(19, "FVG Range (ATR)", str.tostring(v_fvg_min,"#.####") + " – " + str.tostring(v_fvg_max,"#.#"), color.gray, color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(20, "Stochastic P", ui_prob + ui_disc, color.aqua, col_prob, t_sz)
        f_dr(21, "Sup Pivot (L/R)", (tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? "🔄 " : "") + str.tostring(v_piv_l_sup, "#") + " / " + str.tostring(v_piv_r_sup, "#"), color.gray, tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? color.aqua : color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(22, "Res Pivot (L/R)", (tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? "🔄 " : "") + str.tostring(v_piv_l_res, "#") + " / " + str.tostring(v_piv_r_res, "#"), color.gray, tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? color.aqua : color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(23, "Zone Age Max", use_zone_age_fade ? str.tostring(zone_max_age, "#") + " bars" : "OFF", color.gray, use_zone_age_fade ? color.white : color.gray, t_sz)
        f_dr(24, "Asset Adapt", use_asset_adapt ? "ON (" + v_asset_label + ")" : "OFF", color.gray, use_asset_adapt ? color.lime : color.gray, t_sz)
        string vr_txt = str.tostring(v_vol_ratio, "#.##") + "× | HTF:" + str.tostring(v_htf_vol, "#.##") + "×"
        color  vr_col = v_vol_ratio > 1.5 ? color.orange : v_vol_ratio < 0.7 ? color.aqua : color.lime
        f_dr(25, "Vol Ratio", vr_txt, color.gray, vr_col, t_sz)
        string cl_txt = "S:" + str.tostring(v_ob_len_sup, "#") + " R:" + str.tostring(v_ob_len_res, "#") + " Tol:" + str.tostring(v_cluster_tol, "#.##")
        f_dr(26, "SMC Cluster", cl_txt, color.gray, tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? color.aqua : color.white, t_sz)
        f_dr(27, "Inv Dist (ATR)", str.tostring(v_inv_dist_sup, "#") + " / " + str.tostring(v_inv_dist_res, "#"), color.gray, tuning_mode == "Auto-Adaptive" ? color.aqua : color.white, t_sz)

        // V284: Restored dashboard rows (now directly available, no plot channel needed)
        f_dr(28, "Kelly F", str.tostring(v_kelly_f, "#.###"), color.gray, v_kelly_f > 0.2 ? color.lime : (v_kelly_f > 0 ? color.white : color.red), t_sz)
        string sharpe_txt = str.tostring(v_sharpe, "#.##") + " | Sort: " + str.tostring(v_sortino, "#.##")
        color sharpe_col = v_sharpe > 1.0 ? color.lime : (v_sharpe > 0 ? color.white : color.red)
        f_dr(29, "Sharpe/Sortino", sharpe_txt, color.gray, sharpe_col, t_sz)
        f_dr(30, "MC DD95%", str.tostring(v_mc_dd95, "#.#") + "%", color.gray, v_mc_dd95 > 30 ? color.red : (v_mc_dd95 > 15 ? color.orange : color.lime), t_sz)

        // Stochastic model details
        string stoch_detail = "μ=" + str.tostring(v_stoch_mu, "#.#") + " σ=" + str.tostring(v_stoch_sigma, "#.#") + " η=" + str.tostring(v_stoch_eta, "#.#")
        f_dr(31, "Stoch μ/σ/η", v_d_n >= stoch_min_val ? stoch_detail : "Wait", color.aqua, color.white, t_sz)

        // Regime detection
        string regime_names = v_regime == 0.0 ? "Trending ↑ 🟢" : v_regime == 1.0 ? "Trending ↓ 🔴" : v_regime == 2.0 ? "Ranging ⚪" : "Volatile ⚡"
        string regime_advice = v_regime == 0.0 ? "Buy zones" : v_regime == 1.0 ? "Sell zones" : v_regime == 2.0 ? "Fade extremes" : "Wait / Reduce size"
        f_dr(32, "Market Regime", regime_names + " → " + regime_advice, color.aqua, v_regime == 0 ? color.lime : v_regime == 1 ? color.red : v_regime == 3 ? color.orange : color.white, t_sz)

        // Hurst Exponent
        string hurst_txt = str.tostring(v_hurst, "#.##")
        string hurst_label = v_hurst > 0.6 ? "Trending" : v_hurst < 0.4 ? "Mean-Revert" : "Random Walk"
        f_dr(33, "Hurst Exp", hurst_txt + " (" + hurst_label + ")", color.gray, v_hurst > 0.6 ? color.lime : v_hurst < 0.4 ? color.orange : color.white, t_sz)

        // CVD Divergence
        string cvd_txt = v_cvd_div > 0 ? "🟢 Bullish Div" : v_cvd_div < 0 ? "🔴 Bearish Div" : "⚪ None"
        f_dr(34, "CVD Divergence", cvd_txt, color.gray, v_cvd_div > 0 ? color.lime : v_cvd_div < 0 ? color.red : color.white, t_sz)

        // Top Zone Info
        string top_z_txt = "N/A"
        color top_z_col = color.gray
        if not na(v_top1_price) and v_top1_score > 0
            string tier_txt = v_top1_score >= 100 ? "BEST" : v_top1_score >= 80 ? "STRONG" : v_top1_score >= 40 ? "NORMAL" : "PIVOT"
            string dist_txt = not na(v_top1_dist) ? str.tostring(v_top1_dist, "#.#") + " ATR" : "N/A"
            top_z_txt := tier_txt + " @ " + str.tostring(v_top1_price, format.mintick) + " (" + str.tostring(v_top1_score, "#") + "pts) " + dist_txt
            top_z_col := v_top1_score >= 100 ? color.lime : v_top1_score >= 80 ? #00E5FF : color.white
        f_dr(35, "Top Zone", top_z_txt, color.aqua, top_z_col, t_sz)

        // Point of Control
        string poc_txt = not na(v_poc_price) and v_poc_price > 0 ? str.tostring(v_poc_price, format.mintick) : "N/A"
        color  poc_col = not na(v_poc_price) and v_poc_price > 0 ? (math.abs(close - v_poc_price) < nz(atr_val, 1.0) ? color.lime : color.white) : color.gray
        f_dr(36, "Point of Control", poc_txt, color.gray, poc_col, t_sz)

        // Market Microstructure
        string vcp_txt     = v_vcp > 0.5 ? "🟢" : "⚪"
        string sqz_txt     = v_squeeze > 0.5 ? "🟡" : "⚪"
        string abs_txt     = v_absorption > 0.5 ? "🔵" : "⚪"
        string micro_txt   = "VCP:" + vcp_txt + " Sqz:" + sqz_txt + " Abs:" + abs_txt
        color  micro_col   = (v_vcp > 0.5 or v_squeeze > 0.5 or v_absorption > 0.5) ? color.lime : color.white
        f_dr(37, "Microstructure", micro_txt, color.gray, micro_col, t_sz)

        // Structure Breaks
        string bos_txt   = v_bos_signal > 0.5 ? "🟢 Bull" : v_bos_signal < -0.5 ? "🔴 Bear" : "⚪ None"
        string choch_txt = v_choch_signal > 0.5 ? "🟢 Bull" : v_choch_signal < -0.5 ? "🔴 Bear" : "⚪ None"
        string struct_txt = "BOS:" + bos_txt + " CHoCH:" + choch_txt
        color  struct_col = (v_bos_signal != 0 or v_choch_signal != 0) ? (v_bos_signal > 0 or v_choch_signal > 0 ? color.lime : color.red) : color.white
        f_dr(38, "Structure Breaks", struct_txt, color.gray, struct_col, t_sz)

        // Trade Hint status
        string hint_status_txt = "⏳ Ожидание входа"
        if hint_state == 1
            float _h_risk = not na(hint_sl_price) ? (nz(hint_entry_price, close) - hint_sl_price) : na
            float _h_rr = not na(_h_risk) and _h_risk > 0 and not na(hint_tp1_price) ? f_safe_div(hint_tp1_price - nz(hint_entry_price, close), _h_risk) : na
            string _h_rr_txt = not na(_h_rr) ? " R:R " + str.tostring(_h_rr, "#.#") : ""
            hint_status_txt := "🟢 LONG @ " + str.tostring(nz(hint_entry_price, close), format.mintick) + _h_rr_txt
        else if hint_state == -1
            float _h_risk_s = not na(hint_sl_price) ? (hint_sl_price - nz(hint_entry_price, close)) : na
            float _h_rr_s = not na(_h_risk_s) and _h_risk_s > 0 and not na(hint_tp1_price) ? f_safe_div(nz(hint_entry_price, close) - hint_tp1_price, _h_risk_s) : na
            string _h_rr_txt_s = not na(_h_rr_s) ? " R:R " + str.tostring(_h_rr_s, "#.#") : ""
            hint_status_txt := "🔴 SHORT @ " + str.tostring(nz(hint_entry_price, close), format.mintick) + _h_rr_txt_s
        color  hint_status_col = hint_state == 1 ? color.lime : hint_state == -1 ? color.red : color.gray
        f_dr(39, "Trade Hint", show_hints ? hint_status_txt : "OFF", color.aqua, show_hints ? hint_status_col : color.gray, t_sz)
else
    table.clear(dash, 0, 0, 1, 47)

// ── Equity curve + drawdown plots ─────────────────────────────────────────
plot(v_equity_curve, "Equity Curve", color=color.new(color.lime, 30), linewidth=2, display=display.pane)
float v_peak_eq = ta.highest(v_equity_curve, 500)
float v_drawdown = v_peak_eq > 0 ? f_safe_div(v_peak_eq - v_equity_curve, v_peak_eq) * 100.0 : 0.0
plot(-v_drawdown, "Drawdown %", color=color.new(color.red, 50), linewidth=1, display=display.pane)

// ── ВИЗУАЛИЗАЦИЯ ТОРГОВЫХ ПОДСКАЗОК ───────────────────────────────────────
if show_hints
    if hint_entry_long
        float _el_risk = not na(hint_sl_price) and hint_entry_price > hint_sl_price ? (hint_entry_price - hint_sl_price) : na
        float _el_rr1  = not na(_el_risk) and _el_risk > 0 and not na(hint_tp1_price) ? f_safe_div(hint_tp1_price - hint_entry_price, _el_risk) : na
        string _el_rr_txt = not na(_el_rr1) ? "\nR:R " + str.tostring(_el_rr1, "#.#") + ":1" : ""
        string _el_sl_txt = not na(hint_sl_price) ? "\nSL: " + str.tostring(hint_sl_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _el_tp_txt = not na(hint_tp1_price) ? "\nTP1: " + str.tostring(hint_tp1_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _el_tp2_txt = not na(hint_tp2_price) ? " | TP2: " + str.tostring(hint_tp2_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _el_txt = "🟢 ВХОД LONG\n" + str.tostring(nz(hint_entry_price, close), format.mintick) + "\n" + f_hint_tier(v_top1_score) + " (" + str.tostring(v_top1_score, "#") + " pts)" + _el_rr_txt + _el_sl_txt + _el_tp_txt + _el_tp2_txt
        label.new(bar_index, low, _el_txt,
             style=label.style_label_up, color=color.new(#00C853, 10),
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.normal, yloc=yloc.belowbar)
    if hint_entry_short
        float _es_risk = not na(hint_sl_price) and hint_sl_price > hint_entry_price ? (hint_sl_price - hint_entry_price) : na
        float _es_rr1  = not na(_es_risk) and _es_risk > 0 and not na(hint_tp1_price) ? f_safe_div(hint_entry_price - hint_tp1_price, _es_risk) : na
        string _es_rr_txt = not na(_es_rr1) ? "\nR:R " + str.tostring(_es_rr1, "#.#") + ":1" : ""
        string _es_sl_txt = not na(hint_sl_price) ? "\nSL: " + str.tostring(hint_sl_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _es_tp_txt = not na(hint_tp1_price) ? "\nTP1: " + str.tostring(hint_tp1_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _es_tp2_txt = not na(hint_tp2_price) ? " | TP2: " + str.tostring(hint_tp2_price, format.mintick) : ""
        string _es_txt = "🔴 ВХОД SHORT\n" + str.tostring(nz(hint_entry_price, close), format.mintick) + "\n" + f_hint_tier(v_top1_score) + " (" + str.tostring(v_top1_score, "#") + " pts)" + _es_rr_txt + _es_sl_txt + _es_tp_txt + _es_tp2_txt
        label.new(bar_index, high, _es_txt,
             style=label.style_label_down, color=color.new(#FF1744, 10),
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.normal, yloc=yloc.abovebar)
    if hint_exit_long
        float _pnl_l = close - nz(_hint_saved_entry, close)
        string _pnl_l_txt = (_pnl_l >= 0 ? "+" : "") + str.tostring(_pnl_l, format.mintick)
        string _reason_l = "Структурный"
        if not na(nz(hint_sl_price[1])) and low <= nz(hint_sl_price[1])
            _reason_l := "❌ SL Hit"
        else if not na(nz(hint_tp2_price[1])) and high >= nz(hint_tp2_price[1])
            _reason_l := "🎯 TP2 Hit"
        else if not na(nz(hint_tp1_price[1])) and high >= nz(hint_tp1_price[1])
            _reason_l := "🎯 TP1 Hit"
        else if v_bos_signal < -0.5
            _reason_l := "BOS ↓"
        else if v_choch_signal < -0.5
            _reason_l := "CHoCH ↓"
        else if v_global_bear and v_itf_bear
            _reason_l := "Тренд ↓"
        else if v_regime == 3.0
            _reason_l := "Волатильность"
        color _xl_col = _pnl_l >= 0 ? color.new(#00C853, 20) : color.new(#FF1744, 20)
        string _xl_txt = "⬜ ВЫХОД LONG\n" + str.tostring(close, format.mintick) + "\nP&L: " + _pnl_l_txt + "\n" + _reason_l
        label.new(bar_index, high, _xl_txt,
             style=label.style_label_down, color=_xl_col,
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.normal, yloc=yloc.abovebar)
    if hint_exit_short
        float _pnl_s = nz(_hint_saved_entry, close) - close
        string _pnl_s_txt = (_pnl_s >= 0 ? "+" : "") + str.tostring(_pnl_s, format.mintick)
        string _reason_s = "Структурный"
        if not na(nz(hint_sl_price[1])) and high >= nz(hint_sl_price[1])
            _reason_s := "❌ SL Hit"
        else if not na(nz(hint_tp2_price[1])) and low <= nz(hint_tp2_price[1])
            _reason_s := "🎯 TP2 Hit"
        else if not na(nz(hint_tp1_price[1])) and low <= nz(hint_tp1_price[1])
            _reason_s := "🎯 TP1 Hit"
        else if v_bos_signal > 0.5
            _reason_s := "BOS ↑"
        else if v_choch_signal > 0.5
            _reason_s := "CHoCH ↑"
        else if v_global_bull and v_itf_bull
            _reason_s := "Тренд ↑"
        else if v_regime == 3.0
            _reason_s := "Волатильность"
        color _xs_col = _pnl_s >= 0 ? color.new(#00C853, 20) : color.new(#FF1744, 20)
        string _xs_txt = "⬜ ВЫХОД SHORT\n" + str.tostring(close, format.mintick) + "\nP&L: " + _pnl_s_txt + "\n" + _reason_s
        label.new(bar_index, low, _xs_txt,
             style=label.style_label_up, color=_xs_col,
             textcolor=color.white, size=size.normal, yloc=yloc.belowbar)

// ── Session Boxes ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
f_vis_draw_session(string sess_spec, color c_sess) =>
    bool in_sess       = f_vis_in_session(sess_spec)
    bool prev_in_sess  = bar_index > 0 ? in_sess[1] : false
    bool session_start = in_sess and not prev_in_sess
    bool session_end   = not in_sess and prev_in_sess
    var box   s_box    = na
    var float s_high   = na
    var float s_low    = na
    if session_start
        s_high := high
        s_low  := low
        s_box  := box.new(bar_index, high, bar_index + 1, low, border_color=na, bgcolor=c_sess, xloc=xloc.bar_index)
    if in_sess
        s_high := math.max(s_high, high)
        s_low  := math.min(s_low,  low)
        if not na(s_box)
            box.set_top(s_box, s_high)
            box.set_bottom(s_box, s_low)
            box.set_right(s_box, bar_index + 1)
    if session_end and not na(s_box)
        box.set_right(s_box, bar_index)
    in_sess

if show_sess_v
    f_vis_draw_session(sess_asia_t, c_asia)
    f_vis_draw_session(sess_lond_t, c_lond)
    f_vis_draw_session(sess_ny_t,   c_ny)
    f_vis_draw_session(sess_ovrl_t, c_ovrl)

var label _sess_lbl_v = na
if barstate.islast and show_sess_v
    if not na(_sess_lbl_v)
        label.delete(_sess_lbl_v)
    string _st = (_kz_asia ? "Asia " : "") + (_kz_london ? "London " : "") + (_kz_ny ? "NY " : "") + (_kz_overlap ? "Overlap" : "")
    string _cs = _st == "" ? "Quiet" : str.trim(_st)
    color _sc = _kz_overlap ? color.red : _kz_ny ? color.purple : _kz_london ? color.orange : _kz_asia ? color.blue : color.gray
    _sess_lbl_v := label.new(bar_index + 5, high, text="Session: " + _cs,
         color=color.new(_sc, 70), textcolor=color.white, style=label.style_label_left, size=size.small)

// ── PD Band Visualization ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
var line _vis_pd_ln_h = na
var line _vis_pd_ln_l = na
var line _vis_pd_ln_m = na
var box  _vis_pd_bx_u = na
var box  _vis_pd_bx_l = na
if show_pd_v
    float _pd_h = na
    float _pd_l = na
    float _pd_m = na
    if not na(v_dist_bull) and not na(v_dist_bear) and v_dist_bull != 0 and v_dist_bear != 0
        _pd_h := close + v_dist_bull * syminfo.mintick
        _pd_l := close - v_dist_bear * syminfo.mintick
        _pd_m := (_pd_h + _pd_l) / 2.0
    if not na(_pd_h) and not na(_pd_l)
        bool _chg = na(_vis_pd_ln_h) or _pd_h != nz(_pd_h[1]) or _pd_l != nz(_pd_l[1])
        if _chg
            _vis_pd_ln_h := line.new(bar_index, _pd_h, bar_index, _pd_h, color=color.new(color.red,   70))
            _vis_pd_ln_l := line.new(bar_index, _pd_l, bar_index, _pd_l, color=color.new(color.green, 70))
            _vis_pd_ln_m := line.new(bar_index, _pd_m, bar_index, _pd_m, color=color.new(color.gray,  50), style=line.style_dotted)
            _vis_pd_bx_u := box.new(bar_index, _pd_h, bar_index, _pd_m, border_color=na, bgcolor=color.new(color.red,   90))
            _vis_pd_bx_l := box.new(bar_index, _pd_m, bar_index, _pd_l, border_color=na, bgcolor=color.new(color.green, 90))
        line.set_x2(_vis_pd_ln_h, bar_index)
        line.set_x2(_vis_pd_ln_l, bar_index)
        line.set_x2(_vis_pd_ln_m, bar_index)
        box.set_right(_vis_pd_bx_u, bar_index)
        box.set_right(_vis_pd_bx_l, bar_index)

// ── Support / Resistance Zone Visualization ───────────────────────────────
var box _vis_z_sup1 = na
var box _vis_z_sup2 = na
var box _vis_z_res1 = na
var box _vis_z_res2 = na
if show_zones_v
    if not na(_vis_z_sup1)
        box.delete(_vis_z_sup1)
    if not na(_vis_z_sup2)
        box.delete(_vis_z_sup2)
    if not na(_vis_z_res1)
        box.delete(_vis_z_res1)
    if not na(_vis_z_res2)
        box.delete(_vis_z_res2)
    _vis_z_sup1 := na
    _vis_z_sup2 := na
    _vis_z_res1 := na
    _vis_z_res2 := na
    int _zbox_left = bar_index - 50
    if v_sup1_top > 0 and v_sup1_bot > 0 and v_sup1_top > v_sup1_bot
        _vis_z_sup1 := box.new(_zbox_left, v_sup1_top, bar_index + 5, v_sup1_bot,
             border_color=color.new(zone_sup_col, 20),
             bgcolor=zone_sup_col, border_width=2, xloc=xloc.bar_index)
    if v_sup2_top > 0 and v_sup2_bot > 0 and v_sup2_top > v_sup2_bot
        _vis_z_sup2 := box.new(_zbox_left, v_sup2_top, bar_index + 5, v_sup2_bot,
             border_color=color.new(zone_sup_col, 30),
             bgcolor=color.new(zone_sup_col, 80),
             border_width=1, xloc=xloc.bar_index)
    if v_res1_top > 0 and v_res1_bot > 0 and v_res1_top > v_res1_bot
        _vis_z_res1 := box.new(_zbox_left, v_res1_top, bar_index + 5, v_res1_bot,
             border_color=color.new(zone_res_col, 20),
             bgcolor=zone_res_col, border_width=2, xloc=xloc.bar_index)
    if v_res2_top > 0 and v_res2_bot > 0 and v_res2_top > v_res2_bot
        _vis_z_res2 := box.new(_zbox_left, v_res2_top, bar_index + 5, v_res2_bot,
             border_color=color.new(zone_res_col, 30),
             bgcolor=color.new(zone_res_col, 80),
             border_width=1, xloc=xloc.bar_index)

alertcondition(hint_exit_long, title="💡 Hint: ВЫХОД LONG", message="💡 Подсказка: ВЫХОД LONG — структурный сигнал на закрытие позиции")
alertcondition(hint_exit_short, title="💡 Hint: ВЫХОД SHORT", message="💡 Подсказка: ВЫХОД SHORT — структурный сигнал на закрытие позиции")
alertcondition(not na(v_top1_dist) and v_top1_dist >= 0 and v_top1_dist < 1.0 and v_top1_score >= 100, title="🔔 Price near BEST zone", message="🔔 Цена подходит к BEST зоне (< 1 ATR)")
alertcondition(v_cvd_div != 0, title="⚡ CVD Divergence detected", message="⚡ CVD дивергенция обнаружена — потенциальный разворот")

alertcondition(v_bos_signal < 0, title="📊 BOS Bearish", message="📊 Break of Structure: Bearish")
alertcondition(v_choch_signal > 0, title="🔄 CHoCH Bullish", message="🔄 Change of Character: Bullish")
alertcondition(v_choch_signal < 0, title="🔄 CHoCH Bearish", message="🔄 Change of Character: Bearish")
alertcondition(v_squeeze > 0.5, title="🔸 Keltner Squeeze", message="🔸 Keltner Squeeze активен — сжатие волатильности, ожидается импульс")
alertcondition(v_mc_dd95 > 30, title="⚠️ Monte Carlo DD >30%", message="⚠️ Monte Carlo 95th percentile drawdown превысил 30%")
